C O N F I D E N T I A L SECTION 3 OF 3 VALLETTA 0794
4.  THE ELECTION:  PARTIES, PERSONALITIES AND PROCEDURES.
THE PRESENT MALTESE PARLIAMENT WILL COMPLETE ITS FIVE-YEAR
TERM ON AUGUST 15 UNLESS PRIME MINISTER MINTOFF DECIDES ON
AN EARLIER DISSOLUTION. UNDER THE CONSTITUTION, THE GENERAL
ELECTION MUST FOLLOW NOT LATER THAN THREE MONTHS AFTER
DISSOLUTION. THE ELECTION COULD, THEREFORE, OCCUR AT ANY
TIME THIS SUMER OR FALL, UP UNTIL THE WEEKEND OF NOVEMBER
12-13.
BOTH POLITICAL PARTIES HAVE LONG SINCE BEEN CAMPAIGNING
IN EARNEST. THE ONLY REMAINING STEPS TO BE TAKEN BY THE
PARTIES ARE THE OFFICIAL RELEASE OF THEIR LISTS OF
CANDIDATES, AND THE PUBLICATION OF THEIR ELECTORAL PROGRAMS.
THESE PARTY MANIFESTOES TEND TO BE WIDE-RANGING AND COVER
A LARGE NUMBER OF ISSUES, MANY OF WHICH ARE ONLESOF LIMITED
SIGNIFICANCE TO THE ELECTION. THE FOREIGN AND DOMESTIC
POLICY PROBLEMS CITED ABOVE WILL CERTAINLY RECEIVE MAJOR
ATTENTION BY BOTH PARTIES IN THEIR MANIFESTOES.
DESPITE THE VERY REAL ISSUES WITH WHICH THE MALTESE
ELECTORATE MUST GRAPPLE, THE OUTCOME WILL REST TO A
SIGNIFICENT EXTENT ON THE PERSONALITIES OF THE TWO PARTY
LEADERS AND THEIR SUPPORTING CANDIATES.
THE LABOR PARTY IS IDENTIFIED ALMOST TOTALLY WITH
THE ECCENTRIC AND FLAMBOYANT DOM MINTOFF, AND THE
EXTENSIVE PERSONALITY CULT WHICH HAS GROWN UP AROUND
HIM AS PARTY AND PARLIAMENTARY LEADER OVER THE YEARS.
THE NATIONALIST PARTY, ON THE OTHER HAND, IS MORE
NEARLY A COLLECTION OF INDIVIDUALISTS WITHOUT A STRONG
SENSE OF PURPOSE, OTHER THAN SOMEWHAT VAGUE COMMITMENTS
TO FREE ENTERPRISE AND THE RESTORATION OF MALTA'S
TRADITIONAL WESTERN TIES. THE WEAK, INEFFECTUAL OPPOSITION
LEADER, GIORGIO BORG OLIVIER, IS NO MATCH FOR MNTOFF IN
THE PERSONALITY SWEEPSTAKES.
HOWEVER, MALTA'S ELECTORAL SYSTEM IS A VERY COMPLICATED
ONE, WITH A TRANSFERABLE VOTE PROCEDURE THAT PLACES MORE
EMPHASIS ON THE RELATIVE APPEAL OF SECONDARY CANDIDATES
THAN THAT OF THE PARTY LEADERS. THERE ARE THIRTEEN
ELECTORAL DISTRICTS AND SISTY-FIVE PARLIAMENTARY SEATS
AT STAKE. WITH AN ALMOST ENDLESS LIST OF CANDIDATES AND
ONLY 218,000 ELIGIBLE VOTERS, LITERALLY EVERY VOTE WILL
COUNT (AND MORE THAN ONCE UNDER THE MALTESE PREFERENCE
SYSTEM).
IN THE 1971 ELECTION, CANDIDATES WERE ELECTED WITH
AS FEW AS 500 DIRECT VOTES ON THE FIRST "COUNT", AND THE
FINAL OVER-ALL RESULT WAS EXTREMELY CLOSE, WITH THE LABOR
PARTY WINNING ONLY A ONE-SEAT PARLIAMENTARY MAJORITY AND
4,600 VOTES MORE THAN THE NATIONALISTS.
THIS YEAR, THE VOTING IS AGAIN EXPECTED TO BE CLOSE.
THE GENERAL CONSENSUS HAS BEEN THAT MINTOFF AND THE
LABORITIES HAVE ENJOYED A LIMITED, BUT DECIDED ADVANTAGE
OVER THE NATIONALISTS. HOWEVER, THERE IS NOW SOME FEELING
THAT THERE MAY BE A SWING AMONG THE "UNDECIDED" AND
"FLOATING" VOTERS BACK TOWARD THE NATIONALISTS. IN 1971,
THE "TIME FOR A CHANGE" ATTITUDE AMONG THIS GROUP OF
VOTERS WORKED IN MINTOFF'S FAVOR. IN 1976, THERE COULD
BE A REVERSAL OF THIS EFFECT.
IN ANY EVENT, THERE ARE MANY UNKNOWNS. THERE ARE NO
BY-ELECTIONS OR PUBLIC OPINION POLLS IN MALTA, AND 40,000
VOTERS HAVE NEVER PARTICIPATED IN AN ELECTION BEFORE
(THE MINIMUM VOTING AGE RECENTLY WAS LOWERED FROM 21 TO
18). SO DESPITE THE FACT THAT PARTY LEADERS ON BOTH SIDES
CLAIM THEY ARE CONFIDENT OF VICTORY, NO ONE CAN REALLY BE
CERTAIN OF THE OUTCOME. BUT AFTER FIVE YEARS WITHOUT AN
OPPORTUNITY TO EXPRESS THEIR APPROVAL OR DISAPPROVAL OF
MINTOFF'S VARIOUS ACTS OF SHOWMANSHIP, THE MALTESE POEPLE
ARE AT LEAST READY TO HAVE THEIR SAY.
5.  BILATERAL RELATIONS. PRIME MINISTER MINTOFF IS STILL
PRESSING HARD THROUGH EVERY POSSIBLE CHANNEL FOR A MEETING
WITH SECRETARY KISSINGER PRIOR TO THE MALTESE ELECTIONS.
EVEN THOUGH HE IS PROBABLY AWARE OF THE UNLIKELIHOOD OF
SUCH A MEETING BEFORE THE ELECTION, MINTOFF REFUSES TO
TAKE "NO" FOR AN ANSWER. BECAUSE OF MINTOFF'S CLEAR
DESIRE TO UTLIZIE THE PROPOSED MEETING TO GAIN A CAMPAIGN
ADVANTAGE OVER THE OPPOSITION NATIONALIST PARTY, THIS
WILL REMAIN AN IRRITANT TO OUR BILATERAL RELATIONS AT
LEAST UNTIL THE ELECTION IS OVER.
EXCEPT FOR THIS IRRITANT, HOWEVER, OFFICIAL U.S./
MALTESE RELATIONS WERE QUIET AND GENRALLY HARMONIOUS
DURING THIS QUARTER, AND THE EMBASSY CONTINED TO HAVE
EXCELLENT ACCESS TO SENIOR OFFICIALS OF THE GOM.
THE NEW U.S. PEACE CORPS VETERINARIAN ARRIVED IN
MALTA DURING THE QUARTER AND IS NOW ENGAGED IN PROJECTS
RECOMMENDED BY THE GOM MINISTRY OF AGRICULTURE AND
FISHERIES.
THE GOM WAS ABLE TO UTILIZE ALMOST THE ENTIRE FIVE
MILLION DOLLAR USG SUPPORTING ASSISTANCE LOAN BEFORE THE
LOAN TERMINATION DATE OF JUNE 15, 1976. THE UNDISBURSED
AMOUNT WAS REPORTED BY AID/W TO BE ONLY SOME DOLLARS
20,720 AS OF JUNE 30.
WITH THE TERMINATION OF THE SUPPORTING ASSISTANCE
LOAN, THE PEACE CORPS VETERINARIAN PROJECT IS THE ONLY
REMIANING BILATERAL U.S. PROGRAM IN MALTA. SMITH



*******************


** 166593 1976PARIS19593 0.007098791 | 1976-07-06 | PARIS | STATE USUN NEW YORK | POSSIBLE SC MEETING ON ISRAELI RESCUE OPERATION
1.  DISCUSSED SUBJECT REFTEL WITH ST. LEGIER, FOREIGN
MINISTRY DIRECTOR FOR UNITED NATIONS AFFAIRS.
2.  ST. LEGIER SAID IT WAS HIS UNDERSTANDING THAT AMIN
HAD FILED COMPLAINT WITH SECURITY COUNCIL, BUT HAD NOT
REQUESTED A MEETING.  GOF HOPES THIS IS TRUE.
2.  IN THE EVENT AN SC MEETING TAKES PLACE, ST. LEGIER
SAID GOF AGREES THAT ANY RESOLUTION MUST NOT BE UNBAL-
ANCED.  UGANDA MUST BE CRITICIZED FOR AIDING THE TERROR-
ISTS.  THE QUESTION OF ISRAEL'S ACTION IS CAUSING GOF
JURIDICAL PROBLEMS.  WHEREAS UGANDA'S AID TO TERRORISTS
IS CLEARLY IN VIOLATION OF INTERNATIONAL CONVENTIONS,
SPECIFICALLY THE 1972 ANTI-HIJACKING TREATY, IT IS DIF-
FICULT TO FIND A PRECEDENT IN INTERNATIONAL LAW TO JUS-
TIFY ISRAEL'S VIOLATION OF UGANDA'S SOVEREIGNTY.  GOF
LAWYERS ARE WORKING ON THIS ASPECT.
3.  BECAUSE OF THE UNCLEAR JURIDICAL ASPECTS, ST. LEGIER
SAID THE BEST COURSE MIGHT BE TO CALL FOR AN OFFICIAL
ENQUIRY IN ORDER TO BURY THE ISSUE.  ON THE BASIC ISSUES,
HOWEVER, THE GOF IS ON OUR SIDE--OPPOSITION TO AN UNBAL-
ANCED RESOLUTION, AND LANGUAGE IN THE RESOLUTION MUST
INCLUDE CRITICISM OF UGANDA'S ASSISTANCE TO THE TERROR-
ISTS.
4.  COMMENT:  ST. LEGIER'S REMARKS REVEAL GOF DILEMMA.
ISRAELI ACTION WAS TREMENDOUSLY POPULAR IN FRANCE.
FRENCH PRESS WAS ECSTATIC IN ITS PRAISE.  ON THE OTHER
HAND, FRANCE WANTS TO GET THE AIR BUS BACK FROM ENTEBBE
AIRPORT, AND DOES NOT WANT TO BE OPPOSED TO AFRICAN
OPINION RIGHT AFTER RECEIVING CRITICISM OF THE NUCLEAR
REACTOR SALE TO SOUTH AFRICA.  HENCE, A DESIRE FOR NO
MEETING, AND FOR NO RESOLUTION IF THERE IS A MEETING.
RUSH

 * 49500 1976CAIRO09079 0.007098599 | 1976-07-03 | CAIRO | STATE | SADAT'S STATEMENTS RE PEACE TERMS
1. IN CASE YOU MISSED IT, SADAT GAVE CHARLES DEVINE OF
READER'S DIGEST, JUNE 30, FOLLOWING COMMENTS ON HIS VIEWS
RE ME PEACE SETTLEMENT TAKEN FROM FBIS AND CHECKED AGAINST
TODAY'S AL-AKHBAR STORY ON THAT INTERVIEW.
2. REPLYING TO A QUESTION BY MR. DEVINE ON WHETHER A
CHANGE IN U.S. ADMINISTRATION AFTER THE ELECTIONS MIGHT
AFFECT THE ABILITY OF THE UNITED STATES TO PARTICIPATE
IN SOLVING THE MIDDLE EAST PROBLEM, PRESIDENT AS-SADAT
SAID: I BELIEVE, A CHANGE IN ADMINISTRATION MIGHT DELAY
A SOLUTION FOR SOME TIME, BUT IT WILL NOT LEAD TO COMPLICA-
TIONS IN THE U.S. ATTITUDE TOWARD THE MIDDLE EAST QUESTION.
NATURALLY, THE UNITED STATES HAS THE RIGHT TO CHOOSE THE
PRESIDENT IT THINKS MOST SUITABLE FOR IT. WHAT I HAVE
READ ABOUT CARTER SHOWS THAT HE SUPPORTS A PEACEFUL
SOLUTION.
3. I AM SURE THAT AFTER HAVING MET WITH MANY OF THE
POLITICIANS IN THE UNITED STATES AND SEEN THE AMERICAN
PEOPLE--AND I TAKE THIS OPPORTUNITY TO ONCE AGAIN THANK
THEM FOR THE WARM HOSPITALITY ACCORDED US DURING OUR LAST
VISIT AND FOR THEIR REAL SENTIMENTS WHICH HAVE GREATLY
MOVED US--THAT THE AMERICAN PEOPLE WANT A PEACEFUL
SOLUTION. THE U.S. GOVERNMENT ALSO WANTS A PEACEFUL
SOLUTION.
4. IF THERE IS A CHANGE IN ADMINISTRATION AFTER THE
ELECTIONS, THIS WOULD DELAY THE PEACEFUL SOLUTION FOR
SOME TIME AS HAPPENED IN 1974. THE SECOND DISENGAGEMENT
AGREEMENT WAS SUPPOSED TO HAVE BEEN CONCLUDED IN 1974
AND NOT, AS HAPPENED, IN 1975. BUT IN VIEW OF THE
WATERGATE ISSUE, THE SECOND DISENGAGEMENT AGREEMENT WAS
ELAYED FOR ONE YEAR. I BELIEVE A NEW ADMINISTRATION, IF
THERE SHOULD BE ONE, WILL NEED SOME TIME TO STUDY AND
ABSORB THE WHOLE SITUATION. AFTER THAT, AS I SAID, AND
WHETHER THE NEW PRESIDENT IS DEMOCRATIC OR REPUBLICAN,
THE UNITED STATES WILL HOLD 99 PERCENT OF THE CARDS IN
THE MIDDLE EAST GAME.
5. MR. DEVINE ASKED PRESIDENT AS-SADAT THIS QUESTION:
MR. PRESIDENT, YOU SAID IN FEBRUARY 1974 THAT YOU WOULD
NOT RUN AGAIN FOR THE POST OF PRESIDENT IN EGYPT. WHAT
MADE YOU CHANGE YOUR MIND ABOUT THAT?
6. REPLYING TO A QUESTION ON THE SOLUTION HE WILL OFFER
TO THE MIDDLE EAST PROBLEM CONCERNING GAZA, SHARM ASH-
SHAYKH, THE PALESTINIANS, THE GOLAN HEIGHTS, SINAI, THE
WEST BANK AND THE GULF OF AQABA, PRESIDENT AS-SADAT SAID:
FIRST, WE MUST AGREE ON THE BASIC FACT THAT THE ISRAELIS
MUST WITHDRAW FROM ALL THE TERRITORIES TO THE 1967 BORDERS,
INCLUDING JERUSALEM. WE WILL THEN CONSIDER SINAI.
7. THE PRESIDENT SAID: I WILL AGREE TO THE STATIONING OF
UN FORCES IN SHARM ASH-SHAYKH AFTER THE ISRAELI WITHDRAWL
FROM THERE. THE UN FORCES CAN STAY THERE TO GUARANTEE
THE FREEDOM OF SHIPPING. REGARDING THE OTHER INTER-
NATIONAL GUARANTEES, I AM WILLING TO ACCEPT THE PRESENCE
OF A UN FORCE IN SHARM ASH-SHAYKH. REGARDING OUR BORDER,
I AM ALSO WILLING TO AGREE TO THE PRESENCE OF UN FORCES
THERE ALSO, PROVIDED THAT THEY ARE STATIONED ON BOTH SIDES.
BUT I WILL BE UNDERSTANDING AND CONSIDERATE CONCERNING
THE PROPORTION OF THE AREA TO BE GIVEN FOR THE STATIONING
OF THESE FORCES. IF ISRAEL SHOWS A WILLINGNESS TO SOLVE
THE PALESTINE QUESTION COMPLETELY, ITS SHIPS CAN PASS
THROUGH THE SUEZ CANAL. WE ARE READY FOR THAT IF THEY
AREA ALSO READY FOR IT.;
8. REGARDING THE PALESTINIANS, I REQUEST THE SETTING UP
OF A PALESTINIAN STATE IN THE WEST BANK AND GAZA WITH A
CORRIDOR BETWEEN THEM.
9. REGARDING THE GOLAN, THE SYRIANS CAN SPEAK FOR THEM-
SELVES. ONCE WE HAVE REACHED THIS STAGE, I DO NOT THINK
THAT PRESIDENT AL-ASAD, FOR INSTANCE, WILL OBJECT TO THE
STATIONING OF OBSERVERS ON THE BORDER. BUT THIS IS SOME-
THING ON WHICH I CANNOT DECIDE. IT IS UP TO PRESIDENT
AL-ASAD AND SYRIA.
10. THE GREAT CONCESSION WHICH WE WILL MAKE ONCE THE
COMPLETE ISRAELI WITHDRAWAL FROM ALL THE OCCUPIED ARAB
TERRITORIES TO THE 1967 BORDERS IS ACHIEVED, THE
PALESTINE PROBLEM IS SOLVED AND A PALESTINIAN STATE
ESTABLISHED, IS THAT WE WILL END THE STATE OF WAR,WHICH
HAS EXISTED FOR THE PAST 28 YEARS. WE WILL THEN TRY TO
BUILD LASTING PEACE IN THE WHOLE REGION.
11. COMMENT: YOU WILL NOTE THAT SADAT ACKNOWLEDGES THAT
A POSSIBLE CHANGE IN ADMINISTRATION MIGHT DELAY SOLUTION
FOR A TIME PENDING STIDY OF THE PROBLEM BY A NEW ADMINISTRA-
TION. BY PUBLICLY INDICATING THIS, AND HAVING IT
PUBLISHED IN CAIRO'S DAILY, AKHBAR, HE IS GIVING HIMSELF
SOME BREATHING SPACE IF THINGS DO NOT WORK OUT THE WAY
HE WOULD LIKE, I. E., RE-ELECTION OF PRESIDENT FORD.
SADAT'S SUBSTANTIVE VIEWS ARE NOT NEW. NOR ARE HIS
STATED CONDITIONS FOR ENDING THE STATE OF WAR, E.G.,
ISRAELI WITHDRAWAL AND ESTABLISHMENT OF A PALESTINIAN
STATE. HE IS TAKING A LEAF OUT OF THE ISRAELI BOOK BY
THUS PUBLICLY STATING HIS WILINGNESS TO END THE STATE
OF WAR, BUT STIPULATING HIS PRICE FOR DOING SO AND MAKING IT
CONSISTENT WITH ARAB ASPIRATIONS. IN PART, OF COURSE, THIS IS FOR
GENERAL ARAB CONSUMPTION. HOWEVER, HE IS ALSO SIGNALLING US AND
THE ISRAELIS ONCE AGAIN THE
THE EXISTING ISRAELI OFFER IS
INADEQUATE. THIS IS THE FIRST TIME I KNOW OF THAT HE
HAS PUBLICLY SUGGESTED UN CONTROLLED DMZ ON THE BORDERS
MIGHT BE PROPORTIONAL RATHER THAN IDENTICAL IN SIZE,
THOUGH HE MADE THIS STATEMENT TO CODEL OBEY LAST AUGUST.
EARLIER IN THE INTERVIEW SADAT REAFFIRMED HIS BELIEF GENEVA IS BEST
FORUM TO BEGIN INITIAL TALKS AND THAT PLO SHOULD BE REPRESENTED.
EILTS



*******************


** 57197 1976COLOMB02411 0.007096746 | 1976-07-07 | COLOMBO | SECSTATE WASHDC TEL AVIV PARIS USUN NEW YORK | SRI LANKA FOREIGN MINISTRY STATEMENT ON ISRAELI ATTACK ON ENTEBBE  AIRPORT
ON ENTEBBE AIRPORT
1. DEPUTY MINISTER OF DEFENSE AND FOREIGN
AFFAIRS, LAKSHMAN
JAYAKODY, ISSUED STATEMENT JULY 6 WHICH CONDEMNED THE
ISRAELI RESCUE OF HOSTAGES AT ENTEBBE AIRPORT "AS AN ACT OF
AGGRESSION AND A GRAVE VIOLATION OF THE SOVEREIGNITY OF
UGANDA AND NEIGHBORING STATES." STATEMENT ALSO STRESSED,
HOWEVER,THAT SRI LANKA DID NOT CONDONE THE HIJACKING OF
PLANES OR THE HOLDING OF HOSTAGES FOR POLITICAL GAINS.
2. TEXT OF STATEMENT IS: "WE DO NOT CONDONE THE HIJACKING
OF PLANES OR THE HOLDING OF HOSTAGES FOR POLITICAL GAINS
WITH CONSEQUENT RISK TO INNOCENT HUMAN LIVES.
"AT THE SAME TIME WE WISH EXPRESS ONCE AGAIN OUR SUPPORT
FOR THE CAUSE OF THE PALESTINIAN PEOPLE. SRI LANKA HAS
TIME AND AGAIN DECLARED HERE SUPPORT FOR THE LEGITIMATE
NATIONAL ASPIRATIONS OF THE PALESTINIAN PEOPLE AND WILL
CONTINUE TO DO SO.
"WE CONDEMN THE ISRAELI ATTACK ONENTEBBE AIRPORT
IN UGANDA. WE CONSIDER IT AN ACT OF AGGRESSION AND A GRAVE
VIOLATION ON THE OSVEREITNITY OF UGANDA AND NEIGHBORING
STATES. WE FULLY SUPPORT THE POSITION TAKEN UP ON THIS
MATTER BY THE SUMMIT CONFERENCE OF THE ORGANIZATION OF
AFRICAN UNITY".
3. COMMENT: STATEMENT APPEARS TO BE ATTEMPT TO PROMOTE
SRI LANKA'S IMAGE AMONG NON-ALINGED. WHILE IT ALSO REITERATES
SRI LANKA'S STRONG SUPPORT FOR PALESTINIAN
CAUSE, DISCLAIMER AT VERY START INDICATES CEYLONESE WANT
TO AVOID ANY IMPLICATION THAT THEY CONDONE OR SUPPORT
TERRIORISM. IN FACT, MANY CEYLONESE HAVE PRIVATELY EXPRESSED
CONSIDERABLE APPROBATION OF ISRAELI ACTION.
REED

 * 170770 1976PORTL00595 0.007096018 | 1976-07-06 | PORT LOUIS | STATE | 13TH ORDINARY OAU SUMMIT ENDS IN SUPERFICIAL AND ONLY PARTIAL AFRICAN  UNITY
ONLY PARTIAL AFRICAN UNITY
SUMMARY: THE OAU SUMMIT, ALREADY EMBROILED IN CONTROVERSY OVER
THE DJIBOUTI ISSUE AND TO AN EVEN GREATER EXTENT WESTERN SAHARA,
WAS BADLY SHAKEN BY THE ISRAELI COMMANDO ACTION IN UGANDA AND THE
SUDANESE COUP ATTEMPT. NEVERTHELESS, THE 13TH ORDINARY OAU SUMMIT
ENDED EARLY ON JULY 6 UNITED IN ITS CONDEMNATION OF ISRAEL'S
ACTION IN ENTEBBE, IN ITS CRITICISM OF FRANCE FOR ITS MAYOTTE
POLICY AND FOR THE SALE OF NUCLEAR REACTORS TO SOUTH AFRICA.
MORE DIFFICULT ISSUES INVOLVING THE INDIVIDUAL NATIONAL INTERESTS
OF AFRICAN STATES (SUCH AS LOS, CERTAIN TYPES OF RELATIONS WITH
SOUTH AFRICA, ETC.) WERE SENT TO STUDY COMMITTEES WHERE DECISIONS
ON THEM COULD BE POSTPONED UNTIL AT LEAST THE FEBRUARY 1977
COUNCIL OF MINISTERS IN ADDIS. ALL FOUR OAU ASSISTANT SECRETARIES
GENERAL WERE ASKED TO REMAIN UNTIL THE END OF ADMIN SECRETARY
GENERAL WILLIAM ETEKI MBOUMOUA'S TERM IS COMPLETED IN 1978. AT
THAT TIME, THE SECRETARIAT WILL BE DIVIDED INTO FIVE ASSISTANT
SECRETARY GENERALSHIPS, EACH ONE REPRESENTING A DIFFERENT
GEOGRAPHICAL AREA. THE DJIBOUTI RESOLUTION PASSED UNANIMOUSLY
WITHOUT SPECIFIC SOMALI RESERVATION. THE SUMMIT DECIDED TO CALL AN
EXTRAORDINARY OAU SUMMIT TO DEAL WITH THE PROBLEM OF WESTERN
SAHARA. DELEGATES HOPED THIS EXTRAORDINARY SUMMIT WOULD BE HELD
WITHIN ONE MONTH BUT CERTAINLY BEFORE THE END OF THE YEAR. END
SUMMARY.
1. OAU DELEGATES UNANIMOUSLY CRITICIZED ISRAEL FOR THE COMMANDO
OPERATION IN ENTEBBE. KENYAN VICE PRESIDENT ARAP MOI MADE A
STATEMENT DENOUNCING ISRAELI AGGRESSION AND CLAIMING THAT KENYA
WAS "AGGRESSED" AGAINST BY ISRAEL AS WELL. HE TRACED THE PROBABLE
ISRAELI FLIGHT PATH, AND STATED THAT ISRAEL HAD PROBABLY VIOLATED
THE AIRSPACE OF OTHER AFRICAN AND ARAB COUNTRIES. COMMENT:
ALTHOUGH TACIT KENYAN SUPPORT FOR THE ISRAELI OPERATION WAS
GENERALLY ACKNOWLEDGED PRIVATELY BY OAU DELEGATES, THERE WAS NO
PUBLIC OR OVERT CRITICISM OF KENYA OVER THE OPERATION OTHER THAN
AMIN'S MESSAGE TO THE CONFERENCE READ BY HIS REPRESENTATIVE.
END COMMENT.
2. IN AN EARLIER STATEMENT UGANDAN FORMIN LT. COL. JUMA ORIS DE-
SCRIBED THE ISRAELI ACTION WHICH HAD DESTROYED 7 MIG 21'S, 4 MIG
17'S AND SEVERAL CIVILIAN AIRCRAFT. ACCORDING TO ORIS "THE TREACH-
EROUS ATTACK WAS LAUNCHED AND DIRECTED FROM THE SOIL OF THE NEIGH-
BORING STATE OF KENYA." ORIS CALLED FOR TOTAL CONDEMNATION OF AN
AFRICAN STATE WHICH WOULD PROVIDE "HER TERRITORY TO ZIONIST AND
COLONIST COMMANDOS TO INVADE ANOTHER AFRICAN STATE".
3. LIBERIA SPONSORED AND THE SUMMIT ADOPTED A RESOLUTION
EXPRESSING DEEP ALARM AT THE "ISRAELI AGGRESSION" WHICH IT HELD
TO BE A THREAT TO INTERNATIONAL PEACE. SUCH AGGRESSION, THE
RESOLUTION CONTINUED, IS THE RESULT OF ISRAELI-SOUTH AFRICAN
COOPERATION WHICH LIBERIA STRONGLY CONDEMNED. THE ISRAELI AGGRESS-
ION "THWARTED" PRESIDENT AMIN'S HUMANITARIAN EFFORTS TO OBTAIN THE
HOSTAGES' RELEASE, THE RESOLUTION SAID.
4. THE SUMMIT AGREED THAT A SPECIAL OAU SUMMIT WOULD BE HELD TO
DISCUSS THE PROBLEM OF WESTERN SAHARA. IT WAS HOPED THAT THIS
MEETING WOULD BE HELD WITHIN ONE MONTH BUT AT THE LATEST BEFORE THE
END OF THE YEAR. AFTER THE JULY 3 COUNCIL OF MINISTER'S VOTE TO
RECONSIDER THE WESTERN SAHARA QUESTION, MOROCCAN DELEGATES REFUSED
TO TAKE PART IN SUMMIT DELIBERATIONS. MAURITANIAN PRESIDENT OULD
DADDAH, HOWEVER, REMAINED AND STAUNCHLY DEFENDED THE MOROCCAN-
MAURITANIAN POSITION.
5. THE SUMMIT ACCEPTED WITHOUT CHANGE THE DRAFT RESOLUTION ON
DJIBOUTI WHICH CALLS UPON ALL STATES TO REFRAIN FROM INTERFERING
IN FTAI INTERNAL AFFAIRS AND TO ABSTAIN FROM ANY ACTION LIKELY TO
IMPEDE OR ADVERSELY AFFECT PROGRESS TOWARD INDEPENDENCE. THE
RESOLUTION URGES ALL POLITICAL PARTIES AND GROUPS AS WELL AS THE
TWO LIBERATION MOVEMENTS RECOGNIZED BY THE OAU TO HOLD A ROUND-
TABLE CONFERENCE ON NEUTRAL GROUND UNDER OAU AUSPICES IN ORDER TO
DEVELOP A COMMON POLITICAL PLATFORM BEFORE AN INDEPENDENCE
REFERENDUM. IT DIRECTS THE OAU FACT-FINDING MISSION TO OBSERVE
THE REFERENDUM AND SUBSEQUENT ELECTIONS AND TO ASSIST IN THE
DETERMINATION OF REFUGEE STATUS ON THE BASIS OF THE FACT-FINDING
MISSION'S RECOMMENDATIONS. IN THIS REGARD, THE PROPOSED ROUNDTABLE
CONFERENCE WILL PROBABLY BE HELD AT ACCRA DURING THE FIRST HALF
OF AUGUST.
6. ALL FOUR OAU ASSISTANT SECRETARIES GENERAL WERE ASKED TO
REMAIN IN THEIR POSITIONS UNTIL 1978 SO THAT THEIR TENURE WOULD
COINCIDE WITH THAT OF OAU ADMIN SECRETARY GENERAL ETEKI. AT THAT
TIME, THE RESPONSIBILITIES OF THE FOUR ASSISTANT SECRETARIES
GENERAL WILL BE DIVIDED AMONG FIVE REGIONS TO INCLUDE THE NEWLY
AGREED UPON SOUTHERN AFRICAN REGION. (THE OTHER FOUR REGIONS ARE
NORTHERN, WESTERN, EASTERN AND CENTRAL AFRICA).
7. ALTHOUGH IT IS TOO EARLY TO PREDICT THE FINAL REACTION OF OAU
MEMBERS TO THE ISRAELI ACTION IN UGANDA, IT IS UNLIKELY THAT THEY
WILL GO BEYOND THE RITUAL CONDEMNATION MADE AT THE SUMMIT.
MOST PROBABLY, NIGERIAN FORMIN GARBA'S STATEMENT (CF PORT LOUIS
576) WILL HOLD TRUE: THERE IS LITTLE SUB-SAHARAN AFRICAN INTEREST
IN EXPULSION OF ISRAEL FROM THE UNITED NATIONS. AS FAR AS WE
COULD TELL, OTHER MULTILATERAL ISSUES, SUCH AS PUERTO RICO AND
KOREA, WERE TOTALLY MISSING FROM THE OAU DELIBERATIONS.
8. COMMENT: THE 13TH ORDINARY SUMMIT HAD THE SMALLEST ATTENDANCE
OF AFRICAN HEADS OF STATE AND GOVERNMENT ON RECORD. (BONGO OF
GABON, JAWARA OF GAMBIA, SENGHOR OF SENEGAL, KAUNDA OF ZAMBIA,
OULD DADDAH OF MAURITANIA, NIMEIRI OF SUDAN, RAMGOOLAM OF
MAURITIUS, MANCHAM OF SEYCHELLES, AMIN OF UGANDA, TEFERI OF
ETHIOPIA.) DECISIONS ON DIFFICULT AND DIVISIVE ISSUES SUCH AS
LOS AND CERTAIN RELATIONS WITH SOUTH AFRICA WERE POSTPONED. AN
EXCEPTION WAS THE RESOLUTION ON DJIBOUTI WHERE ALL AFRICAN NATIONS
COULD AGREE ON THE PRINCIPLE OF NON-INTERFERENCE AND INDEPENDENCE
FOR THE TERRITORY. THE WESTERN SAHARA ISSUE, HOWEVER, ALMOST SPLIT
THE CONFERENCE. WESTERN SAHARA REMAINS A BURNING PROBLEM AND MUST
BE DEALT WITH SOON. DELEGATES AND SECRETARIAT MEMBERS WORKED
DILIGENTLY AND WITH DEDICATION BUT REPEATEDLY ADMITTED TO EMBOFF
AND OTHER "OUTSIDERS" THAT THE OAU IS PRIMARILY INVOLVED IN "BLAH-
BLAH" (USELESS TALK) INSTEAD OF CONCRETE, DECISIVE AND PRODUCTIVE
MATTERS.
KEELEY



*******************


 * 63761 1976DAMASC04376 0.007093155 | 1976-07-07 | DAMASCUS | STATE | JULY 7 SYRIAN MEDIA REPORT INCREASED FIGHTING IN LEBANON; TUNISIAN AND  BAHRAINI FONMINS DEPART DAMASCUS

FOR HOME

AND TWO ENLISTED MENPLUS DESTRUCTION OF TWO SYRIAN LORRIES.
(COMMENT: ON OTHER HAND US OFFICIAL IN CONVOY TRAVELLING
BEIRUT-SIDON-NABATIYYEH-DAMASCUS TODAY NOTED NO FIGHTING.)
2. PLA COMMANDER BYDAYRI ESCORTED ARAB AND FOREIGN
JOURNALISTS JULY 6 ON TOUR OF YARMUK PALESTINIAN
CAMP IN ATTEMPT TO PROVE LIFE GOING ON AS NORMAL AND
FALSITY OF CLAIMS THAT PALESTINIANS IN CAMP AREA BEING

CAMPS FROM INVASION AND SIEGE. HE RIDICULED IRAQ'S DISPATCH
OF MILITARY FORCES TO BORDER, AS DID DEFMIN TLAS IN ARTICLE
EXCERPTED FROM MILITARY JOURNAL. TLAS DENOUNCED IRAQI
HYPROCRISY FOR URGING CREATION OF REJECTION FRONT AGAINST

BLOCKING FLOW OF OIL THROUGH PIPELINE ON OTHER. HE REAFFIRMED
SYRIAN COMMITMENT TO OBTAINING ISRAELI WITHDRAWAL FROM
OCCUPIED TERRITORIES BY PEACEFUL MEANS RATHER THAN WAR,
"
WHICH INTERNATIONAL COMMUNITY WILL NOT PERMIT."
4. COLUMNISTS CONTINUED TO HAMMER AWAY AT IMPERIALIST-ZIONIST
PLOT AGAINST LEBANON AND TO DEFEND SYRO-PALESTINIAN
COOPERATION.
5. COMMENT: VISIT TO YARMUK CAMP CONDUCTED BY BUDAYRI
MAY BE PART OF NEW SYRIAN CAMPAIGN TO PATCH UP ITS
DIFFERENCES WITH PALESTINIANS. ONE PALESTINIAN
OBSERVER OF LOCAL SCENE TOLD US THAT RECENT EDITORIAL
IN LOCAL PRESS, WHICH SPOKE OF "TRANSCENDING MISTAKES
AND IRRITATIONS REGARDLESS OF PAST POSITIONS," INTERPRETED
BY MANY IN PALESTINIAN COMMUNITY AS HINT REGIME WOULD
LIKE TO RESOLVE ITS DISPUTE WITH FATAH AND OTHER PALESTINIAN
ORGANIZATIONS. WE PREFER TO SUSPEND JUDGEMENT UNTIL WE
SEE MORE EVIDENCE OF THIS TREND.

 * 139510 1976MOSCOW10713 0.007092447 | 1976-07-07 | MOSCOW | STATE | NEW MOVES AGAINST JEWISH EMIGRANTS
1. SUMMARY. JEWISH SOURCES TELL US OF NEW RESTRICTIVE
INTERPRETATIONS OF AND CHANGES IN THE PROCEDURES GOVERN-
ING EMIGRATION. IN ONE CITY THE POLICE HAVE BECOME INVOLVED
IN DISTRIBUTING "VYZOVS" LETTERS OF INVITATION, IN OTHER CITIES
A NEW AND RESTRICTIVE DEFINITION OF WHAT CONSTITUTES A "FAMILY"
MAY RESULT IN A LESSENING IN THE NUMBER OF APPLICANTS FOR
EMIGRATION. IN ANOTHER CITY, WITH A LARGE JEWISH COMMUNITY,
ONLY ONE VYZOV HAS BEEN RECEIVED IN TWO MONTHS. OUR
SOURCES SPEAK OF A POSSIBLE CAMPAIGN IN THE WEST TO
PRESSURE THE SOVIET AUTHORITIES TO CHANGE THEIR POSITION.
END SUMMARY.
2. JEWISH DISSIDENTA MARK AZBEL AND VIKTOR BRAYLOVSKIY
TOLD US JULY 6 OF NEW MOVES BY THE SOVIET AUTHORITIES
TO KEEP DOWN THE NUMBER OF POTENTIAL JEWISH EMIGRANTS.
IN ODESSA, OUR SOURCES SAY, THE POSTAL AUTHORITIES
HAVE BEEN TOLD TO GIVE ALL VYZOVS WHICH THEY RECEIVE
TO THE POLICE. THE LATTER CALL IN THE ADDRESSESS AND
ASK FIRST IF HE HAS ANY RELATIVES IN ISRAEL. IF THE
ANSWER IS NO (EITHER FROM FEAR OF REVEALING THIS FACT
OR BECAUSE THERE ARE NONE), THE VYZOV IS THROWN AWAY.
IF THE ANSWER IS YES, THE NEXT QUESTION IS TO ASK FOR
THE NAME OF THE RELATIVE. THE VYZOV IS DISCARDED IF
THE NAME DOES NOT CORRESPOND TO THAT GIVEN BY THE
ADDRESSEE. IF THE NAMES CORRESPOND, THE ADDRESSEE
IS THEN ASKED ABOUT THE NATURE OF THE RELATIONSHIP. HE
GETS HIS VYZOV ONLY IF THE RELATIONSHIP CORRESPONDS.
3. OUR SOURCES REPORT THAT THE INVOLVEMENT OF THE
POLICE IN ODESSA HAS BEEN GOING ON FOR ABOUT A MONTH.
THEY OBSERVE RUEFULLY THAT THIS APPROACH GIVES THE
AUTHORITIES SEVERAL ADVANTAGES (AND ADD THAT IT IS
ODD THAT THE AUTHORITIES HAD NOT PREVIOUSLY THOUGHT
OF THIS TACTIC). FIRST, THERE IS THE NATURAL FEAR
OF ANY SOVIET CITIZEN TO HAVE ANY CONFRONTATION WITH
THE POLICE. MORE SIGNIFICANTLY, HOWEVER, GIVEN THE
LARGE NUMBRS OF WHOLLY OR PARTIALLY FALSE ISRAELI
VYZOVS (FICATIONAL RELATIVES OR A FICTITIOUS RELATION-
SHIP), THIS POLICY, IF EXTENDED TO THE USSR AS A WHOLE,
WOULD GREATLY REDUCE THE POTENTIAL POOL OF JEWS ABLE
TO MEET THE REQUIREMENTS FOR EMIGRATION. OUR SOURCES
SAY THAT THEY, AND BY IMPLICATION THE JEWISH COMMUNITY
AS A WHOLE, ARE EXTREMELY CONCERNED ABOUT THE IMPLICA-
TIONS OF AN EXTENSION OF THE ODESSAN APPROACH.
4. AZBEL AND BRAYLOVSKIY ALSO REPORT THAT ONLY ONE
VYZOV HAS, TO THEIR KNOWLEDGE, BEEN RECEIVED IN KHARKOV
IN THE LAST TWO MONTHS. THEY SAU THAT SEVERAL KHARKOV
JEWS HAD RECEIVED CABLES OR TELEPHONE CALLS FROM
ABROAD INFORMING THEM THAT VYZOVS WERE ON THE WAY, BUT
ONLY ONE HAS GOTTEN THROUGH. THEY ADDED THAT THE
RECIPIENT OF THE VYZOV TREATED THE EVENT AS THE OCCASION
FOR A PARTY, AND IT WAS THEN, ABOUT TWO WEEKS AGO, THAT
IT BECAME CLEAR JUST HOW BAD THE EMIGRATION SITUATION
HAD BECOME IN THAT CITY. (THERE ARE ALMOST 77,000 JEWS
IN KHARKOV OBLAST, ACCORDING TO THE 1970 CENSUS.)
5. OTHER RELIABLE SOURCES REPORT THAT THE NEW DEFINITION
OF FAMILY, I.X. FOR THE PURPOSE OF EMIGRATION, A FAMILY
TO BE "REUNIFIED" WOULD BE CONSIDERED AS HUSBAND, WIFE,
AND UNMARRIED (OR MINOR) CHILDREN -- IS BEING APPLIED NOT
ONLY IN MOSCOW (SEE MOSCOW 10146) BUT ALSO IN KIEV,
KISHINEV AND NOVOSIBIRSK. THESE SOURCES CAUTION THAT
THEY HAVE STILL NOT SEEN EVIDENCE THAT THE NEW DEFINITION
WILL BE APPLIED ON AN ALL-UNION BASIS. OUR SOURCES
CLAIM THAT SEVERAL OVIR HAVE SAID THAT THE NEW POLICY
FULLY ACCORDS WITH THE HELSINKI PRINCIPLES AND WILL BE
APPLIED IN THE FUTURE. THEY NOTE THAT IT WOULD BE
IN KEEPING WITH THE CUSTOMARY SOVIET APPROACH TO SUCH
MATTERS THAT THEY DECIDE TO MAKE THEIR POLICY ON JEWISH
EMIGRATION MORE STRICT WHILE AT THE SAME TIME WRAPPING
THEMSELVES IN THE CSCE FINAL ACT.
6. OUR SOURCES SAY THAT IF THEY CAN GET
EVIDENCE OF A CHANGE TOWARD GREATER RESTRICTIVENESS IN
DEGREE OF CONSANGUINUITY, THE JEWISH "REFUSENIK"
LEADERSHIP WILL ENDEAVOR TO MOUNT A CAMPAIGN IN THE WEST,
ESPECIALLY IN THE U.S. THEY TELL US THAT THEY FEEL
THE NEWLY-CREATED U.S. CONGRESSIONAL
CSCE COULD BE USEFUL COMMISSION IN THIS EFFORT. THEY
ADD THAT THE AMERICAN PRESIDENTIAL ELECTION CAMPAIGN
MIGHT ALSO PROVIDE THEM WITH OPPORTUNITIES TO
MAKE THEIR POINT.
7. COMMENT: IF THESE RESTRICTIVE MEASURES ARE INDEED
TO BE APPLIED ON AN ALL-UNION BASIS, IT WOULD MAKE THE
SITUATION OF THE WOULD-BE EMIGRANT EVEN MORE DIFFI-
CULT THAN IT ALREADY SI. APPLICATION OF THE ODESSA AND
THE "CSCE DEFINITION" MEASURES UNDOUBTEDLY WOULD
DIMINISH THE NUMBER OF SOVIET JEWS ABLE EVEN
TO APPLY SUCCESSFULLY FOR EMIGRATION. WE FEEL IT QUITE
POSSIBLE THAT WIDER USE OF THE MEASURES WOULD CAUSE THE
REFUSENIKS TO TRY TO ORGANIZE A CAMPAIGN.
8. IN THIS CONNECTION, WE NOTE THAT THE INFORMATION
WE REPORT HERE HAS COME FROM SEVERAL OF THE DIFFERENT
GROUPS THAT MAKE UP THE REFUSENIK COMMUNITY. WHILE
THESE GROUPS TEND TO BE MUTUALLY ANTIPATHETIC,
RESTRICTIONS ON EMIGRATION AND A GENERALIZED TIGHTENING
UP ON THE PROCEDURES COULD WELL PROVIDE THE IMPETUS FOR
THEM TO UNITE. THE REFUSENIK GROUPS NORMALLY HAVE
SEPARATE LINES OF COMMUNICATION TO DIFFERENT WESTERN
ORGANIZATIONS AND PROMINENT INDIVIDUALS: AN AGREEMENT
TO COORDINATE ACTION IN THE USSR AND IN THE WEST COULD
RESULT IN AN UNUSUALLY VIGOROUS CAMPAIGN.
STOESSEL



*******************


** 309224 1976TELAV04645 0.007092118 | 1976-07-06 | TEL AVIV | STATE | ISRAELI/EGYPTIAN JOINT COMMISSION
1.  DURING JULY 6 MEETING WITH AMBASSADOR TOON AND SSM
DIRECTOR KONTOS, MINDEF PERES WAS ASKED IF HE VIEWED THE
JOINT COMMISSION AS A USEFUL FORUM.  HIS RESPONSE WAS
DECIDEDLY POSITIVE.  HE SAID IT WAS A VEHICLE WHICH EN-
COURAGED DE FACTO COOPERATION BETWEEN EGYPT AND ISRAEL.
SEVERAL POINTS OF CONTENTION HAVE BEEN RESOLVED AS A RESULT
OF NEGOTIATIONS CONDUCTED UNDER THE AEGIS OF THE JOINT
COMMISSION.
2.  ACCORDING TO PERES, EGYPT HAS RECENTLY REQUESTED ADDITIONAL
MEETINGS OF THE JOINT COMMISSION TO DISCUSS SPECIFIC
PROBLEM AREAS, SOME OF WHICH PERES DESCRIBED AS "TOUCHY."
THE COMMISSION HAS MET TWICE TO DISCUSS THESE PROBLEMS.
PERES SAID THAT AGREEMENT ON SEVERAL OF THE AREAS WAS
REACHED ON THE SPOT AND OTHERS ARE STILL IN NEGOTIATION.
AT EGYPT'S REQUEST, NO PUBLICITY HAS BEEN GIVEN THESE
MEETINGS.
3.  THE ONLY SPECIFIC POINT CITED BY PERES WAS THE ISSUE OF
BORDER TRANSIT BY RESIDENTS OF EGYPT AND GAZA STRIP.  PERES
CLAIMED THAT ISRAELI FOOT-DRAGGING RESULTED FROM FEAR
OF REPORTED EPIDEMIC OF PLAGUE IN EGYPT, BUT THAT FEARS
HAVE NOW BEEN ALLAYED.
TOON

** 309214 1976TELAV04606 0.007090061 | 1976-07-04 | TEL AVIV | STATE USUN NEW YORK | RABIN KNESSET STATEMENT ON ISRAELI ACTION IN UGANDA SUMMARY
SUMMARY
1.  PRIME MINISTER RABIN, AT SPECIAL KNESSET SESSION AT 3PM ON JULY
4, DELIVERED FIFTEEN MINUTE STATEMENT TO PACKED CHAMBER ON GOI
DECISIONS AND IDF ACTIVITY AT ENTEBBE AIRPORT ON NIGHT OF JULY 3-4.
HIS MAIN POINT WAS THAT ISRAELI GOVERNMENT BEARS EXCLUSIVE RESPON-
SIBILITY FOR THE RESCUE OPERATION.  ALL KNESSET PARTIES EXCEPT RAKAH
COMMUNISTS ADOPTED RESOLUTION PRAISING THE IDF ACTION.  FOLLOWING
ARE HIGHLIGHTS.  END SUMMARY.
2.  THE ISRAELI DEFENSE FORCES (IDF), RABIN SAID, HAD CARRIED OUT
WITH GREAT HEROISM THE GOVERNMENT'S DECISION TO RESCUE THE HOSTAGES
ON THE AIR FRANCE AIRCRAFT AT ENTEBBE AIRPORT.  THREE ISRAELIS, TWO
CIVILIAN HOSTAGES AND THE MILITARY COMMANDER, HAD BEEN KILLED.
(RABIN DID NOT SPECIFY UGANDAN OR TERRORIST CASUALTIES).  THIS WAS ON
E
OF THE FINEST OPERATIONS IN THE IDF'S HISTORY, AND ONE OF WHICH ALL
ISRAELIS COULD BE JUSTIFIABLY PROUD.
3.  THE ISRAELI GOVERNMENT ALONE BEARS THE RESPONSIBILITY FOR THIS
RESCUE OPERATION WHICH WAS NOT COORDINATED WITH ANY OTHER GOVERNMENT.
HOWEVER, ALL GOVERNMENTS MUST WORK TOGETHER IN THE CONTINUING
STRUGGLE AGAINST INTERNATIONAL AIR TERRORISM.
4.  RABIN REVIEWED DEVELOPMENT OF EVENTS SINCE START OF HIJACKING
INCIDENT, EMPHASIZING THE UNIQUE DIFFICULTIES CONFRONTING THE GOI
IN DEALING WITH SITUATION INVOLVING GOVERNMENT OF UGANDA WITH WHICH
ISRAEL DOES NOT HAVE DIPLOMATIC RELATIONS.  FROM THE OUTSET, THERE
WAS FULL POLITICAL COORDINATION WITH THE FRENCH GOVERNMENT FOR THE
RELEASE OF THE HOSTAGES.  IT BECAME CLEAR DURING THE WEEK THAT A) A
MAIN OBJECTIVE OF THE TERRORISTS WAS TO KEEP THE ISRAELI PASSENGERS
HOSTAGES AND B) IDI AMIN, THE HEAD OF THE UGANDAN GOVERNMENT, WAS
COOPERATING WITH THE TERRORISTS.
5.  ON JULY 1, THE ISRAELI GOVERNMENT DECLARED ITS READINESS TO NE-
GOTIATE AN EXCHANGE OF PRISONERS FOR THE RELEASE OF THE HOSTAGES.
THIS WAS NOT A PHONY DEVICE TO BUY TIME.  THE GOI WAS PREPARED TO
IMPLEMENT ITS JULY 1 DECISION.
6.  SIMULTANEOUSLY, HOWEVER, THE IDF FORMULATED ITS PLANS FOR A RESCU
E
OPERATION.  IN THE LAST PHASE, THE GOI UNANIMOUSLY AUTHORIZED THE IDF
TO CARRY OUT THIS OPERATION.  THE GOVERNMENT MAINTAINED FULL CONSUL-
TATIONS AND BRIEFINGS WITH THE KNESSET FOREIGN AFFAIRS AND SECURITY
COMMITTEE THROUGHOUT THE VARIOUS STAGES OF DECISION-MAKING.
7.  THIS RESCUE OPERATION CONSTITUTES ISRAEL'S CONTRIBUTION TO THE
INTERNATIONAL FIGHT AGAINST TERRORISM.  BUT THIS STRUGGLE IS FAR FROM
FINISHED AND IT WILL REQUIRE CONTINUING VIGILANCE AND ACTION.  IN
CLOSING, RABIN AGAIN NOTED THAT THE RESCUE OPERATION WAS ONE OF THE
GREATEST ACHIEVEMENTS OF THE IDF.
8.  LIKUD OPPOSITION LEADER, BEGIN SAID THAT ISRAEL HAD NOT HAD
NATIONAL UNITY AS GREAT AS IT ENJOYED TODAY SINCE ITS VICTORY IN THE
1967 WAR.  HE PAID THIBUTE TO THE IDF, AND EXPRESSED CONDOLENCES TO
THE ISRAELI VICTIMS.  CONGRATULATING RABIN FOR HIS LEADERSHIP, BEGIN
SAID THAT RESCUE OPERATION HAD FULL SUPPORT OF THE LIKUD, AND THAT IN
THIS MOMENT INTERNAL POLITICAL DIFFERENCES WERE TRANSCENDED BY SENSE
OF NATIONAL UNITY.  BEGIN URGED FORMATION OF SPECIAL COMMANDO UNIT TO
COMBAT TERRORISM.  HE COMPARED TERRORISTS TO NAZIS, AND MADE SHARP
ATTACK ON SOVIETS FOR SUPPLYING UGANDA'S RACIST DICTATOR WITH MIGS
AND OTHER EQUIPMENT.  HE WARNED ARABS THAT ISRAEL WILL NOT BE PASSIVE
IN CONFRONTING ITS ENEMIES, ALTHOUGH IT SEEKS TO LIVE IN PEACE WITH
ITS NEIGHBORS.
9.  AT CLOSE OF 45 MINUTE SESSION, ALL PARTIES EXCEPT RAKAH COMMU-
NISTS ADOPTED RESOLUTION EXPRESSING APPRECIATION TO IDF, CONDOLENCES
TO ISRAELI DEAD, AND QUICK RECOVERY FOR THE WOUNDED.
10.  COMMENT:  CABINET AND KNESSET MEMBERS WERE OBVIOUSLY RELIEVED
AT END OF WEEK LONG ORDEAL AND NEAR-JUBILANT OVER ITS OUTCOME.
SUCCESSFUL RESCUE OPERATION HAS GIVEN STRONG BOOST TO PUBLIC MORALE
AND CERTAINLY STRENTHENED RABIN GOVERNMENT'S DOMESTIC POSITION.  IN
CONVERSATION WITH EMBOFF, KNESSET MEMBERS EXPRESSED APPRECIATION FOR
PRESIDENTIAL MESSAGE WHICH HAD ALREADY RECEIVED WIDE DISSEMINATION.
TOON



*******************


 * 67043 1976DUBLIN01309 0.007089058 | 1976-07-06 | DUBLIN | STATE | IRISH HOTELS BOMBED
1. FOUR HOTELS IN THE IRISH REPUBLIC WERE BOMBED JULY 3 IN AN
ACTION THAT APPEARS TO BE RETALIATION FOR KILLINGS OF PROTESTANT
BUSINESSMEN IN NORTHERN IRELAND.  THE BOMBINGS WERE PRECEDED
BY A TELEPHONE WARNING FROM A MAN WITH A NORTHERN IRISH ACCENT WHO
IDENTIFIED HIMSELF AS "CAPTAIN BLACK OF THE ULSTER FREEDOM
FIGHTERS."  FOUR PERSONS WERE INJURED IN THE BOMBINGS; FURTUNATELY,
ONE SERIOUSLY.
2. THE FOLLOWING ARE THE FOUR HOTELS THAT WERE BOMBED:
A) DUBLIN'S GRESHAM HOTEL WERE 25 LBS OF GELIGNITE WERE
HIDDEN IN A LINEN CLOSET ON SECOND FLOOR.  NONE OF THE 200
GUESTS OR 150 STAFF OF THIS LUXURY HOTEL WAS INJURED, ALTHOUGH
SOME WERE TREATED FOR SHOCK.
B) ROSSLARE'S GREAT SOUTHERN HOTEL. A SUITCASE OF EXPLOSIVES
WAS LEFT IN A PARKING BAY UNDER THE HOTEL.  SIXTEEN OF THE
HOTEL'S 100 BEDROOMS WERE DAMAGED.  THREE PERSONS WERE TREATED
FOR SHOCK.
C) LIMERICK'S ROYAL GEORGE HOTEL. A 10 LB BOMB CAUSED CONSIDERABLE
DAMAGE AND INJURED A TEN YEAR OLD BOY.
D) KILLARNEY'S TORC GREAT SOUTHERN HOTEL. GUESTS HAD BEEN
EVACUATED WHEN THE BOMB EXPLODED NEAR A TANK OF BUTANEGAS.
FORTUNATELY, THE GAS WAS NOT IGNITED.
3. THE BOMBINGS CAUSED SHOCK AND DISMAY THROUGHOUT THE
REPUBLIC OF IRELAND, AND ONE OF THE MAIN CONCERNS EXPRESSED
IN THE IRISH NEWSPAPERS WAS THAT OF THE EFFECT OF THE BOMBINGS
ON TOURISM AND INVESTMENT. THE TOURIST SEASON IN IRELAND HAD
GOTTEN OFF TO A GOOD START THIS YEAR, AND IRISH TOURIST OFFICIALS
WERE HOPING FOR A SHARP INCREASE IN THE NUMBER OF TOURISTS
THIS YEAR.  TOURIST BOARD OFFICIALS FEAR THAT MANY CANCELLATIONS
WILL RESULT FROM THE BOMBINGS.  ONE HIGH LEVEL TOURIST
OFFICIAL PRIVATELY COMMENTED TO AN EMBASSY OFFICER THAT THE
ISRAELI RAID IN UGANDA MAY HAVE BEEN OF SOME HELP IN THIS
RESPECT, INASMUCH AS IT PUSHED THE NEWS OF THE IRISH BOMBINGS TO
THE INSIDE PAGES OF THE NEWSPAPERS.  NEVERTHELESS, THE
BOMBINGS WILL UNDOUBTEDLY HAVE SOME EFFECT ON TOURISM, ALTHOUGH
THE EXTENT IS DIFFCICULT TO ASSESS AT THIS TIME.  A SOUTHAMPTON
SOCCER CLUB HAS ALREADY CANCELLED TWO MATCHES THAT WERE TO HAVE
BEEN PLAYED IN IRELAND AT THE END OF JULY - A NUMBER OF TEAM
MEMBERS REPORTEDLY REFUSED TO TRAVEL.
4. THE GOVERNMENT IS REVIEWING THE SECURITY SITUATION AND
SECURITY MEASURES IN BORDER AREAS ARE REPORTEDLY BEING
INTENSIFIED. CURLEY



*******************


** 94747 1976KATHMA02882 0.007088902 | 1976-07-06 | KATHMANDU | SECSTATE WASHDC NEW DELHI TEL AVIV | NEPALESE REACTION TO ISRAELI RAID
1. PRIVATE REACTION OF NEPALESE LEADERSHIP TO RECENT
ISRAELI RAID AGAINST ENTEBBE AIRPORT IS NEARLY UNIVERSAL
IN ITS ACCLAIM. FOREING MINISTRY OFFICIALS EXPRESSED RELIEF

THAT THEY THOUGHT ISRAEL SHOULD BE CONGRATULATED BY WORLD
FOR ITS PROMPT AND DECISIVE ATTACK, BUT BOTH ADMITTED THEY
COULD NOT MAKE SUCH STATEMENTS PUBLICLY.
2. EDITORIAL COMMENT HAS BEEN BALANCED. SEMI-OFFICIAL
DAILY RISING NEPAL OFFERED VIEW THAT RAID WILL
STRENGTHEN THE VIEW OF "NO COMPROMISE HARD LINE
IN DEALING WITH HIJACKERS... AND COULD THUS
LEAD TO DISCOURAGING WOULD-BE-HIJACKERS" IN
FUTURE. PAPER ALSO NOTES, HOWEVER, THAT RAID
WAS CLEAR VIOLATION OF UGANDAN SOVEREIGNTY CARRIED
OUT WITH ASSITANCE OF KENYA, FACT WHICH WILL
HAVE SERIOUS REPERCUSSIONS FOR POLITICS IN AFRICA.
EDITORIAL CONCLUDES BY STATING THAT TERRORISM
IS LIEKLY TO PERSIST AS LONG AS ROOT CAUSES
REMAIN UNSOLVED AND CALLS FOR JUST SOLUTION TO PALESTININAN
PROBELM.
MAYTAG

** 309223 1976TELAV04644 0.007088881 | 1976-07-06 | TEL AVIV | STATE | TRAFFIC ACROSS THE ISRAELI/LEBANESE BORDER
1.  DURING JULY 6 MEETING WITH AMBASSADOR TOON AND DIRECTOR
OF SSM, KONTOS, MINDEF PERES DISCUSSED SITUATION ON ISRAEL'S
BORDERS.  HE MADE POINT THAT BORDER CONDITIONS ARE REMARKABLE
GIVEN FACT THAT A STATE OF WAR STILL EXISTS BETWEEN ISRAEL
AND HER NEIGHBORS.  PERES CALLED THE EGYPTIAN FRONTIER
"PEACEFUL," STRESSED THE "OPEN BRIDGES" POLICY ON THE
JORDANIAN FRONTIER, AND DESCRIBED THE LEBANESE BORDER AS
"THE MOST PEACEFUL FRONTIER IN THE WORLD."
2.  FROM HIS DESCRIPTION IT SEEMS CLEAR THAT THERE IS A
SIGNIFICANT AMOUNT OF TRAFFIC ACROSS THIS BORDER.  PERES
CLAIMS THAT WELL OVER A THOUSAND LEBANESE HAVE CROSSED INTO
ISRAEL FOR MEDICAL TREATMENT.  MOST ARE TREATED AND RETURN
IMMEDIATELY TO LEBANON.  SOME HOWEVER, ARE ADMITTED TO
ISRAELI HOSPITALS WHERE THEY STAY AS LONG AS REQUIRED.
THESE LATTER INCLUDE CASUALTIES OF THE FIGHTING AS WELL
AS WOMEN ABOUT TO GIVE BIRTH.  THE IDF HAS ESTABLISHED
CLINICS NEAR THE BORDER, BUT PERES ASSERTED THAT CIVILIAN
HOSPITALS ARE NOW COMPETING TO SEND PEOPLE AND EQUIPMENT
AS WELL.
3.  THIS WHOLE PROGRAM STARTED SLOWLY, WITH SMALL NUMBERS OF
LEBANESE CHRISTIANS CROSSING FOR MEDICAL TREATMENT, BUT
SOON MUSLIMS WERE ASKING IF ISRAEL WAS DISCRIMINATING AGAINST
THEM.  CHRISTIANS AND MUSLIMS NOW CROSSING IN INCREASING
NUMBERS.  PERES CLAIMED THAT NOW FATAH SUPPORTERS ARE ALSO
CROSSING FOR TREATMENT.  DECISION TO PUBLICIZE THIS
PROGRAM RESULTED FROM REQUEST OF LEBANESE PEOPLE INVOLVED.
4.  TRAFFIC IS  NOT RESTRICTED TO MEDICAL PATIENTS, ACCORDING
TO PERES.  LEBANESE ARE BUYING FOOD FROM ISRAELIS AND
ISRAELIS ARE BUYING TOBACCO FROM LEBANESE FARMERS.  IN
RESPONSE TO A REQUEST FROM THE LEBANESE PEOPLE, THE IDF HAS
LAID A WATER PIPELINE INTO SOUTHERN LEBANON AND IS PUMPING
ISRAELI WATER TO THAT AREA.  LEBANESE PEOPLE REQUESTED ON JULY 5
THAT ISRAEL OPEN A "SUPERMARKET" ON THE BORDER, WHICH PERES SAID
ISRAEL IS PREPARED TO DO.
5.  MOST STRIKING POINT WAS PERES' ASSERTION THAT A LEBANESE
VILLAGE (POPULATION 6,000 CHRISTIANS) SENT A RESOLUTION TO
THE GOI, REQUESTING THAT IT BE ANNEXED BY ISRAEL.  PERES
LAUGHINGLY SAID THAT GOI'S ANSWER WAS "WE'VE GOT ENOUGH
PROBLEMS WITH THE U.S. WITHOUT BITING OFF THIS ONE."
TOON



*******************


 * 309226 1976TELAV04652 0.007088719 | 1976-07-07 | TEL AVIV | STATE | MINDEF PERES VIEWS ON SFM
1.  AMBASSADOR TOON AND SFM DIRECTOR KONTOS CALLED ON MINDEF
PERES ON JULY 6.  AFTER AN EXCHANGE OF PLEASANTRIES, PERES
HEAPED PRAISE ON THE SINAI FIELD MISSION.  IN HIS VIEW, NO
OTHER ONE SINGLE ELEMENT OF THE SINAI II AGREEMENT HAD DONE
AS MUCH AS THE SFM TO REDUCE TENSIONS IN THE SINAI.  HE FELT
THAT INTERPOSITION OF U.S. PERSONNEL WAS AN IMPORTANT PERCEDENT
AND HE SPECULATED THAT IT COULD SERVE AS USEFUL MODEL FOR
SIMILAR FUTURE ARRANGEMENT BETWEEN ISRAELI AND SYRIAN FORCES
ON THE GOLAN AND PERHAPS BETWEEN ISRAELI AND JORDANIAN
FORCES AS WELL.  PERES STRESSED THAT ONE IMPORTANT ADVANTAGE
OF U.S. PRESENCE IS THAT IT AVOIDS SEMI-ANNUAL TRAUMA
ASSOCIATED WITH RENEWALS OF U.N. MANDATES.
2.  PERES ADMITTED THAT IT WAS LARGELY AT HIS INSISTENCE
THAT THE ISSUE OF U.S. TECHNICIANS WAS INCLUDED IN SINAI
II.  HE ASSERTED THAT WHEN AGREEMENT WAS SIGNED, HE WAS
VIEWED BY HIS COLLEAGUES AS THE FATHER OF A VERY UNWELCOME
BABY, BUT CLAIMS THAT MOST CRITICS HAVE NOW COME AROUND
AND APPRECIATE THE VALUE OF THE SFM.
3.  IN CLOSING, PERES REFERRED TO AN OPINION POLL CONDUCTED
BY THE 1976 NATIONAL CONFERENCE ON GREAT DECISIONS IN
UNITED STATES FOREIGN POLICY.  POLL, TABULATED AS OF
APRIL 20, 1976, RESULTED IN 6,571 BALLOTS.  ON QUESTION OF
U.S. TECHNICIANS IN SINAI. 4,450 WERE IN FAVOR, 1,401 AGAINST
AND 720 NO OPINION.  PERES SEEMED SURPRISED, ALBEIT
PLEASED, AT THIS OVERWHELMING PUBLIC SUPPORT FOR THE
CONCEPT OF THE SFM.
TOON

 * 170765 1976PORTL00581 0.007087834 | 1976-07-05 | PORT LOUIS | STATE | AIR FRANCE HIJACKING
(C) STATE 166419 (NOTAL)
1. PRESIDENT AMIN LEFT MAURITIUS ABOUT 1500 HOURS LOCAL
JULY 3 TO RETURN TO UGANDA, PRESUMABLY DIRECT. HE FLEW IN
HIS GRUMMAN GULFSTREAM II EXECUTIVE JET.
2. IN VIEW OF JULY 4 RADIO NEWS OF SUCCESSFUL ISRAELI RESCUE
OPERATION, DID NOT CARRY OUT INSTRUCTIONS REFTEL (C) RE
AMCITS HELD AT ENTEBEE.
3. NEWS FROM ENTEBBE APPARENTLY PREEMPTED OTHER CONCERNS
AT OAU SUMMIT SESSIONS JULY 4. IN PRIVATE CONVERSATIONS AT
RAMGOOLAM'S RECEPTION FOR SUMMIT ATTENDEES JULY 4 NUMBER OF
DELEGATES WERE HIGHLY CRITICAL OF KENYA'S "COOPERATION"
WITH ISRAELIS. MOST OF DELEGATION LEADERS INCLUDED REFERENCES
TO ENTEBBE EVENTS IN THEIR SPEECHES AT SUMMIT SESSIONS THROUGH-
OUT DAY. ACCORDING TO DELEGATES I TALKED WITH, NO SPEAKER
MADE DIRECT MENTION OF KENYA BUT THERE WERE CLEAR AND CRITICAL
ALLUSIONS TO KENYA'S ROLE. KENYAN REPRESENTATIVES WERE UNABLE
TO REPLY AS THEY LACKED FACTS. SENGHOR, SENIOR MODERATE
LEADER AT SUMMIT CONFERENCE, INTRODUCED RESOLUTION WHICH WAS
ADOPTED AND WHICH WAS IN NATURE OF "CONDOLENCE"MESSAGE TO
AMIN.
4. MAURITIAN UN PERMREP RAMPHUL TOLD ME THAT UNSYG WALDHEIM,
WHO DEPARTED MAURITIUS VIA LUFTHANSA EARLY EVENING JULY 4,
WOULD MAKE STOPOVER IN NAIROBI "TO LOOK INTO SITUATION THERE
AND REPORT BACK TO OAU CONFERENCE WHAT HE FINDS OUT."
EARLIER IN DAY WALDHEIM TOLD ME HE WOULD FLY DIRECT TO EUROPE,
BUT HE MAY HAVE CHANGED HIS PLANS.
KEELEY
NOTE BY OC/T:  DISTRIBUTION PER S/S-O, MR. HOGANSON.

YOUR INTEREST IN AND SUPPORT OF COLONEL TOKO.  TOKO WAS
SUMMONED TO ARUSHA (EAST AFRICAN COMMUNITY HEADQUARTERS)
THIS MORNING.  ON HIS RETURN TO NAIROBI HE ADVISED ME THAT

FOR DISMISSAL BY AMIN: "ON POLITICAL GROUNDS AS HAVING
BEEN IMPLICATED IN RECENT ISRAELI ACTION IN ENTEBBE."

 * 23604 1976BEIRUT05872 0.007086595 | 1976-07-05 | BEIRUT | STATE INFO SIT-REP COLLECTIVE | LEBANESE SITUATION JULY 5: ARAB LEAGUE EFFORTS TAKE ON NEW
1. SUMMARY: AFTER UNINSPIRING START OF ARAB LEAGUE MEDIATION
EFFORT WITH UNSUCCESSFUL CEASEFIRE "AGREEMENT" (SITREP JULY 4),
BEIRUT SURPRISED BY MEETING JULY 4 AT SOFAR UNDER AL AUSPICES,
BRINGING TOGETHER MOST MAJOR PARTIES TO CONFLICT. SECOND
MEETING EXPECTED JULY 5. DE FACTO PARTITION NOW WELL ATO TED
AS KATAEB ADMINISTRATIE APPARATUS IN EAST BEIRUT FUNCTIONS AS
LOCAL GOVERNMENT IN EVERYTHING BUT NAME. TELL ZAATAR REMAINS
TENSE, BUT CHRISTIANS IN CONTROL OF ALL BUT POCKETS OF
RESISTANCE. FIGHTING ELSEWHERE
INDECISIVE. ISRAELI MILITARY SUPPLY OF CHRISTIAN SIDE NOW
BEING MORE OPENLY DISCUSSED. END SUMMARY.
2. NEWSPAPERS HEADLINE JULY 4 SURPRISE MEETING AT SOFARJOINING
SECGEN MAHMOUD RIAD AT HEAD OF AL MEDIATION TEAM,
SYRIAN FOREIGN MINISTER ABDEL HALIM KHADDAM, AND REPRESENTATIVES
OF BOTH PALESTINIAN RESISTANCE AND RIGHTIST LEBANESE FRONT. AL
GROUP ORIGINALLY SCHEDULED RETURN CAIRO JULY 4 BUT INSTEAD CAME
DIRECTLY FROM DAMASCUS AFTER MEETING WITH LIBYAN PREMIER
JALLOUD, WHO EVIDENTLY CONTINUES HIS SOMEWHAT ISOLATED MEDIATION
EFFORTS THERE. RADIO SILENCE ON MEETING GUARDED BY STATIONS OF
ALL PARTIES, BUT IT APPEARS TO HAV BEEN ATTENDED ALSO BY YASIR
ARAFAT WHO HAD RETURNED TO LEBANON BY SEA THROUGH SIDON ON
JULY 3 AND HAS SINCE MET WITH HIGH-LEVEL PALESTINIANS AND KAMAL
JUNBLATT. KATAEB POLITBURO MEMBER KARIM PAKRADOUNI, IN SYRIA
EARLIER JULY FOR CONSULTATION WITH PRESIDENT ASSAD, MADE IT BACK
TO SOFAR IN TIME. MEETING SAID TO BE PRELIMINARY TO POLITICAL
TALKS AMONG LEBANESE LEFT AN RIGHT, PALESTINIANS, AND SYRIANS.
SECOND MEETING SCHEDULED FOR JULY 5. CHRISTIANS REPORTEDLY
SAYING REALLPOLITICAL DIALOGUE ONLY POSSIBLE IF CAIRO ACCORDS
ADHERED TO AND PALESTINIANS SAYING THERE CAN BE NO DIALOGUE
UNTIL ATTACK ON TELL ZAATAR STOPS.  LEBANESE LEFT SHOWS SIGNS
OF DISSATISFACTION OVER ITS NON-REPRESENTATION AT
JULY 4 MEETING WHICH REPORTEDLY DISCUSSED TELL ZAATAR AS
MOST IMMEDIATE PROBLEM. ON SECONDARY LEVEL, AL DEPUTY
SECGEN KHOLI AND PEACEKEEPING FORCE CHIEF OF STATE COL.
CHEDID MET PIERRE GEMAYEL WHO RENEWED HIS DEM JRTTOGAT
PALESTINIANS RETURN TO THEIR OWN NATIONAL OBJECTIVE
AND BE RESETTLED IN OTHER ARAB COUNTRIES.
3. FROM LATE REPORT JULY 5 WE UNDERSTAND AL HOPES TO ORGANIZE
CEASEFIRE AT TELL ZAATAR TODAY, BUT THIS IS REPORTEDLY
JEOPARDIZED BY MID-MORNING JULY 5 REPORTS OF PALESTINIAN ATTACK
ON CHEKKA, COASTAL VILLAGE AT NORTHERN END OF CHRISTIAN-DOMINATED
TERRITORY SOUTH OF TRIPOLI.
4. CHRISTIANS IN WEST BEIRUT INCREASINGLY DISTURBED OVER
CONTINUED SIGNS OF DE FACTO PARTITION. RAYMOND EDDE ADDRESSEES
YET ANOTHER LIST OF RHETORICAL QUESTIONS, THIS TIME TO
MARONITE "KFOUR FRONT," SAYING CHRISTIANS DARE NOT ANSWER
ACCUSATIONS ON THEIR PARTITION PLANS. DAR AL-AMAL ORGANIZATION
SET UP BY KATAEB SEVERAL MONTHS AGO TO PROVIDE ADMINISTRATIVE
CONTROL OF CHRISTIAN HELD AREAS STILL NOT CALLED A GOVERNMENT,
BUT EAST BEIRUT SECURITY AND ADMINISTRATIVE APPARATUS FAR MORE
DEVELOPED THAN IN WEST BEIRUT. BRANCHES FOR HEALTH, EDUCATION,
TAXATION, ETC., OPERATING AND LEBANESE IN RIGHTIST-CONTROLLED
AREAS SPEAKING OPENLY OF "DECENTRALIZATION" AND
"REGIONALIZATION," IF NOT YET OF EXPLOSIVE TERM "PARTITION."
5. FR TUTOJS "CONSTITUTIONAL DOCUMENT" OF FEBRUARY 14 ONCE AGAIN
UNDER ATTACK, THIS TIME BY "ASSOCIATION OF THE ANCIENTS OF
MAKASSED" WHICH CALLS DOCUMENT " AN AMALGAM OF CONTRADICTORY
IDEAS." GROUP SAYS DOCUMENT IS INAPPLICABLE AND FRANGIE
COMMITTED NEW ERROR WHEN HE MADE IT BASIS HIS RECENT MESSAGE
TO AL.
6. FIGHTING AT TELL ZAATAR IS VIRTUALLY OVER WITH FINAL REDOUBT
TAKEN AND ONLY POCKETS OF RESISTANCE REMAINING. WE UNDERSTAND
THAT MAJORITY REMAINING DEFENDERS HAVE SURRENDERED. RED
CROSS, ON REQUEST OF BOTH SIDES,
HAS UNDERTAKEN EVACUATION OF WOUNDED AND WE UNDERSTAND
SOME 200 PALESTINIAN WOUNDED BROUGHT OUT OF TELL ZAATAR AND
DELIVERED TO RED CROSS ON JULY 3 AND 4. PALESTINIANS CLAIM AL
DEPUTY SECGEN HASSAN KHOLI HAD ARRANGED WITH RED CROSS FOR
TRANSPORT OF PALESTINIAN PRISONERS TO MUSEUM SECTOR FROM WHERE
THEY CAN REACH SABRA QAMP, BUT RIGHTIST MUTE ON SUBJECT.
WESTERN EYEITNESS WHO TOOK CONSIDERABLE RISK OF CROSSING
"GREEN LINE" FROM RIGHTIST SIDE SAYS IT DOUBTFUL RIGHTISTS HAVE
SUFFERED MORE THAN 100 CASUALTIES IN ENTIRE TELL ZAATAR BATTLE.
(YESTERDAY AL REPRESENTATIVE, SABRI AL-KHOULI, WAS SHOT AT WHILE
CROSSING HERE.) EYEWITNESS SAYS CAMP TOTALLY SURROUNDED FOR LAST
FEW DAYS AND CHRISTIANS DID NOT NEED MAKE FINAL ASSAULT AS CAMP
COMPLETELY CUT OFF AND CHRISTIANS DOMINATED CAMP FROM TALAT EL MIR.
KATAEB LEADERSHIP SAYING IT PLANS CLEAN OUT NABAA NEXT, AND
MANY SHIITE INHABITANTS REPORTED LEAVING AREA. NABAA IS UNDER
CONTROL OF LEFTIST AND PALESTINIAN ELEMENTS, AND IS LAST
REMAINING NON-CHRISTIAN ENCLAVE IN EAST BEIRUT.
7. IN BEIRUT AREA, KATAEB SAYS INFILTRATION EFFORTS OF
"PALESTINIANS AND THEIR MERCENARIES" HAVE BEEN REPULSED ALONG
CENTER CITY CONFRONTATION LINE. ACHRAFIYYAH STILL UNDER
BOMBARDMENTS FROM NABAA AND FIREFIGHTS CONTINUE ALONG
BECHARA EL-KHOURY AXIS. VILLENT FIGHTING CONTINUES IN ALEY
DISTRICT ON THE ROAD TO ARAY AND KAHALE. LEFTIST CLAIM TO
HAVE TAKEN VILLAGE OF ARAYA IS APPARENTLY FALSE. VILLAGE OF
BSOUSS AND KAHALE ALSO INVOLVED IN FIGHTING. CONTRARY TO
PREVIOUS REPORTS, HUGE FIRE OF NIGHT JULY 3 AND 4 WAS NOT AT
TELL ZAATAR BUT WAS BURNING OF WOODS AROUND ARAYA. VOICE OF
PALESTININE ANNOUCNES ANOTHER LARGE FOREST FIRE NEAR JDAIDE
FOLLOWING PALESTINIAN BOMBARDMENT OF SABTIE.
8. ELSEWHERE, LEFTIST SOURCES CLAIM SYRIAN ARMY ATTACKED
JOINT PALESTINIAN/LEFTIST GROUPS JULY 4 IN BEKAA. LEFTISTS
MAKE UNSUBSTANTIATED AND PROBABLY FALSE CLAIM THEY HAVE
DESTROYED SYRIAN ARMY HEADQUARTERS AT RAYAK. SYRIAN
BLOCKADES OF BAALBECK AND HERMEL CONTINUE. BOMBARDMENTS
CONTINUE BUT THERE IS NO GROUND ACTION IN NORTH METN OR AT
OUYOUN EL SIMANE. IN NORTH LEBANON, MUTUAL BOMBARDMENTS
CONTINUE BETWEEN TRIPOI AND ZGHORTA AND SOME FIGHTING
CONTINUES IN KOURA DISTRICT. DATE REORT OF BATTLE AT CHEKKA, OTED
ABOVE, INDICATES NORTH MAY BECOME CENTER OF STRIFE IN COMING DAYS.
9. SAEB SALAM FOLLOWED UP JULY 3 STATEMENT BY FATAH NO. 2
SALAH KHALAF ON ISRAELI MILITARY SUPPORT TO RIGHTISTS. SALAM
SAID NOT ONLY HAVE ISRAELIS SENT 40 TANKS TO JOUNIEH, BUT
NATIONAL LIBERAL PARTY AND ITS ALLIES HAVE ON SVERAL OCCASIONS
RECEIVED ARMS AND FUNDS FROM ISRAEL VIA CERTAIN LEBANOESE
AMBASSADORS IN EUROPE. AMIN GEMAYEL ALSO REACTED TO KHALAF
STATEMENT, SAYING IT IS "LIE" THAT HE ONCE TOLD KHALAF THAT
WHERAS HE HAD REFUSED ISRAELI MILITARY AID, CAMILLE CHAMOUN
HAD ACCEPTED IT. FOREIGNER WHO VISITED RIGHTIST HELD AREAS
SAYS CHRISTIAN FIGHTERS MAKING NO BONES ABOUT CARRYING
ISRAELI-SUPPLIED WEAPONS THOUGH SOME
WEAPONS HAVE SERIAL NUMBERS FILED OFF.

 * 23583 1976BEIRUT05822 0.007086108 | 1976-07-03 | BEIRUT | STATE | TALK WITH JUMBLATT JULY 1 SUMMARY: JUMBLATT SPOKE FOR ALMOST 2 HOURS  WITH ME ON WIDE
SUMMARY: JUMBLATT SPOKE FOR ALMOST 2 HOURS WITH ME ON WIDE
RANGE OF SUBJECTS. HE OUTLINED THE "SINS" OF THE CHRISTIANS AND
THE NEED TO REALIZE HOW MUCH THEY HAD TO LOSE IN SPECIFIC TERMS
FROM THEIR CURRENT ALLIANCE WITH THE SYRIANS.  HE ATTACKED
SYRIAN POLICY AND THOUGHT THE FIRST STEP IS THAT SYRIANS GET OUT
BEFORE A ROUND TABLE DISCUSSION CAN PROCEED.  HE WAS
GENERALLY OPTIMISTIC ABOUT CHANCES OF ENDING THE FIGHTING IN THE
NEAR FUTURE (THOUGH GIVING NO SPECIFIC EVIDENCE OF THIS BEYOND
THE GENERAL FEELING THAT "PEOPLE NEED A REST"), AND SAID TIME HAD
COME FOR COMPROMISE. HOWEVER, ROUND TABLE DISCUSSIONS MUST
BE CAREFULLY PREPARED, AND GAVE AS AN EXAMPLE TALKS HE AND THE
PALESTINIANS HAVE HAD WITH BASHIR GEMAYEL, SON OF PIERRE
GEMAYEL. HE OUTLINED SOME REFORMS, INCLUDING PROPORTIONAL
REPRESENTATION AND DE-CONFESSIONALIZATION OF THE STATE, AS
EXAMPLES OVER WHICH COMPROMISE CAN BE REACHED. THOUGH
RESTED AND SPEAKING IN REASONABLE TERMS, HE WAS NOT VERY
CONVINCING THAT PEACE IS AROUND THE CORNER.  END SUMMARY.
1.  I TOOK LAMBRADIS WITH ME TO CALL ON JUMBLATT JULY 1.  HE
LOOKED RESTED AFTER SOMETIME IN HIS MOUNTAIN RETREAT, WHERE
HE WAS NOT VERY INVOLVED WITH CURRENT POLITICS OVER THE PAST
WEEK OR SO.  HE WAS WELL-DRESSED, HAD A NEAT HAIRCUT, AND
GENERALLY PRESENTED A VERY RELAXED IMAGE AS HE OFFERED US
FRUIT AND DEVOURED IT HIMSELF, AS IS HIS AFTERNOON HABIT.
2.  NOTING THAT HE HAD NEVER MET AMBASSADOR MELOY
PERSONALLY, HE BEGAN WITH EXPRESSIONS OF PERSONAL SORROW AT
THE DEATH OF ROBERT WARING.  HE HAD CONSIDERED HIM AN
HONEST FRIEND AND HAD NOTED THINGS HE HAD DISCUSSED WITH
WARING WERE LISTENED TO IN WASHINGTON, SINCE HE HAD SEEN
PLAYBACKS OF THEM A FEW DAYS LATER IN PUBLIC ANNOUNCEMENTS
OR PRESS REPORTS.  WHEN ASKED FOR HIS CURRENT BEST
ESTIMATE OF WHO THE MURDERERS WERE, JUMBLATT SAID HE
THOUGHT THE MURDERS HAD BEEN ORDERED BY DR. HADDAD, WHO
IS GEORGE HABASH'S DEPUTY IN THE PFLP.  HE SAID HE HAD
NOT BEEN IN TOUCH MORE RECENTLY WITH SPECIFICS OF THE
INVESTIGATION, BUT WOULD LOOK INTO IT FOR US.  I PRESSED HIM
ON THIS SCORE, AND HE SEEMED COMPLETELY WILLING TO DO WHAT
HE COULD.  HE NOTED HIS OWN SISTER'S DEATH AND THE WOUNDING
OF HIS NIECES.  SUCH PERSONAL GRIEF HELPS ONE APPRECIATE
THE GRIEF OF OTHERS, HE SAID.
3.  I EXPLAINED MY MISSION TO THE LEBANON, AND NOTED THAT IN
EARLIER CONVERSATIONS SINCE MY ARRIVAL CERTAIN SUGGESTIONS HAD
COME UP ON WHICH I HAD CONSISTENTLY TRIED TO SET THE RECORD
STRAIGHT.  I HAVE BEEN POINTING OUT THAT THE US IS AGAINST
LEBANESE PARTITION.  I HAVE MADE A POINT OF MENTIONING UNITY
OF LEBANON IN MY PUBLIC UTTERANCES.  I ALSO HAVE TRIED TO DEBUNK
LIES SUGGESTING THERE IS A SYRIAN-ISRAELI-CHRISTIAN-USG
CONSPIRACY TO SUPPRESS THE PALESTINIAN AND THE LEFT IN LEBANON.
I NOTED THAT THE PRESS AND RADIO NEVERTHELESS CONTINUED TO INSIST
ON THIS THEME DESPITE ANYTHING THE USG OR I CAN SAY.  JUMBLATT
NODDED HIS UNDERSTANDING.
4.  JUMBLATT ADVERTED INDIRECTLY TO US-SYRIAN COLLUSION.  HE
SAID HE BELIEVED US WHEN WE SAY WE ARE AGAINST PARTITION.
HOWEVER, US USED TO BE VERY STRICT ON QUESTION OF THE
INDEPENDENCE OF LEBANON.  THIS CAME UP IN 1958 EVEN IN
CONNECTION WITH US FACILITATING THE ELECTION OF GENERAL CHEHAB.
ISRAEL HAD BEEN WELL AWARE OVER THE YEARS OF US SUPPORT FOR
LEBANESE INDEPENDENCE.  HOWEVER, THERE HAVE BEEN SOME
CURIOUS EVENTS RECENTLY IN SYRIA.  ASSAD HAS "TURNED COSSACK"
AGAINST THE SOVIETS.  HE HAS RENEWED UNDOF MANDATE ON
GOLAN HEIGHTS WITHOUT ANY FUSS.  ONE CANNOT ESCAPE THE
CONCLUSION THAT US PERMISSION HAS BEEN GIVEN TO SYRIANS TOH
TO VERY FAR INDEED.  EVERYONE BELIEVES THIS, AND JUMBLATT
HAD TOLD THIS TO AMBASSADOR BROWNN WHO HE SAID OF COURSE
DENIED IT.  ONE CANNOT IMAGINE THE SYRIANS WOULD DARE ALLOW
THEIR TROOPS TO ENTER LEBANON WITHOUT SOME KIND OF US
GO-AHEAD. THIS IS A "PLOT" OF WHICH EDDE HAS BEEN TALKING
FOR A YEAR AND A HALF.
6.  JUMBLATT SAID HE BELIEVED SECRETARY KISSINGER HAS A
METHOD WHICH JUMBALTT ADMIRES IN ITS TACTICAL EFFICACY.  IT LETS
PEOPLE FIGHT EACH OTHER UNTIL THEY ARE TIRED AND THEN KISSINGER
STEPS IN WITH A SOLUTION.  BUT US SHOULD BE CAREFUL NOT TO LOSE
ITS FRIENDS IN THE LEBANON.  A SOCIALIST STATE MIGHT RISE IN THE
LEBANON OVER THE NEXT 2 TO 4 YEARS. (IN REPLY TO MY QUESTION,
JUMBLATT INSISTED HE WAS SPEAKING ABOUT A SOCIALIST STATE, NOT
A COMMUNIST.)
7.  SOCIAL REFORM HAD BECOME NECESSARY TO COUNTER MARONITE
PRIVILEGE, WHICH IS EXERCISED IN TERMS REMINISCENT OF THE
MIDDLE AGES.  FIVE PROPRIETORS OWN MOST OF THE BEKAA.  THERE
ARE UNCULTIVATED LANDS GOING TO WASTE WHILE HUNDREDS AND
THOUSANDS ARE MISERABLE IN THEIR POVERTY.  THE COUNTRY NEEDS
TRUE DEMOCRACY.  PROGRESSIVE FORCES WHICH JUMBLATT LEADS
BELIEVE IN LIBERTY.  THEY DO NOT BELIEVE IN COMMUNISM, NOR
CLASS WARFARE, OR IN COUPS D'ETAT.  HE CLAIMED ALONG THAT
LINE TO HAVE PREVENTED GENERAL AHDAB FROM MARCHING AGAINST
FRANGIE WHEN FRANGIE DID NOT RESIGN IN MARCH.  THIS WAS NOT
THE DEMOCRATIC WAY, JUMBLATT SAID.  (AS WE RECALL IT,
JUMBLATT'S GROUP MAY HAVE HAD A PART IN THIS, BUT IT IS FAR
FROM CLEAR THAT HE ALONE PREVENTED AHDAB FROM MARCHING.)
8.  THE MARONITES MUST UNDERSTAND THAT OPPOSITION TO THEM CAN
CONTINUE FOR YEARS IF THEY DO NOT YIELD.  JUMBLATT IS PREPARED
TO DISCUSS THINGS OVER THE ROUND TABLE, BUT NOT TO CONTINUE
ACCEPTING MARONITE MASTERY OF THE COUNTRY.  MARONITES HAVE
SEVERAL SPECIFIC THINGS THEY SHOULD THINK ABOUT: FIRST, IT IS
NOT CLEAR HOW FAR COMMUNISTS MIGHT GO IN LEBANON.
JUMBLATT SAID HE DID NOT LIKE THE COMMUNISTS HIMSELF (AND IN
FACT EXPECTS GREATER DEMOCRATIZATION IN THE SOVIET UNION BY
ABOUT 1985).  HOWEVER, MARONITES SHOULD FEAR COMMUNIST
TREND IN LEBANON IF CONDITIONS ON WHICH THEY BREED ARE NOT
CHANGED.  SECOND, MARONITES SHOULD FEAR EMIGRATION OF THEIR
OWN PEOPLE IF THEY MAINTAIN CURRENT SEPARATENESS BEHIND
THEIR GUNS.  JUMBLATT WAS TOLD 80 PERCENT OF DOCTORS HAVE
ALREADY FLED THE COUNTRY.  THESE STUBBORN
MARONITES MAY SOME DAY FIND THEIR NUMBERS
SO REDUCED THAT THEY WILL BE FACED BY A CRUSHING
MAJORITY OF ISLAM.  THIRD, MARONITES SHOULD FEAR SYRIA.
SOME SUCH AS BASHIR GEMAYEL WISELY OPPOSED SYRIAN
INTERVENTION FOR THIS REASON; OTHERS -- PARTICULARLY THE
MONKS AND CLERICS OF THE CATHOLIC FRONT -- MAINTAIN THEIR
HOPES FOR A NEW CRUSADE.  SYRIANS BELIEVE THEY HAVE A CHANCE
TO REPLACE MOTHER FRANCE AS PROTECTOR OF LEBANON, AND IN
PARTICULAR THE MARONITES.  BUT ONE DAY THERE COULD BE A CHANGE
OF REGIME IN SYRIA WITH SUNNIS OVERTHROWING THE REGIME AND
LIVING UP THEIR FORCES IN LEBANON WITH THE LEFT.  TOP
CHRISTIAN LEADERS SHOULD REALIZE THIS.  (COMMENTING
SPECIFICALLY ON GEMAYEL, JUMBLATT SAID HE SUFFERED FROM
HALLUCINATIONS AND HAD NO INTELLECTUAL BAGGAGE.  CLINICALLY HIS
FATHER HAD SUFFERED FROM HALLUCINATIONS.)
9.  FINALLY, CHRISTIANS SHOULD REALIZE FORTUNE THEY MADE IN
THE PAST WAS BASED ON EXPLOITATION OF ARAB OIL AND SERVICES TO
OTHER ARAB COUNTRIES.  MARONITES HAVE LOST MUCH OF THIS
MONEY (HE SPOKE OF 50,000 LEBANESE IN FRANCE, MANY OF
THEM IN FINANCIAL NEED AT PRESENT).  MARONITES MUST REALIZE
THAT THESE ARAB STATES WILL TURN AGAINST EHEM AND ISOLATE
THEM IF THEY CONTINUE TO BEHAVE AS THEY DO.  JUMBLATT
HIMSELF HAD TO INTERVENE SOME MONTHS AGO FOR FRIENDS WHO WERE
ABOUT TO BE EXPELLED FROM LIBYA AND KUWAIT.
FM AMEMBASSY BEIRUT

INFO AMEMBASSY CAIRO
AMEMBASSY DAMASCUS
AMEMBASSY AMMAN

AMEMBASSY TEL AVIV
AMEMBASSY KUWAIT
AMEMBASSY PARIS
AMEMBASSY LONDON
C O N F I D E N T I A L SECTION 2 OF 2 BEIRUT 5822
10.  TROUBLE WITH MARONITES, JUMBLATT SUMMED UP, IS THAT THEY
ARE OBSESSED BY FEAR.  SARKIS MAY TURN OUT TO BE THE LAST
MARONITE PRESIDENT OF LEBANON.  THEY MADE A BIG MISTAKE IN
CURRENT ATTACK ON TELL ZAATAR, WHICH HE WAS SORRY TO SEE
BASHIR GEMAYEL ALSO JOINED IN ON FINALLY.  MUSLIMS COULD HAVE
DONE NASTY THINGS TO CHRISTIAN VILLAGES SUCH AS DEIR EL-QAMAR
(IN THE CHOUF), BUT THEY WOULD NOT.  NOR WOULD MUSLIMS ATTACK
CHRISTIANS IN RAS BEIRUT, AS MANY SEEMED TO FEAR.  MARONITES
MUST HAVE CONFIDENCE IN DEMOCRACY AND ACCEPT WESTERNIZING
THE COUNTRY INSTITUTIONS.  BY THIS HE MEANT REFORMS TO SUPPRESS
SECTARIANISM AND ESTABLISH GOVERNMENT ON MODERN PRINCIPLES.
11.  I ASKED HIM IF HE HAD NOT ACCEPTED THE COMPROMISE AGREEMENT
ANNOUNCED LAST FEBRUARY BY FRANGIE.  JUMBLATT SAID THOSE POINTS
HAD BEEN ACCEPTABLE THEN, BUT CHRISTIANS HAD REJECTED THEM, AND
SITUATION HAS CHANGED.  THE LEFT ALLIANCES PARTIES WILL NO LONGER
ACCEPT THEM.  IN THIS SENSE MARONITES ARE ARABS, AND HAVE BEEN
ACTING AS ARABS HAVE ACTED HISTORICALLY TOWARDS ISRAEL --
THEY ACCEPT NOTHING UNTIL IT IS TOO LATE.
12.  COURSE AHEAD, JUMBLATT SAID, MUST BE TO PREPARE A
COMPROMISE AGREEMENT.  THIS MUST BE PRECEDED BY NEGOTIATIONS
THROUGH QUIET OR PUBLIC CONTACTS BETWEEN THE SIDES, BEFORE FINAL
AGREEMENT IS BROUGHT TO A ROUND TABLE AND SANCTIONED THERE.
THEN THERE SHOULD BE A NEW PARLIAMENTARY ELECTION ACCORDING
TO THE NEW PRINCIPLES AGREED UPON.  WHEN ASKED TO SPECIFY
REFORMS HE WANTED, HE MENTIONED PROPORTIONAL REPRESENTATION
IN PARLIAMENT WITH THE OBJECTIVE OF GETTING MORE YOUNG PEOPLE
IN.  HOWEVER, THIS SHOULD BE LIMITED TO NO MORE THAN THREE
PARTIES BEING ELECTED, AND LIST SHOULD PERMIT VOTERS TO EXPRESS
INDIVIDUAL PREFERENCES FOR PEOPLE ON THE LIST.  A SECOND CHAMBER
SHOULD BE CREATED IN ACCORDANCE WITH HIS WELL-PUBLICIZED
PROGRAM.  OBJECTIVE IS TO ABOLISH CONFESSIONALISM AND
ELEIMINATE MEDIOCRITY IN PARLIAMENT.  I ASKED IF HE MEANT
ELIMINATING FEUDAL REMNANTS.  NO, JUMBLATT INSISTED, HE MEANT
ELIMINATING MEDIOCRITY. (COMMENT: JUMBLATT OF COURSE
DERIVES HIS MOST STEADY SUPPORT FROM HIS TRADITIONAL FEUDAL
SUZERAINTY OVER MUCH OF THE DRUZE COMMUNITY).
13.  PHALANGE (PROBABLY BASHIR GEMAYEL) HAS ACCEPTED
PROPORTIONAL REPRESENTATION, JUMBLATT ASSERTED, BUT NOT
AN END TO CONFESSIONALISM.  JUMBLATT THOUGH PARTIES OF THE
LEFT CAN IMPOSE ON OTHER, MORE CONSERVATIVE MUSLIMS A REFORM
PROGRAM WHICH WOULD, FOR EXAMPLE, PERMIT CIVIL MARRIAGE AND
SIMILAR CHANGES WHICH MANY CHRISTIANS SUPPORT.  YOUNG
PEOPLE, BOTH CHRISTIAN AND MUSLIM, ARE IDEALISTIC.  THEY WILL
INSIST ON TOUGH REFORMS.  THERE IS LITTLE DIFFERNENCE BETWEEN
THESE YOUNG PEOPLE, EXCEPT THAT THE CHRISTIAN YOUTH DO NOT
UNDERSTAND THE PALESTINIANS AND HOW TO HANDLE THEM.
MEANWHILE, COMPETITION AMONG TRADITIONAL CHRISTIAN LEADDERS
SUCH AS CHAMOUN AND GEMAYEL LENDS TO ESCALATION OF RHETORIC
AND MILITARY ACTION FOR NO GOOD REASON.  THIS SHOULD END.
14.  AS TO PALESTINIANS, ELIMINATION OF SAIQA HAS BEEN A GOOD
THING.  OF COURSE SOME GROUPS SUCH AS PFLP RESORT
INOPPORTUNELY TO TERRORISM (HERE JUMBLATT SHOWED HE DID
NOT APPROVE RECENT AIR FRANCE HIJACKING).  THERE ARE ALSO
TROUBLE-MAKING SMALL GROUPS BACKED BY LIBYANS AND IRAQIS
AS WELL AS SYRIANS.  HOWEVER, WITH SAIQA DISAPPEARANCE,
PALESTINIANS CAN NOW IMPOSE THEIR OWN LAW AMONG MOST OF
THEIR PEOPLE.  LEBANESE MUST LEARN HOW TO DEAL WITH
PALESTINIANS, OFFER THEM A BETTER LIFE.  THIS IS AN IMPORTANT
PEOPLE NUMBERING THREE MILLION THROUGHOUT THE WORLD.  THEY DO
NOT WANT TO LIVE HERE ONLY AS AN ARMY.  IN THIS SENSE, JUMBLATT
SAID HE HAD NO FEAR FOR THE FUTURE OF THE COUNTRY.  PEOPLE MAY
EVEN HAVE BENEFITED FROM THEIR EXORCISM OF BLOOD....
15.  SPECIFICALLY, JUMBLATT SAID, 1969 DAIRO ACCORD IS OUT OF
DATE,  BUT MODUS VIVENDI CAN BE REACHED WITH PALESTINIANS.  HE
NOTED THAT PALESTINIANS REMAIN IN TOUCH WITH CHRISTIANS THROUGH
ABU HASSAN WHO GOES BACK AND FORTH ACROSS THE DIVIDING LINE,
AS DOES PHALANGE'S BAYIR GEMAYEL.  HE THEN MADE SOME
REMARKS ABOUT A VIABLE PALESTINIAN STATE TO INCLUDE JORDAN,
AND THE 1,200,000 PALESTINIANS HAVING A COANCE TO RETURN TO
THEIR HOMES IN HAIFA, ETC. ETC. (JUMBLATT IS CLEARLY BEYOND
HIS DEPTH OR INTEREST WHEN HE STARTS TALKING ABOUT THE LARGER
PALESTINIAN PROBLEM).
16.  SPECIFICALLY ON SYRIANS, JUMBLATT SAID THAT THEY MUST LEAVE
AS SOON AS POSSIBLE.  ALL MUSLIMS ARE AGAINST THEM.  ASSAD IS
A MEDIOCRE MAN WHO HAS REPEATEDLY REFUSED TO TAKE
OPPORTUNITIES TO GET OUT OF THE LEBANON.  AS TO REASONS FOR
SYRIAN INTERVENTION, JUMBLATT SPECULATED, SOME SAY SYRIA
WANTS THE BEKAA.  OTHERS SAY SYRIA WISHES TO REPLACE FRANCE
AND HAS TAKEN THIS HISTORIC OPPORTUNITY TO GET CLOSE TO THE
MARONITES.  JUMBLATT CLAIMED ASSAD HAS SPECIFICALLY
TOLD HIM THIS ON FREQUENT OCCASIONS WHILE THEY WERE STILL IN
CONTACT, AS OF A FEW MONTHS AGO.  ALSO, ASSAD HOPED TO WIN
A CARD IN HIS DIPLOMATIC GAME, GOING TO FRANCE AS A FRIEND OF
JORDAN ON THE ONE HAND AND WITH CONTROL OVER LEBANON AND THE
PALESTINIANS ON THE OTHER.  THIS WOULD HAVE HELPED HIM IN US
EYES TOO AND MAYBE HELPED GET A GOLAN SETTLEMENT OF THE KIND
HE WANTS.  HOWEVER, EGYPT IS NOW BEGINNING TO REPLACE
SYRIA IN THE LEBANON AS IS NORMAL.  AT LEAST SADAT IN HIS
SINAI II POLICY WAS FRANK.  HE HAS WON MUCH RESPECT.
17.  JUMBLATT TENDED TO DOWN-PLAY THE PROBLEM OF SECURITY
IN LEBANON.  HE SAID THE VARIOUS PARTIES ARE BEGINNING TO TAKE
SECURITY IN HAND.  THERE ARE FEWER ASSASSINATIONS NOW AND LOOTING
IS LESS BOTH IN BEIRUT AND IN THE MOUNTAINS.  THE LEBANESE
ARMY WILL BE REBUILT.  THE POPULACE, ONCE IT HAS PEACE, WILL
SELL ITS ARMS.  WITH $20 MILLION, JUMBLATT SAID, THE STATE
COULD BUY BACK THE ARMS ITSELF.  PEOPLE ARE HUNGRY.  AGAIN
HE RETURNED TO HIS THEME THAT YOUNG PEOPLE MUST BE ALLOWED
TO TAKE POWER IN THIS COUNTRY.
18.  FINALLY, JUMBLATT WISHED ME WELL.  HE SAID DEAN BROWN
DID A GOOD JOB HERE.  HE PERHAPS LACKED PATIENCE.  IT IS
BETTER TOWORK A LITTLE MORE SLOWLY AND PATIENTLY AND PERHAPS
WITH LOWER PROFILE, BUT US CAN BE HELPFUL.
19.  SUMMING UP HIS VIEWS, JUMBLATT SAID HE EXPECTED THE
WAR TO END SOON.  EVEN THOUGH HE ADMITTED HIS OWN AIMS ARE
WHAT AMOUNT TO A CONTINUOUS REVOLUTION UNTIL POWER MOVES
FROM THE HANDS OF THE MARONITES TO HIS OWN AND THOSE OF
OTHERS ALLIED WITH HIM, HE THOUGHT MEDITERRANEAN PEOPLE
SUCH AS THE LEBANESE AND PALESTINIANS NEED A REST.  TIME
HAS COME FOR COMPROMISE, AND HE IS PREPARED FOR THAT.
WHEN I ASKED WHETHER CONCENTRATED BITTERNESS BETWEEN
FACTIONS MIGHT NOT IMPEDE COMPROMISE, HE SAID PEOPLE
TEND TO FORGET THE CARNAGE, BLOOD, AND DESTRUCTION,
PARTICULARLY IF A CATASTROPHE IS BIG ENOUGHT.  MEANWHILE
NOTHING CAN BE DONE BY WAY OF FORMAL PEACEMAKING UNTIL
THE SYRIANS WITHDRAW TOTALLY FROM THE LEBANON.
20.  COMMENT:  AS I HAVE BEEN TOLD TO EXPECT, JUMBLATT
HAS AN UNCANNILY WINNING PERSONALITY.  IT IS HARD TO DISLIKE THE
MAN FACE TO FACE.  HE HAS MANY MOODS AND MANY GUISES AND
SEEMS TO BE SPEAKING FRANKLY AT ALL TIMES.  HOWEVER, WHAT HE
SAID OFTEN STRUCK ME AS UNREALISTIC TO SAY THE LEAST.  IN
PARTICULAR, I WAS STRUCK BY HIS GREAT OPTIMISM TO ME IN VIEW
OF HIS SIMULTANEOUS PUBLIC PRONOUNCEMENTS THAT THE WAR WILL
CONTINUE AND VIETNAMIZATION MAY RESULT IF THE CHRISTIANS DO NOT
STOP THEIR ATTACK ON TELL XAATAR.  HE IS CLEARLY A MAN WHOSE
WORDS SHOULD NOT BE TAKEN AT FACE VALUE.  BUT HE IS ALSO A
LEADER WHO SEEMS INDISPENSIBLE IN THE CURRENT POLITICAL
MAKEUP HERE.  HE IS OUT TO BECOME NUMBER ONE IN THE LEBANON,
EVEN IF THIS TAKES A FEW MORE YEARS.
SEELYE



*******************


** 91062 1976JIDDA04709 0.007086047 | 1976-07-05 | JIDDA | STATE | PRINCE FAHD'S VIEWS ON ARAB/ISRAELI SETTLEMENT
1.  PRIOR TO PROVIDING PRINCE FAHD WITH YOUR VIEWS ON
PROBLEMS OF MOVING TOWARD GENERAL SETTLEMENT OF ISRAELI-ARAB
ISSUES AS THEY EMERGED IN PARIS MEETING, I BELIEVED HE WAS
OF OPINION THAT SUCH AN EFFORT SHOULD NOT BE ATTEMPTED UNTIL
AFTER ELECTIONS.  HE CORRECTED MY IMPRESSION, SAYING THAT HE
AGREED THAT NOTHING WOULD BE PRACTICAL UNTIL REPUBLICANS
NOMINATE THEIR CANDIDATE FOR THE PRESIDENCY, BUT HE HOLDS THAT
USG CAN AND SHOULD IMMEDIATELY AFTER THAT EVENT MOUNT AN
EFFORT TO NEGOTIATE A GENERAL SETTLEMENT AND SHOULD PROVIDE ITS
OWN VIEWS AS TO WHAT THAT MIGHT INCLUDE.  FAHD BELIEVES THAT
ALL PRINCIPAL FACTORS, MEANING ISRAELI, ARAB, U.S. AND INTERNATIONAL
OPINION ARE READY FOR SUCH AN EFFORT AND THAT TO AWAIT THE
OUTCOME OF THE U.S. ELECTIONS WOULD DIMINISH RATHER THAN
ENHANCE THE PROSPECTS FOR SUCCESS.
2.  HE ADDS THAT THE AMERICAN PUBLIC, WHICH IS THE MOST
IMPORTANT ELEMENT IN THE EQUATION, IS NOW SUFFICIENTLY EDUCATED
ABOUT ARAB-ISRAELI ISSUES, AND IS AWARE THAT LOGIC AND JUSTICE
ARE NOT ALL ON ONE SIDE.  AMERICANS ARE AWARE THAT OUR
RESPONSIBILITY FOR THE EXISTENCE AND SECURITY OF THE STATE OF
ISRAEL IS CLEAR AND THAT WE CANNOT DIVEST OURSELVES OF THAT
RESPONSIBILITY.  AT SAME TIME HE BELIEVES THE AMERICAN PUBLIC
IS MORE THAN TIRED OF POLITICAL ISOLATION, THE EXPENSE AND THE
MANEUVERING WHICH HAVE KEPT THE PROBLEM IN THE FOREFRONT OF
AMERICAN DOMESTIC POLITICS FOR SO LONG.
3.  FAHD SAID THESE THINGS TO ME AND MORE.  HIS HOPE THAT
PRESIDENT FORD'S CAMPAIGN WOULD BE SUCCESSFUL WAS CLEARLY
EXPRESSED AND, ONCE THE NOMINATING PROCESS ENDS, HE SEES THE
INTERIM BETWEEN IT AND ELECTION DAY AS AN OPPORTUNITY FOR
ACTION RATHER THAN STAGNATION.  AMERICANS ADMIRE THE PRESIDENT'S
POLITICAL COURAGE, HE DECLARED, AND WOULD ADMIRE HIM MORE FOR
ACTION DESIGNED TO SETTLE THE PROBLEM.  HE WOULD NOT LISTEN TO
MY COMMENT THAN AN ANNOUNCEMENT OF THE CHARACTER HE HAD IN
MIND MIGHT EMBITTER THE CAMPAIGN.  THE CAMPAIGN HAD ALREADY
DEMONSTRATED THAT ZIONIST SUPPORT COULD NOT ACHIEVE A GREAT DEAL
FOR THOSE CANDIDATES WHO HAD IT, HE DECLARED.
4.  AS FOR LEBANON, HE APPRECIATED HEARING AGAIN THAT WE DO
NOT FAVOR PARTITION.  HE ADDED THAT WOULD NOT EVEN BE IN THE
INTEREST OF THE IERAELIS, THOUGH THEY MIGHT THINK IT IS.  HE
OBVIOUSLY FEARS THE DISINTEGRATING AND GENERALLY DANGEROUS EFFECT
OF THE PLO PRESENCE IN LEBANON AND SAID THAT RECENT EVENTS HAD
MADE THE NECESSITY OF GETTING THEM BACK INTO THEIR HOMELAND,
THE WEST BANK, EVEN CLEARER.
5.  RETURNING TO THE SUBJECT OF A GENERAL SETTLEMENT OF THE ARAB-
ISRAELI PROBLEM, HE INSISTED THAT AN AMERICAN EFFORT TO ACHIEVE
"PEACE AND TRANQUILITY IN RETURN FOR ARAB TERRITORIES TAKEN OVER
BY ISRAEL IN 1967" WOULD EVOKE WIDESPREAD ARAB, ISLAMIC AND
INTERNATIONAL SUPPORT.
PORTER



*******************


 * 170761 1976PORTL00577 0.007085989 | 1976-07-03 | PORT LOUIS | STATE | AIR FRANCE HIJACKING
(C) MAPUTO 746 (NOTAL)
1. AT RECEPTION HOSTED BY PRESIDENT AMIN FOLLOWING OAU SUMMIT
OPENING SESSION EVENING JULY 2 I APPROACHED WALDHEIM AND HAD BRIEF
EXCHANGE WITH HIM RE ENTEBBE HIJACKING SITUATION. HE SAID: "PLEASE
TELL YOUR SECRETARY OF STATE THAT I AM DOING ALL IN MY POWER TO BE
HELPFUL." HE HAD HAD NO DIRECT NEWS SINCE DEPARTING MAPUTO EARLIER
IN DAY. WALDHEIM SAID HE HAD HAD A BRIEF CONVERSATION WITH AMIN
PRIOR TO OAU SUMMIT OPENING SESSION AND THEY HAD SCHEDULED ANOTHER
MEETING FOR THIS MORNING (10 A.M. LOCAL JULY 3). WALDHEIM
REMARKED THAT AMIN "LIKES TO RUN THE WHOLE SHOW," SO IT IS
DIFFICULT TO GET HIM TO DO WHAT ONE WANTS. WALDHEIM THOUGHT
THERE WAS SOME ADVANTAGE IN THE FACT THAT THE UNDP REP IN
KAMPALA WHOM HE HAD INSTRUCTED TO GET INVOLVED IS AN AFRICAN
(GHANAIAN). HE ALSO REMARKED THAT AMIN HAD SAID HE WANTED THE
ISRAELIS TO COME TO KAMPALA TO NEGOTIATE.
2. NEITHER AMIN NOR WALDHEIM ATTENDED A MAURITIAN CEREMONY WHICH
PRECEDED FIRST WORKING SESSION OF OAU SUMMIT MORNING OF JULY 3.
3. ALSO HAD A BRIEF ENCOUNTER WITH AMIN AT HIS RECEPTION. EXCHANGE
WAS FRIENDLY, REMARKABLY SO CONSIDERING THAT AT OUR LAST MEETING
IN KAMPALA IN OCTOBER 1973 HE THREATENED TO ARREST ALL AMERICANS
IN UGANDA STARTING WITH ME IF U.S. INTERVENED ON SIDE OF ISRAEL
IN WAR THEN UNDERWAY IN MIDDLE EAST. AMIN INVITED ME TO KAMPALA
AND SAID HE NOW HAS FIFTY AMERICANS IN UGANDA ADVISING HIS AIR
FORCE. A MEMBER OF HIS ENTOURAGE (BYAGAGAIRE) LATER CORRECTED
THIS TO ABOUT FIVE AMERICANS PROVIDING TECHNICAL HELP
AND SERVING AS PILOTS FOR THEIR NEW INTERNAL AIRLINE,
AIR UGANDA.
4. AMIN DISCUSSED HIJACKING IN COURSE OF HIS EXTEMPORANEOUS
REMARKS AT OAU OPENING. IN A BOASTFUL FASHION, HE MADE
FOLLOWING POINTS: (A) ALTHOUGH HE HAD NOT INVITED HIJACKERS
TO UGANDA, HE HAD PERMITTED PLANE TO LAND FOR HUMANITARIAN
REASONS; (B) FACT THAT EUROPEANS WERE AMONG HIJACKERS SHOWED
THAT PALESTINIANS ENJOY WORLD-WIDE SUPPORT; (C) FOR FIRST TIME
IN HISTORY HOSTAGES HAVE BEEN PERMITTED TO LEAVE PLANE AND
SEEK COMFORT IN AIRPORT TRANSIT LOUNGE; (D) HE HAD WORKED
HARD TO GET AS MANY HOSTAGES RELEASED AS POSSIBLE;
(E) HE HAD COMPLIED WITH HIJACKERS' DEMANDS REGARDING
RELEASE OF ONLY PART OF HOSTAGE GROUP BECAUSE THEY
WERE "SURROUNDED" BY EXPLOSIVES AND WERE IN DANGER OF BEING
KILLED; (F) "SOME OF THE ISRAELI HOSTAGES ARE "INNOCENT", SO
THEY SHOULD NOT BE KILLED; (G) AS A RESULT OF THIS INCIDENT, HE
HAD RECEIVED SEVERAL PHONE CALLS FROM ISRAEL, FOR FIRST TIME
SINCE HE HAD BROKEN RELATIONS WITH ISRAEL IN 1972. AMIN
REMARKED THAT HE WOULD PROBABLY NOT BE ABLE TO PARTICIPATE
FULLY IN OAU SUMMIT AS HE HAD A PROBLEM AT HOME THAT HE HAD
TO DEAL WITH. THIS HAS LED TO SPECULATION THAT AMIN WILL
RETURN TO KAMPALA, POSSIBLY TODAY, JULY 3, TO CONTINUE
DEALING WITH HIJACKERS. A MEMBER OF HIS DELEGATION (PAUL
ETIANG) TOLD ME LAST NIGHT THAT THIS WAS PROBABLE.
KEELEY



*******************


 * 309235 1976TELAV04701 0.007085381 | 1976-07-07 | TEL AVIV | STATE | CABINET AND KNESSET TO RECONSIDER DEATH PENALTY FOR TERRORISTS
TERRORISTS
SUMMARY: FOLLOWING THE ENTEBBE EPISODE, A NUMBER OF
MINISTERS AND KNESSET MEMBERS HAVE PROPOSED THAT THE
GOVERNMENT REVIEW ITS POLICY ON DEATH PENALTY FOR TERRORIST
KILLERS.  MINISTERYFREPORTEDLY ARE RELUCTANT TO HOLD A
FULL SCALE DEBATE ON THE SUBJECT UNDER THE IMMEDIATE IMPACT OF THE
ENTEBBE OPERATION, BUT IS EXPECTED THAT THE MATTER
WILL BE PLACED ON THE CABINET AGENDA WITHIN A FEW WEEKS.
END SUMMARY.
1.  ISRAELI LAW PROVIDES FOR CAPITAL PUNISHMENT BUT IT
HAS BEEN GOVERNMENT POLICY NOT TO APPLY IT IN PRACTICE.
JUSTICE MINISTER ZADOK, REVIEWING THE GOVERNMENT'S
POSITION IN JULY 6 KNESSET DEBATE, RECALLED THAT ON
OCTOBER 29, 1967, THE ESHKOL GOVERNMENT HAD INSTRUCTED
PROSECUTORS TO WITHOLD REQUESTS FOR EXECUTION OF
CONVICTED TERRORISTS.  THE RABIN GOVERNMENT REAFFIRMED
THIS POLICY ON AUGUST 4, 1974.  (INDEED, AS FAR AS THIS
EMBASSY KNOWS, THERE HAVE BEEN ONLY TWO CASES OF CAPITAL
EXECUTIONS IN ISRAEL'S HISTORY--THE FIRST WAS AN ISRAELI
CHARGED WITH TREASON DURING THE WAR OF INDEPENDENCE
AND POSTHUMOUSLY FOUND TO HAVE BEEN INNOCENT AND THE
SECOND WAS ADOLF EICHMAN IN 1962.)
2.  PRIME MINISTER RABIN REFERRED BRIEFLY TO THE NEED
FOR A POLICY REVIEW IN A JULY 5 MEETING OF THE LABOR
ALIGNMENT EXECUTIVE.  HE GAVE NO INDICATION, HOWEVER,
AS TO HIS OWN VIEWS ON THE MATTER.  DEFENSE MINISTER PERES
IN A SPEECH ON JULY 6 SAID THAT HIS PERSONAL VIEW WAS
THAT ISRAEL SHOULD REFRAIN FROM EXECUTINLRTERRORISTS
EXCEPT FOR UNUSUAL CASES SUCH AS THAT OF THE JAPANESE
TERRORIST KOZO OKAMOTO WHO PARTICIPATED IN THE 1972 LOD
AIRPORT MASSACRE.
3.  JUSTICE MINISTER HAIM ZADOK TOLD THE KNESSET THAT HE
WAS NOT IMPOSED TO THE DEATH PENALTY FOR TERRORISTS "ON
PRINCIPLE OR ON HUMANITARIAN GROUNDS..."HE ADDED THAT
"AS THINGS STAND NOW, SHYING AWAY FROM THE DEATH PENALTY FOR
TERRORISTS IS NOT A LAW BUT A MATTER OF GOVERNMENT
POLICY.  IT MAY BE ADVISABLE TO REVIEW THAT POLICY NOW, NOT
IN THE HEAT OF EMOTION, BUT IN A DVBUBERATE MANNER...
FOR ME, THE ONLY CONSIDERAT*, 8 , WILL IT (THE DEATH
PENALTY) AID IN OUR FIGHT AGAINST TERRORISM?"
4.  JERUSALEM POST CORRESPONDENTS WALLFISH AND LANDAU
WRITE ON JULY 6 THAT THE CURRENT DEBATE IS A RESULT
OF THE REALIZATION "THAT THE TERROR GROUP RESPONSIBLE
FOR THE UGANDA HIJACK IS AN UNPRECEDENTEDLY SOPHISTICATED
AS
DETERMENED GANG OF INTERNATIONAL OUTLAWS--NOT ALL
PALESTINIANS--WHO ARE LIKELY TO TRY SIMILAR ACTIONS AGAIN...
THOSE WHO FAVOR A REVIEW OF THE DEATH PENALTY POLICY
ARGUE THAT THE PRESENCE IN ISRAEL OF SUCH 'SPECTACULAR'
KILLERS AS ILAMOTO SERVES AS A INNSTANT INCENTIVE AND
INCITEMENT FOR FURTHER HIJACK ATTEMPTS...AT THE SAME
TIME, HOWEVER, HUMANITARIAN AND MORAL CONSIDERATIONS
WHICH HAVE GUIDED ISRAEL AWAY FROM EVER IMPLEMENTING
THE DEATH
PENALTY STILL POWERDELLY AFFECT POLICYMAKERS."
5.  THE LIKUD EXECUTIVE JULY 5 UNANIMOUSLY VOTED IN
FAVOR OF APPLYING THE DEATH PENALTY FOR TERRORISTS AND
HAS DEMANDED AN URGENT KNESSET DEBATE ON THE SUBJECT.
6.  COMMENT: PUBLIC DEBATE OVER THE MERITS OF THE
DEATH PENALTY FOR TERRORISTS INEVITABLY SURFACES IN
THE WAKE OF MAJOR TERRORISTS OPERATIONS.  THE ISSUE
WAS VIGOROUSLY ARGUED AFTER DVE KIRYAT SHMONA AND MAALOT
MASSACURES IN THE SPRING OF 1974 WHICH INVOLVED THE
DEATH OF CHILDREN AND TEENAGERS.  IN THE PRESENT INSTANCE,
THERE IS AGAIN A GROUNDSWELL OF SENTIMENT IN FAVOR OF
REVERSING GOVERNMENT POLICY.   THE FINAL DECISION, HOWEVER,
WILL REST WITH RABIN WHO, ON THIS PARTICULAR
MATTER, IS LIKELY TO CONSULT CLOSELY WITH JUSTICE
MINISTER ZADOK.
TOON



*******************


 * 170769 1976PORTL00594 0.007084986 | 1976-07-06 | PORT LOUIS | STATE | MAURITIUS BREAKS RELATIONS WITH ISRAEL
1. BEGIN UNCLASSIFIED: MAURITUAN PAPERS JULY 6 CARRIED
AFP REPORT THAT MAURITIUS HAS SEVERED DIPLOMATIC RELATIONS
WITH ISRAEL. ACCORDING TO THE PRESS, RELATIONS HAD BEEN
COOLING BETWEEN THE TWO COUNTRIES FOR SEVERAL MONTHS AND
MAURITIUS HAD NOT RESPONDED TO ISRAELI REQUESTS TO ACCREDIT
NEW ISRAELI AMBASSADOR. PRESS REPORTED THAT GOM ACTION OF
BREAKING RELATIONS HAD ALREADY BEEN TAKEN JULY 1 BEFORE THE
ISRAELI COMMANDO OPERATION IN UGANDA. HOWEVER, GOM HAS
NOT MADE PUBLIC ANNOUNCEMENT OF RUPTURE. END UNCLASSIFIED
2. COMMENT: MINEXTAFF PERMANENT SECRETARY TOLD EMBOFF
THAT PRIME MINISTER RAMGOOLAM HAD INSTRUCTED MAURITIAN
EMBASSY IN LONDON TO INFORM ISRAELIS OF GOM DECISION TO
TERMINATE DIPLOMATIC RELATIONS, APPARENTLY SOMETIME LAST
WEEK. GOM CONTINUED TO MAINTAIN DIPLOMATIC RELATIONS WITH
ISRAEL AFTER OTHER AFRICAN STATES HAD SEVERED THEIR RELATIONS
LARGELY BECAUSE OF THE HIGH RESPECT RAMGOOLAM HAS FOR GOLDA
MEIR. RAM HAS COMMENTED THAT HE DOESN'T KNOW THE NEW
GENERATION OF LEADERS IN ISRAEL AND HE HAS NOTICEABLY
COOLED TOWARDS ISRAEL AS HIS FRIEND GOLDA MEIR LEFT ACTIVE
POLITICS. IN RECENT MONTHS, GOM HAS UNDERTAKEN TO
STRENGTHEN DIPLOMATIC RELATIONS WITH THE ARAB WORLD. THE
NEW GOM ALIGNMENT WITH THE ARABS AND AFRICAN OAU PRESSURE
SEEM TO HAVE CONVINCED RAM THAT DIPLOMATIC TIES WITH ISRAEL
WERE A LUXURY HE COULD NO LONGER AFFORD. RAM MAY ALSO HOPE
THAT BREAKING RELATIONS WITH ISRAEL WILL HELP HOM WITH MOSLEM
VOTERS IN GENERAL ELECTIONS LATER THIS YEAR.
KEELEY



*******************


** 101074 1976KUWAIT03191 0.007084616 | 1976-07-06 | KUWAIT | STATE | KUWAITI REACTION TO ISRAELI ENTEBBE OPERATION
1. ALL KUWAIT DAILIES UNANIMOUS IN DENOUNCING ISRAELI RAID ON
AIRPORT IN UGANDA.  EDITORIALS IN MOST KUWAIT DAILIES CRITICAL
OF ISRAELS BUT REACTION ONE OF FRUSTRATION DUE TO SUCCESSFUL
PRE-EMPTIVE ATTACK.  THEREFORE ARABS FEELING MORTIFIED BUT
UNABLE COORDINATE RESPONSES.  EDITORIALS PRIMARILY ADOPT
WRINGING-OF-HANDS ATTITUDE.  "AL RAI AL AAM" DISCUSSES "MYTHICAL
FEAR SKILLFUL AND INGENIOUS...".  AL SIYASSAH COLUMNIST NOTES
FACTS ISRAEL SEEMS TO BE NATION "WHICH IS ALWAYS CAPABLE..."
AND DEPLORES "DECLARED INNOCENCE ARAB REGIME...".  ONLY AL
SIYASSAH, IN COLUMN BY MUSTAFA ABU LIBDEH, TOP POLITICAL/ECONOMIC
WRITER, IS QUESTION OF AMERICAN INVOLVEMENT RAISED.  LIBDEH
CALLS OPERATION ONE WHICH MEANT TO AVERT "ESCALATION OF FIGHTING
IN LEBANON...CONTRARY TO U.S. POLICY..."  "THEREFORE AN OPERATION
ON THE WHOLE AMERICAN...".  ENGLISH LANGUAGE DAILY "KUWAIT TIMES"
CALLS FOR "A HITLER FOR THE ARABS" IN A VERY EMOTIONAL COMMENTARY
BY "A PALESTINIAN" AND FRONT PAGE EDITORIAL, UNSIGNED, IS
ENTITLED "LAUGH NOW, CRY LATER" WHICH IS BITTER IN DENUNCIATION
ISRAEL RADI AND LOOKS FOR RETALIATION.
2. COMMENT: THE ISRAEL ENTEBBE OPERATION, COMING AS IT DOES ON
TOP OF SEVERAL QUASI-TERRORIST INCIDENTS IN KUWAIT (THE BOMBING
AT SYRIAN AIRLINES AND "AL-ANBA" NEWSPAPER), HAS ONLY UNDERSCORED
TENDER-BOX SECURITY SITUATION IN KUWAIT AND JITTERINESS AMONG
KUWAITI AUTHORITIES.  KUWAITS HAVE BEGUN TO INSTITUTE LATE-
NIGHT RANDON ROAD CHECKPOINT SEARCHES, SOMETHING UNHEARD OF
IN RECENT TIMES, IN AN EFFORT TO CHECKMATE MOVES BY POTENTIAL
TROUBLE-MAKERS.  WE UNDERSTAND THAT BOMB SCARE ALSO OCCURRED
AT AIRPORT 2 JULY, LEADING TO EVACUATION OF TERMINAL. INTERIOR
MINISTER SHAYKH SA'D AL-ABDULLAH REPORTEDLY DELIVERED REPORT TO
COUNCIL OF MINISTERS ON SECURITY SITUATION AT WEEKLY SESSION
TODAY, AND THERE IS NO DOUBT THAT AUTHORITIES VERY SERIOUS
ABOUT PROSPECTS FOR VIOLENCE HERE IN NEAR FUTURE.
MAESTRONE



*******************


** 252173 1976STATE166537 0.007083929 | 1976-07-05 | STATE | SECRETARY | PRINCE FAHD'S VIEWS ON ARAB/ISRAELI SETTLEMENT

 * 132810 1976MOGADI01053 0.007083493 | 1976-07-06 | MOGADISCIO | STATE | SIAD CONDEMNS RAID AT ENTEBBE IN SPEECH CLOSING REGIONAL SPORTS  COMPETITION JULY 4 PRESIDENT
IN SPEECH CLOSING REGIONAL SPORTS COMPETITION JULY 4 PRESIDENT
MOHAMED SIAD BARRE CONDEMNED "INTERNATIONAL ZIONISM FOR RAID ON
UGANDA BY JEWISH TROOPS" WHICH HE SAID "VIOLATED NATIONAL SOVER-
EIGNTY" OF UGANDA. ASSERTING ISRAELIS " HAD BACKING OF INTERNATIONAL
IMPERIALISM IN THIS ACT," SIAD WARNED THAT EVENTS IN UGANDA
WOULD BE REPEATED ELSEWHERE IN AFRICA AND, IN UNMISTAKEABLE
REFERENCE PROPOSED US ARMS SALES TO KENYA AND ZAIRE, SAID
IMPERIALISTS' "POURED ARMS INTO SOME AFRICAN COUNTRIES ON PRETEXT
THAT ARMS WERE FOR DEFENSE THOSE COUNTRIES" WHILE, IN FACT,
"ACTUAL AIM WAS PROTECT IMPERIALIST INTERESTS." PREDICTABLY,
IN COMMENTS ON UGANDA INCIDENT, SIAD MADE NO REFERENCE TO EVENTS
PRECEDENT ISRAELI ACTION.
LOUGHRAN



*******************


** 49534 1976CAIRO09166 0.007082208 | 1976-07-07 | CAIRO | STATE | POSSIBLE SC MEETING ON ISRAELI RESCUE OPERATION
(B) CAIRO 9128 (NOTAL)
1. REFTEL (A) JUST RECEIVED. ASSUME NO ACTION IS TO BE
TAKEN WITH GOE UNTIL AND UNLESS UNSC IS CALLED INTO
SESSION TO DEBATE ISRAELI RESCUE OPERATION.
2. GOE, IN PERSON OF FAHMY, HAS PUBLICLY CONDEMNED
ISRAELI OPERATION. HIS EVEN STRONGER DENUNCIATION,
AS GIVEN TO AMBASSADOR, WAS REPORTED REFTEL B (EXDIS).
HE DISMISSES PUBLIC CHARGES OF UGANDAN COLLABORATION
WITH HIJACKERS AS ISRAELI FABRICATIONS INTENDED JUSTIFY
WHAT HE REGARDS AS AN ILLEGAL ISRAELI ACTION. FAHMY'S
REACTION IS BASED PARTLY ON CHAGRIN THAT ISRAELIS COULD
SUCCESSFULLY MOUNT SUCH AN OPERATION AND PARTLY ON OAU
CONSIDERATIONS. HE HAS SAID THAT GOE WILL SUPPORT
UGANDAN CALL FOR UNSC MEETING IF SUCH CALL IS MADE.
AT SUCH MEETING, GOE MAY BE EXPECTED ASSOCIATE ITSELF
WITH THOSE DEMANDING A RESOLUTION CONDEMNING ISRAELI
ACTION.
3. AT SAME TIME, GOE IS PUBLICLY ON RECORD AS OPPOSING
TERRORISM, WHICH WOULD BE PEG ON WHICH A DEMARCHE COULD
BE HUNG TO REQUEST SUPPORT FOR AN OPERATIVE PARA RE
EVERY GOVERNMENT'S OBLIGATION TO END ACTS OF TERRORISM.
PROBLEM THIS INSTANCE WILL BE THAT, DESPITE GENERAL
NATURE OF PROPOSED PARA, GOE WILL RECOGNIZE IT IS
DIRECTED AGAINST UGANDA AND WILL PROBABLY OPPOSE IT.
IF THERE IS TO BE ANY CHANCE OF GETTING GOE TO GO ALONG,
WE WILL HAVE TO PROVIDE
FAHMY WITH SOME STRONG EVIDENCE
OF UGANDAN INVOLVEMENT IN AIDING AND ABETTING HIJACKERS.
EVEN WITH CONCLUSIVE EVIDENCE TO THAT EFFECT, GOE MAY
STILL FIND IT POLITICALLY NECESSARY FOLLOW OAU CONSENSUS.
4. ON CONTINGENCY BASIS, WE WOULD APPRECIATE HAVING
DETAILED STATEMENT RE UGANDAN INVOLVEMENT FOR USE WITH
FAHMY WHEN AND IF NEEDED.
EILTS

 * 28789 1976BERN02980 0.00708184 | 1976-07-02 | BERN | STATE | AIR FRANCE HIJACKING
1. SWISS FOREIGN OFFICE (KAUFFMAN) INFORMS US THAT ISRAELIS HAD
PASSED LIST OF 12-15 IMPRISONED TERRORISTS TO FRENCH GOVT
WHOM THEY WERE PREPARED TO RELEASE IN EXCHANGE FOR RELEASE
OF ISRAELIS IN KAMPALA.
2. KAUFFMAN SAID THAT GOS IS PREPARED TO REMAIN FIRM, BUT
WOULD FOLLOW LEAD OF OTHER COUNTRIES INVOLVED IF THEIR
RESOLVE WEAKENS. SWISS HAVE HAD NO DIRECT NEWS FROM TEL AVIV
AND ARE CONCERNED THAT ISRAELIS MAY BE PREPARING TO GIVE IN TO
HIJACKERS' DEMANDS WITHOUT FULL CONSULTATIONS WITH OTHER
COUNTRIES HOLDING TERRORISTS DEMANDED BY HIJACKERS.
DAVIS
