 * 170771 1976PORTL00596 0.007081494 | 1976-07-06 | PORT LOUIS | STATE | 13TH ORDINARY OAU SUMMIT: OVERALL IMPRESSIONS SUMMARY. THE 13TH  ORDINARY OAU SUMMIT DISPLAYED UNANIMITY
SUMMARY. THE 13TH ORDINARY OAU SUMMIT DISPLAYED UNANIMITY
IN PREDICTABLE AREAS, FOR EXAMPLE HARSH CRITICISM OF SOUTH
AFRICA OVER THE SOWETO KILLINGS, OF ISRAEL FOR THE COMMANDO
RAID AT ENTEBBE, OF FRANCE FOR SEPARATING MAYOTTE FROM THE
COMORES. BUT ON THE ISSUES OF SUBSTANCE RATHER THAN
RHETORIC THE GENERAL IMPRESSION CREATED WAS ONE OF SISHARMONY,
ACRIMONY AND UNWILLINGNESS TO COMPROMISE. OAU MEMBERS
SHOWED AN ABILITY TO UNITE ON CERTAIN BASIC ISSUES OF
IMPORTANCE TO THEM SUCH AS THE LIBERATION OF SOUTHERN
AFRICA, BUT IT WAS EVIDENT THAT THEIR ENERGIES WERE OFTEN
DISSIPATED ON DISPUTES WITH THEIR NEIGHBORS OVER EVEN MORE
COMPELLING ISSUES INVOLVING TERRITORY OR IDEOLOGY.
END SUMMARY.
1. ACCORDING TO SOME PEOPLE WHO ATTEND OAU MEETINGS
REGULARLY, THE ORGANIZATION AND FACILITIES FOR THE 13TH
ORDINARY SUMMIT WERE AMONG THE BEST EVER. FEW HEADS OF
STATE AND GOVERNMENT TOOK ADVANTAGE OF THE WARM HOSPITALITY
OF MAURITIUS, HOWEVER, AS ATTENDANCE BY THE LEADING POLITICALR
FIGURES OF AFRICA FELL TO ITS LOWEST LEVEL IN THE HISTORY
OF THE ORGANIZATION. A FEW DID SHOW UP -- NOTABLY SENGHOR,
AMIN, NIMEIRI, BONGO, OULD DADDAH, MANCHAM, JAWARA,
TEFERI BANTE, KAUNDA -- BUT MOST STAYED AWAY. SPECULATION
HERE ABOUT THE REASONS FOR THE ABSENCES STRESSED THE DISTANCE
OF MAURITIUS FROM MOST AFRICAN CAPITALS, PROTOCOLAIRE
RESERVATIONS ABOUT HOST RAMGOOLAM'S LESSER STATUS AS A
MERE HEAD OF GOVERNMENT, AND, ESPECIALLY, FEARS OF A
POSSIBLE COUP AT HOME AGAINST A LEADER ATTENDING THE
CONFERENCE (AS HAPPENED LAST YEAR TO GOWON OF NIGERIA, AND
AS NEARLY HAPPENED THIS YEAR TO NIMEIRI OF THE SUDAN).
2. THE NAME OF THE ORGANIZATION AND ITS MOTTO ("WE WILL
NOT BE DIVIDED") WERE THE SOURCE OF IRONIC AMUSEMENT, FOR
DISUNITY PREVAILED OVER UNITY IN MANY OF THE DELIBERATIONS.
AFRICAN COUNTRIES WHOSE CONFLICTS DOMINATED THE SESSIONS
INCLUDED ETHIOPIA VS. SOMALIA OVER THE FTAI, ALGERIA VS.
MORROCCO AND MAURITANIA OVER THE WESTERN SAHARA, UGANDA
VS. KENYA OVER THE ISRAALI COMMANDO RAID AT ENTEBBE, AND
SUDAN VS. LIBYA OVER THE COUP ATTEMPT AGAINST NIMEIRI.
THERE WAS ADDIDTIONAL DIVISIVENESS AMONG THE FACTIONS OF THE
ANC OF ZIMBABWE. THE UGANDA-KENYA AND SUDAN-LIBYA DISPUTES
ERUPTED ON THE FINAL DAY OF THE CONFERENCE AND MOVED ON TO
OTHER FORA SUCH AS THE UN SECURITY COUNCIL. THE FTAI
ISSUE WAS PARTIALLY SMOOTHED OVER, WITH FURTHER CONSIDERATION
POSTPONED TO A ROUND-TABLE CONFERENCE OF ALL FTAI FACTIONS
TO BE HELD IN ACCRA NEXT MONTH. THE DISPUTE OVER WESTERN
SAHARA WAS THE MOST SERIOUS OF ALL, WITH MOROCCO AND
MAURITANIA THREATENING TO LEAVE THE OAU IF THE MATTER WAS
EVEN DISCUSSED. THIS ISSUE WAS PUT FORWARD FOR LATER
CONSIDERATION BY A SPECIAL OAU SUMMIT, AND IT REMAINS FAR
FROM SETTLED.
3. AS IS PERHAPS NORMAL, THE OAU CONFERENCE THIS YEAR
WAS DOMINATED BY ISSUES AND PROBLEMS WHICH CAME INTO PRO-
MINENCE JUST BEFORE OR DURING THE MEETINGS. THE COUNCIL
OF MINISTERS CONFERENCE HIGHLIGHTED THE SOWETO RIOTS WHICH
SHORTLY PRECEDED THE OPENING SESSION. THE SUMMIT ITSELF
TURNED MUCH OF ITS ATTENTION TO THE ISRAELI RAID ON ENTEBBE
WHICH OCCURED IN THE MIDST OF THE CONFERENCE, AND THE COUP
ATTEMPT AGAINST NIMEIRI, WHICH TOOK PLACE JUST PRIOR TO THE
SUMMIT OPENING. ALTHOUGH PRACTICALLY ALL OF THE RESOLUTIONS
PREPARED BY THE COUNCIL OF MINISTERS (WITH THE NOTABLE
EXCEPTION OF THE ONE ON WESTERN SAHARA) WERE ADOPTED WITHOUT
DIFFICULTY, THE PUBLIC IMAGE OF THE OAU MEETING WAS ONE
OF DISHARMONY AND CONTROVERSY BECAUSE OF THESE DIVISION-
CAUSING EXTERNAL EVENTS.
4. FRANCE AND ISRAEL WERE THE PRINCIPAL NON-AFRICAN TARGETS
OF OAU RHETORIC AT THE 1976 MEETING. FRANCE WAS ATTACKED
FOR SUPLLYING NECLEAR PLANTS TO SOUTH AFRICA, FOR SEPARATING
MAYOTTE FROM THE COMOROS AND FOR ALLEGED FOOT-DRAGGING ON
GRANTING INDEPENDENCE TO THE FTAI. BESIDES THE ENTEBBE
INCIDENT, ISRAEL'S "CRIME" WAS ALLEGED COOPERATION WITH
SOUTH AFRICA, HIGHLIGHTED BY VORSTER'S VISIT TO ISRAEL.
SOUTH AFRICA ITSELF WAS OF COURSE THE FAVORITE TARGET OF
ALL, WITH THE FOCUS ON SOWETO AS THE MOST SERIOUS INSTANCE
OF SAG VIOLENCEIAGAINST THE COUNTRY'S BLACK MAJORITY SINCE
SHARPEVILLE. ECONOMIC TIES AND SPORTS LINKS WITH SOUTH
AFRICA WERE CRITICIZED, AND NEW ZEALAND WAS SINGLED OUT
BECAUSE OF THE TOUR OF ITS ALL BLACKS RUGBY TEAM TO
SOUTH AFRICA. A BOYCOTT OF THE OLYMPICS WAS RECOMMENDED IF
NEW ZEALAND IS ALLOWED TO PARTICIPATE. THE KOREAN QUESTION
WAS NOT RAISED OR EVEN MENTIONED BY ANYONE AT THE CONFERENCE.
5. THE UNITED STATES GOT OFF LIGHTLY, IN THEM VIEW OF ALL
OBSERVERS. THE SHARPEST CRITICISM DIRECTED AGAINST THE
USG WAS OVER OUR VETO OF ANGOLA'S ADMISSION TO THE UN.
A NUMBER OF SPEAKERS MENTIONED THIS, NOT EXCEPTING UNSYG
WALDHEIM (WHO, THOUGH HE DID NOT MENTION THE US BY NAME,
EXPRESSED THE HOPE THAT ANGOLA WOULD BE PERMITTED TO JOIN
THE UN IN KEEPING WITH THE PRINCIPLE OF UNIVERSALITY).
WE WERE ALSO CRITICIZED FOR FAILING TO PAY OUR DUES TO
UNESCO, WITH THE THREAT THAT ACTION WOULD BE TAKEN TO CANCEL
OUR VOTING RIGHTS. SOME SPEAKERS MENTIONED ALLEGED COLLABORA-
TION WITH SOUTH AFRICA, WITH REFERENCES TO SECRETARY
KISSINGER'S MEETING WITH VORSTER, BUT PRIVATELQ MOST
DELEGATES WERE MORE CURIOUS ABOUT POSSIBLE RESULTS FROM
THE TALKS THAN CRITICAL OF THEIR HAVING BEEN HELD.
6. THE FOLLOWING WERE THE PRIXNCIPAL TOPICS AND THEMES
RAISED BY OAU DELEGATES IN CONVERSATIONS WITH ME AT THE
SEVERAL PUBLIC FUNCTIONS AND CEREMONIES: (A) HARSH CRITICISM
OF THE FRENCH NECLEAR DEAL WITH SOUTH AFRICA AND THE
THREAT THAT BLACK AFRICAN STATES WOULD HAVE TO OBTAIN NUCLEAR
ARMS BY ANY MEANS POSSIBLE TO COUNTER THE SOUTH AFRICAN
DANGER; (B) A STRONGLY NEGATIVE REACTION TO THE US VETO OF
ANGOLA'S MEMBERSHIP IN THE UN; (C) SOME CRITICISM OF THE
GREATLY INCREASED MILITARY ASSISTANCE TO KENYA AND ZAIRE
AS REPRESENTING THE "INTRODUCTION" OF COLD WAR COMPETITION
TO AFRICA; (D) INTEREST IN THE KISSINGER-VORSTER TALKS;
(E) GENEROUS PRAISE FOR AMBASSADOR SCRANTON, BOTH FOR HIS
PERFORMANCE AT THE UN AND ON HIS TOUR OF AFRICA; (F) AD-
VOCACY OF ACTIVE AND DIRECT SUPPORT BY THE US TO THE AFRICAN
LIBERATION MOVEMENTS, WITH THE THREAT THAT OTHERWISE THESE
MOVEMENTS WOULD HAVE TO TURN TO THE COMMUNIST POWERS FOR
THE ARMS THEY NEED.
7. ALTHOUGH ISRAEL WAS ROUNDLY CRITICIZED, IN GENERAL AND
FOR THE ENTEBBE RAID, MIDDLE EAST ISSUES AS UUCH DID NOT
FIGURE PROMINENTLY IN THE DEBATES AND IN FACT WERE NOTABLE
FOR THEIR ABSENCE FROM THIS OAU SESSION. UNSYG WALDHEIM
STARTLED MANY BY SPENDING MORE TIME ON THE MIDDLE EAST IN
HIS SPEECH TO THE OAU OPENING THAN ANY OF THE AFRICAN
LEADERS. INCLUDING THE ARABS, DID IN THEIRS. THE US WAS
MENTIONED NEGATIVELY AS A SUPPORTER OF ISRAEL, BUT NOT
IN AN EXTREME FASHION.
8. THE STAR PERSONALITY AT THE CONFERENCE WAS OF COURSE
IDI AMIN, BECAUSE OF HIS SIZE, HIS CHESTFUL OF GLITTERING
MEDALS, HIS HALF-LITERATE HALF-COMIC IMPROVISATIONS, AND
THE IMAGE OF BRUTE, POTENTIALLY EXPLOSIVE STRENGTH HE RADIATES.
HIS LECTURES ABOUT THE NEED FOR UNITY AND HIS
BOAST THAT HE WILL MARCH HIS TROOPS TO CAPE TOWN WERE
HEARTILY IF MIRTHFULLY APPLAUDED, AND FORTUNATELY FOR HIM
HE WAS GONE FROM MAURITIUS BY THE TIME THE ISRAELIS GAVE
VIVID PROOF OF HIS INABILITY EVEN TO DEFEND HIS OWN AIRPORT.
KEELEY



*******************


** 85495 1976ISLAMA06080 0.0070805 | 1976-07-06 | ISLAMABAD | STATE | POSSIBLE SC MEETING ON ISRAELI RESCUE OPERATION
OPERATION
REFERENCE: STATE 166529
1.  ACTING DCM AND POLITICAL COUNSELOR CALLED ON GOP
ADDITIONAL FOREIGN SECRETARY NIAZ NAIK ON JULY 6 AND
MADE POINTS DRAWN FROM REFTEL, PARAS 1-5.  NAIK INDICATED
GOP COULD NOT SUPPORT PROPOSED US DRAFT RESOLUTION.
2.  NAIK TOOK A VERY HARDLINE AGAINST ISRAELI ACTION.
HE SAID GOP COULD NOT PUT THE HIJACKING AND THE
SUBSEQUENT ISRAELI OPERATION ON SAME PLANE.  OFFICIAL
GOP POSITION, HE SAID, HAD ALREADY BEEN SPELLED OUT IN
PRESS STATEMENT JUST RELEASED,  TEXT OF WHICH HAD BEEN
CABLED TO PAK PERMREP IN NEW YORK.  GOP HAD ALSO SENT
INSTRUCTIONS TO PERMREP ON BASIS PRESS STATEMENT
TELLING HIM TO SUPPORT A DRAFT RESOLUTION CONDEMNING
ISRAEL.  PERMREP HAS BEEN INFORMED PAKISTAN'S
POSITION RE KENYA WOULD DEPEND ON THE CASE WHICH IS
DEVELOPED AGINST GOK.  PERMREP HAS BEEN TOLD TO
SEEK INSTRUCTIONS ON THIS POINT WHEN THE ACTUAL
RESOLUTION IS DRAFTED.  NAIK SAID THAT HIS INFORMATION
WAS THAT THERE WOULD BE NO DIRECT REFERENCE TO KENYA,
JUST A CONDEMNATION OF "THOSE WHO HAD SUPPORTED"  THE
ISRAELI OPERATION.
3.  TEXT OF THE GOP STATEMENT "CONDEMNING ISRAEL'S
TERRORIST ATTACK AGAINST THE PEOPLE OF UGANDA " FOLLOWS:
" THE GOVERNMENT OF PAKISTAN EXPRESSES ITS SENSE OF
PROFOUND SHOCK OVER ISRAEL'S BRAZEN ACT OF AGGRESSION
AGAINST THE PEOPLE AND THE STATE SOVEREIGNTY OF UGANDA.
ISRAELI ARMED FORCES ATTACKED THE ENTEBBE AIRPORT IN
UGANDA ON THE NIGHT OF JULY 3 CAUSING SERIOUS DAMAGE TO
LIFE AND PROPERTY THERE.  DRAWING ATTENTION TO ITS
CONSISTENT OPPOSITION TO ISRAEL'S POLICY OF AGGRESSION,
THE GOVERNMENT OF PAKISTAN CONDEMNS THE ISRAELI ATTACK
ON THE ENTEBBE AIRPORT AND EXPRESSES PAKISTAN'S
SOLIDARITY WITH THE GOVERNMENT AND THE PEOPLE OF UGANDA.
THIS BLATANT AGGRESSION DEMONSTRATED ONCE AGAIN
ISRAEL'S TOTAL DISREGARD FOR THE PRINCIPLES OF
SOVEREIGNTY AND TERRITORIAL INTEGRITY OF STATES AND
ITS LACK OF RESPECT FOR AFRICAN AND ARAB LIVES.
"THIS WAS, HOWEVER, NOT THE FIRST TIME THAT ISRAEL
HAD VIOLATED, WITH TOTAL IMPUNITY, THE CHARTER OF
THE UNITED NATIONS AND HAD LAUNCHED UNPROVOKED AGGRESSION
AGAINST A SOVEREIGN STATE.  THE LAST TWENTY-EIGHT
YEARS ABOUND WITH INNUMERABLE ACTS OF AGGRESSION
COMMITTED BY ISRAEL IN FURTHERANCE OF ITS EXPANSIONIST
DESIGNS.  THE LATEST ACT OF ISRAELI AGGRESSION WAS
SPECIALLY SHOCKING SINCE PRESIDENT IDI AMIN HAD
PERSONALLY BEEN NEGOTIATING THE RELEASE OF THE
HOSTAGES WITH THE HIJACKERS AND HAD ALREADY SUCCEEDED
IN SECURING THE RELEASE OF OVER 150 PERSONS."
4.  IN FURTHER DISCUSSION, NAIK REITERATED THAT GOP
DRAWS A DISTINCTION BETWEEN HIJACKINGS BY INDIVIDUAL
TERRORISTS, WHICH IT CONDEMNS, AND THOSE CARRIED OUT BY
RECOGNIZED LIBERATION ORGANIZATIONS IN PURSUANCE OF THEIR
EFFORTS TO ACHIEVE SELF-DETERMINATION.  PAKISTAN, HE
SAID, WOULD SUPPORT ANY MEASURES AT THE UN TO PROTEST
THE FIRST CATEGORY OF HIJACKINGS.  AS FOR THE SECOND,
HE SAID THAT ACTION MUST BE TAKEN TO REMOVE THE
FUNDAMENTAL REASONS WHY THEY TAKE PLACE.  ASKED IN
WHICH CATEGORY HE THOUGHT THE LATEST HIJACKING FELL,
NAIK REPLIED THAT THE ISRAELI ACTION HAD GIVEN A NEW
COMPLEXION TO THE AFFAIR.
5.  NAIK STOUTLY DEFENDED IDI AMIN'S ROLE CLAIMING THAT
THE UGANDAN PRESIDENT HAD BEEN RESPONSIBLE FOR RELEASE
OF MANY HOSTAGES AND THAT HE WAS MAKING FURTHER PROGRESS WHEN
ISRAELIS INTERVENED.  CITING HIS OWN ROLE IN THE
SUCCESSFUL EFFORTS TO DEAL WITH ARAB HIJACKERS WHO HAD
SEIZED CONTROL OF A GREEK SHIP IN KARACHI HARBOR IN 1974,
NAIK MAINTAINED THAT NEGOTIATIONS SUCH AS THOSE AMIN
HAD REPORTEDLY MOUNTED TOOK MUCH TIME AND PATIENCE.
THE ISRAELIS HAD NO JUSTIFICATION WHATEVER FOR ACTING
AS THEY DID AND THEIR ACTION MIGHT WELL HAVE ADVERSE
REPERCUSSIONS ON THEM.
COMMENT:  NAIK'S REACTION COMES AS NO SURPRISE.  AS
MUSLIM COUNTRY CHAMPIONING ARAB CAUSE AND CONSTANTLY
SEEKING TO ASSOCIATE ITSELF WITH THIRD WORLD CAUSES,
PAKISTAN COULD BE EXPECTED TO JOIN WITH ARAB/AFRICAN
MOVES CONDEMING ISRAELIS, HOWEVER MUCH INDIVIDUAL PAKS
MAY SECRETLY ADMIRE BOLDNESS OF GOI ACTION.
BYROADE



*******************

*  299729 1976STOCKH03682 0.007078662 | 1976-07-06 | STOCKHOLM | STATE | SWEDISH GOVERNMENT REACTION TO ISRAELI ACTION IN UGANDA
1.  SWEDISH FOREIGN MINISTER SVEN ANDERSSON HAS
RELEASED A STATEMENT EXPRESSING THE SWEDISH GOVERNMENT'S
RELIEF AT THE RESCUE OF THE HOSTAGES FROM ENTEBBE
AIRPORT. UNOFFICIAL TRANSLATION FOLLOWS:
2.  "THE SWEDISH GOVERNMENT HAS WITH GREAT RELIEF
RECEIVED THE INFORMATION THAT ALMOST ALL THOSE WHO WERE
TAKEN HOSTAGE - AMONG THEM THE SWEDISH CITIZEN ANN-CARINA
FRANKING - HAVE ESCAPED UNHARMED FROM THE HIJACKING DRAMA
IN UGANDA. AT THE SAME TIME THE GOVERNMENT WISHES TO
EXPRESS ITS DEEP SYMPATHY WITH THE PERSONS FROM SEVERAL
COUNTRIES WHO HAVE LOST A CLOSE RELATIVE. THE
GOVERNMENT HAS REPEATEDLY STRONGLY CONDEMNED THE TAKING
OF HOSTAGES AND OTHER TYPES OF INTERNATIONAL TERRORISM.
IT IS ENTIRELY UNACCEPTABLE THAT IRRESPONSIBLE AND
CRIMINAL GROUPS ATTACK PRIVATE CITIZENS THIS WAY. THIS
HIJACKING DRAMA CAUSES THE SWEDISH GOVERNMENT TO
SHARPLY REPEAT THIS VIEWPOINT. HOWEVER, THIS DOES
NOT MEAN THAT WE TAKE A STAND ON THE INTERNATIONAL LAW
ASPECTS OF WHAT JUST HAPPENED. THE GOVERNMENT WILL
HAVE AN OPPORTUNITY TO PRESENT ITS VIEWS ON THIS AT THE
EXPECTED DEBATE IN THE UN SECURITY COUNCIL."
SMITH

 * 75249 1976GENEVA05310 0.007077632 | 1976-07-06 | GENEVA | STATE | UNDP 22ND GOVERNING COUNCIL: TECHNICAL COOPERATION AMONG DEVELOPING  COUNTRIES: AGENDA ITEM 11
DEVELOPING COUNTRIES: AGENDA ITEM 11
1. SUMMARY. THE UNDP SESSIONAL COMMITTEE ON TCDC,
MEETING FOR THE SECOND TIME, 1) DISCUSSED AT LENGTH THE
ORGANIZATIONAL AND FINANCIAL ASPECTS OF THE WORLD CON-
FERENCE; 2) CONDUCTED A BRIEF, INCONCLUSIVE REVIEW OF
THE RECOMMENDATIONS IN THE FINAL REPORT OF THE WORKING
GROUP ON TCDC (DP/69); 3) AGREED THAT THE SESSIONAL
COMMITTEE ON TCDC SHOULD ACT AS THE PREPARATORY COMMITTEE
FOR THE WORLD CONFERENCE AND 4) AGREED THAT THE CONFERENCE
BE HELD FROM 23 AUGUST TO 6 SEPTEMBER 1977 IN BUENOS AIRES,
ARGENTINA. END SUMMARY.
2. MEETING FOR THE SECOND TIME, THE UNDP SESSIONAL COM-
MITTEE ON TCDC HEARD A POSITIVE INTRODUCTORY STATEMENT
ON TCDC BY THE UNDP ADMINISTRATOR IN WHICH HE REITERATED
HIS PERSONAL COMMITMENT TO THE CONCEPT OF TCDC; DECLARED
THAT HE WOULD CONSULT WITH UN AGENCIES TO ASSURE THAT
IMPLEMENTATION OF TCDC MOVED AHEAD FASTER; AND
PLEDGED HE WOULD DO HIS UTMOST TO MAKE THE WORLD TCDC
CONFERENCE NEXT YEAR A SUCCESS.
3. IN ACCORDANCE WITH DECISIONS OF THE TWENTIETH AND
TWENTY-FIRST SESSIONS OF THE GOVERNING COUNCIL, THE
COMMITTEE HAD TWO MAJOR ISSUES BEFORE IT: ONE WAS
THE ORGANIZATIONAL AND FINANCIAL ASPECTS OF THE WORLD
CONFERENCE; THE OTHER WAS A PRELIMINARY EXCHANGE OF
VIEWS ON THE RECOMMENDATIONS IN THE REPORT OF THE
WORKING GROUP ON TCDC.
4. MEMBERS COMMENDED THE RESULTS OF THE ASIAN AND
LATING AMERICAN REGIONAL MEETINGS ALREADY HELD PREPA-
RATORY TO THE CONFERENCE ON TCDC. IT WAS POINTED OUT
THAT THE BANGKOK MEETING IDENTIFIED SEVERAL AREAS
ESPECIALLY SUITABLE FOR TCDC ACTIVITIES WHILE THE LIMA
MEETING PROPOSED A MAJOR TCDC PROJECT AMONG MEMBERS
OF THE REGIONA, TO BE ASSISTED AN FINANCED BY UNDP.
WHILE TCDC HAD BEEN ADVANCED AT THE REGIONAL LEVEL,
IN THE VIEW OF SOME MEMBERS MORE INTEREGIONAL COOPERA-
TION WAS NEEDED.
5. THE COMMITTEE THEN DISCUSSED AT LENGTH DP/202,
ORGANIZATION OF THE CONFERENCE, MOST ESPECIALLY CON-
FERENCE ARRANGEMENTS, CONFERENCE FINANCING ISSUES,
CONFERENCE DOCUMENTATION, CONFERENCE PARTICIPANTS
(WITH NEW EMPHASIS ON THE IMPORTANT ROLE OF ORGANIZA-
TIONS OF THE UN SYSTEM AND PRIVATE ENTITIES), THE PROPOSED
PROVISIONAL AGENDA, AND INFORMATION ACTIVITIES.
6. AMONG THE MOST IMPORTANT POINTS RAISED AND DECI-
SIONS TAKEN WERE:
A) WITH RESPECT TO THE CONFERENCE ON TCDC, THE
REPRESENTATIVE OF ARGENTINA ANNOUNCED THAT THE INVITA-
TION HAD NOW BEEN FORMALIZED IN DOCUMENT A/31/82.
LATER THE COUNCIL PROPOSED THAT THE CONFERENCE BE HELD
FROM 23 AUGUST TO 6 SEPTEMBER, 1977 IN BUENOS AIRES,
ARGENTINA.
B) IT WAS AGREED THAT THE SESSIONAL COMMITTEE ON
TCDC SHOULD ACT AS THE PREPARATORY COMMITTEE FOR THE
CONFERENCE, WITH THE LATTER OPEN TO OTHER INTERESTED
GOVERNMENTS. IT WAS GENERALLY AGREED THAT THERE SHOULD
BE TWO, AND POSSIBLY THREE MEETINGS OF THE PREPARATORY
COMMITTEE.
C) THE COMMITTEE AGREED TO RECOMMEND TO THE
GOVERNING COUNCIL THAT THE COUNCIL SHOULD DEVOTE THE
FIRST WEEK OF ITS TWENTY-THIRD SESSION TO THE PREPARA-
TORY COMMITTEE IN ORDER TO FACILITATE ITS WORK.
D) VARIOUS MEMBERS, WHILE EXPRESSING THEIR AWARE-
NESS OF UNDP'S FINANCIAL STRINGENCIES, NONETHELESS
VOICED CONCERN LEST THE PROPOSED BUDGET FOR THE PREPA-
TIONS FOR THE CONFERENCE FALL SHORT OF MEETING ALL ACTUAL
NEEDS.
E) THERE WAS GENERAL AGREEMENT ON THE NEED FOR
ASSISTANCE FROM THE ECONOMIC AND SOCIAL COUNCIL
SECRETARIAT IN THE VIEW OF ITS EXTENSIVE WORLD
CONFERENCE EXPERIENCE.
F) MEMBERS EXPRESSED THE VIEW THAT DOCUMENTATION
SHOULD BE KEPT TO A MINIMUM AND EMPHASIZED THE IMPOR-
TANCE OF ONE CLEAR AND CONCISE SUMMARY PRESENTATION
FOR GENERAL DISCUSSION.
G) THE VIEW WAS EXPRESSED THAT SOME OF THE PRO-
POSED AGENDA ITEMS READ MORE LIKE STATEMENTS OF PRIN-
CIPLE THAN ISSUES FOR DISCUSSION AND THAT IT NEEDED
TO BE REVISED AND EXPANDED.
H) IT WAS SUGGESTED THAT THE GOVERNING COUNCIL
RECOMMEND THE UNITED NATIONS OFFICE OF PUBLIC INFORMA-
TION (OPI) BE REQUESTED TO MAKE TCDC ONE OF ITS FIVE
ITEMS OF SPECIAL EMPHASIS FOR THE YEAR 1977.
I) IT WAS GENERALLY ACCEPTED THAT, AS HAD BEEN
THE CASE AT THE RECENT HABITAT CONFERENCE, ARABIC
SHOULD BE ADDED AS A SIXTH OFFICIAL LANGUAGE FOR THE
CONFERENCE.
7. A NUMBER OF SUGGESTIONS PUT FORTH BY THE US DELE-
GATION RECEIVED CONSIDERABLE SUPPORT INCLUDING THAT:
A) THERE WAS NO NEED TO INCREASE THE AMOUNT OF
PROPOSED UNDP FINANCIAL SUPPORT FOR CONFERENCE PREPARA-
TIONS -- AT LEAST FOR THE MOMENT;
B) PRIVATE INSTITUTIONS SHOULD ALSO BE INVITED
TO THE CONFERENCE;
C) THE ROLE OF WOMEN IN TCDC SHOULD BE ADDED TO
THE PROPOSED AGENDA OF THE WORLD CONFERENCE;
D) THAT "SOCIAL" COOPERATION SHOULD ALSO BE ADDED
TO THE PROPOSED AGENDA WITH "CULTURAL" COOPERATION
BEING DELETED; AND
E) THERE BE NO SOUND RECORDINGS MADE OF THE DELIBERATIONS
OF THE WORKING GROUP AT THE WORLD
CONFERENCE.
8. RECOMMENDATIONS OF THE WORKING GROUP. AFTER
COMPLETING ITS DISCUSSION OF CONFERENCE ARRANGEMENTS,
THE COMMITTEE UNDERTOOK A BRIEF, VERY PRELIMINARY DIS-
CUSSION OF A FEW OF THE RECOMMENDATIONS OF THE WORKING
GROUP ON TCDC (DP/69). THIS WAS DONE AT THE INSISTENCE
OF INDIA AND IN SPITE OF THE FACT THAT THE COMMITTEE
DID NOT HAVE A DOCUMENT ON THE STATUS OF THE IMPLEMEN-
TATION OF THE RECOMMENDATIONS FROM WHICH TO WORK.
9. VERY LITTLE WAS ACCOMPLISHED IN THE BRIEF, PARTIAL
REVIEW WITH ONLY THE FIRST THREE OF THE THIRTY-THREE
RECOMMENDATIONS BEING DISCUSSED.
10. MEMBERS WERE THEN ASKED TO SUGGEST GUIDELINES FOR
THE USE OF THE ADMINISTRATION IN DRAWING UP A REPORT ON
THE IMPLEMENTATION OF THE WORKING GROUP'S RECOMMENDATIONS
TO GUIDE THE COMMITTEE'S REVIEW OF ALL THE RECOMMEN-
DATIONS AT THE NEXT MEETING OF THE COUNCIL IN JANUARY.
1. THE COMMITTEE CONCLUDED ITS WORK BY DRAFTING TWO
DETAILED DECISIONS WHICH, ALONG WITH ITS REPORT, WERE
APPROVED BY THE GOVERNING COUNCIL.
12. FOLLOWING APPROVAL OF THE COMMITTEE'S REPORT BY
THE GOVERNING COUNCIL, THE ISRAELI OBSERVER TO THE
COUNCIL'S PROCEEDINGS (WHO HAD TAKEN NO PART IN THE
COMMITTEE'S PROCEEDINGS) LODGED A RESERVATION POINTING
OUT THAT UNDER THE PARTICIPANT FORMULA PROPOSED FOR
THE TCDC WORLD CONFERENCE AN ILLEGAL LIBERATION MOVEMENT,
THE PLO, WOULD BE PERMITTED TO ATTEND AND TO ONCE AGAIN
JEOPARDIZE THE WORK OF AN IMPORTANT WORLD CONFERENCE
AS HAD BEEN THE CASE AT THE RECENT HABITAT CONFERENCE.
THE REMARKS OF THE ISRAELI OBSERVER WERE REBUTTED BY
KUWAIT, THE PRC AND THE USSR.ABRAMS



*******************


 * 145853 1976NAIROB06998 0.00707733 | 1976-07-07 | NAIROBI | STATE | PRESIDENT AMIN'S MESSAGE TO PRESIDENT KENYATTA AS BROADCASTED BY RADIO  UGANDA AT 1700 GMT JULY 6.
BY RADIO UGANDA AT 1700 GMT JULY 6.
BEGIN TEXT
TEXT: PRESIDENT AMIN HAS IN A MESSAGE TO MZEE JOMO
KENYATTA ASSURED ALL KENYANS THAT IN SPITE OF RECENT DEVELOPMENTS,
UGANDA STILL REGARDS THE ENTIRE PEOPLE OF KENYA AS OUR BROTHERS AND
SISTERS.
IN THE MESSAGE, WHICH WAS COPIED TO PRESIDENT JULIUS
NYERERE OF TANZANIA, FM AMIN SAID: I FELT COMPELLED TO ADDRESS YOU
DIRECTLY ON THE RECENT TRAGIC INVASION OF UGANDA BY THE FORCES
OF ZIONIST ISRAEL.
FROM ALL THE INFORMATION AVAILABLE TO ME, THE ISRAELI
INVASION OF UGANDA, MEMBER COUTRY OF THE EAST AFRICAN
COMMUNITY HAD BEEN CARRIED OUT WITH YOUR EXCELLENCY'S FULL
KNOWLEDGE, AS WELL AS THE AUTHORITY OF YOUR GOVERNMENT.
I THEREFORE (WORDS INDISTINCT) PERSONALLY AND THE PEOPLE
OF UGANDA IN GENERAL, NO LITTLE SURPRISE TO LEARN THAT YOUR
AUTHORITIES COULD READILY OBLIGE FACILITIES TO THE ZIONIST ISRAEL,
FOR LAUNCHING AN ATTACK ON UGANDA WHICH, AS YOU WELL KNOW, IS NOT
ONLY A FELLOW MEMBER OF THE AST AFRICAN COMMUNITY, THE OAU, THE
NON-ALIGNED MOVEMENT BUT ALSO OF THE UN.
FOLLOWING THE PAST HISTORY OF KENYA, DURING ITS STRUGGLE
AGAINST BRITISH COLONIALISM, IT IS OBVIOUS THAT BESIDES YOU
PERSONALLY MANY COUTRIES SUCH AS EGYPT, UNDER THE LATE ABD AL-NASR,
SYRIA, IRAQ AND EVEN THE PALIESTINIANS DID ACTUALLY CONTRIBUTE
IMMEDIATELY, BY PROVIDING KENYA FREEDOM FIGHTERS BOTH ALL THE
NECESSARY WEAPONS AND COMMUNICATIONS WHICH UNDOUBTEDLY ENABLED YOUR
COUNTRY TO OBTAIN HER INDEPENDENCE.
YOUR EXCELLENCY: YOU MAY FURTHER WISH TO NOTE THAT FROM
THE MORNING FOLLOWING THE NIGHT OF THE ZIONIST RAID, IT FURTHER
OCCASIONED ME NO LITTLE SURPRISE TO LEARN THAT YOUR EXCELLENCY
HAS SINCE THEN HEAVILY REINFORMCED THEIR (ED: AS HEARD) MILITARY
UNITS ALONG THE ENTIRE COMMON BORDER OF OUR TWO SISTER COUNTRIES AND,
AT SOME POINTS,FOR EXAMPLE IN LOMINO IN THE SOUTH, KENYAN TROOPS
HAVE EVEN CROSSED INTO UGANDAN TERRITORY, UP TO THREE MILES.
HOWEVER, IN SPITE OF THE RECENT DEVELOPMENTS WHICH HAVE
UNFORTUNATELY BUILT UP UNNECESSARY HIGH TENSION BETWEEN UGANDA AND
KENYA, WE, THE PEOPLE OF UGANDA, STILL REGARD THE ENTIRE PEOPLE OF
KENYA AS OUR BROTHERS AND SISTERS.
WOU SHOULD NOT THEREFORE WORRY OF ANY ATTACK FROM OUR
SIDE OF THE BORDER.
AS A STRONG BELIEVER IN THE EAST AFRICAN COMMUNITY, I AM
THEREFORE SENDING A COPY OF THIS MESSAGE TO OUR BROTHER PRESIDENT,
MWALIMU JULIUS NYERERE, THE OTHER MEMBER OF THE EAST AFRICAN
AUTHORITY, FOR INFORMATION.
I WISH HOWEVER, TO REITERATE TO YOU MY ASSURANCE THAT
KENYA SHOULD HAVE NO CAUSE TO WORRY ABOUT ANY POSSIBLE ATTACK FROM
UGANDA. END TEXT
MARSHALL

 * 139499 1976MOSCOW10695 0.007073471 | 1976-07-07 | MOSCOW | STATE | SOVIET JEWISH EMIGRATION
1.  IT MAY BE OF INTEREST THAT SEVERAL WOULD-BE EMIGRANTS HAVE
TOLD US THAT THEY FEEL THE GOI DECISION NOT TO SEND "VYZOVS"
THROUGH THE DUTCH EMBASSY IN MOSCOW REPRESENTS A DELIBERATE
ATTEMPT ON THE PART OF THE ISRAELI GOVERNMENT TO FORCE THEIR
HANDS.  WE KNOW OF THREE CASES OF MUSCOVITE JEWS, ONLY ONE OF THEM
"KNOWN TO SEEK EMIGRATION," WHO HAD ASKED TO HAVE THEIR "VYZOVS"
SENT THROUGH THE DUTCH EMBASSY, EITHER BECAUSE THEY HAD NOT
FINALLY DECIDED TO EMIGRATE, OR BECAUSE THEY FELT THEY MIGHT
BE ABLE TO AVOID TAKING THE ISRAELI ROUTE.  THE DUTCH TELL US
THEY HAVE NO DIFFICULTY IN AGREEING TO TRANSMIT THE "VYZOVSZ
NONE RECEIVED ANY RESPONSE UNTIL ABOUT TEN DAYS AGO, WHEN ALL
RECEIVED THE DOCUMENTS THROUGH THE SOVIET POST OFFICE.  THE
CASES CONCERN RELATIVES (OR POTENTIAL SPOUSES) OF FIGURES
PROMINENT ON THE SOVIET CULTURAL AND INTELLECTUAL SCENE.  IN THE
CASES OF WHICH WE ARE AWARE, THE RECIPIENTS HAVE TOLD US
(
SEPARATELY) THAT THEY FEEL THAT THE ISRAELI GOVERNMENT DELIBER-
ATELY IGNORED THEIR WISHES AND SENT THE "VYZOVS" DIRECTLY IN
ORDER TO INSURE THAT THE RECIPIENTS, REALIZING THAT THE SOVIET
AUTHORITIES HAD TAKEN NOTE OF THE RECEIPT OF THE DOCUMENTATION,
WOULD THEN FEEL OBLIGED TO GO THROUGH WITH THE FORMAL APPLICATION
TO LEAVE THE USSR.
2.  JEWISH DISSIDENT LEADERS TELL US THAT THEY BELIEVE THERE
HAS BEEN A DECLINE IN THE NUMBER OF "VYZOVS" RECEIVED, ESPECIALLY
IN CITIES OUTSIDE MOSCOW.  THEY ATTIRBUTE THIS DECLINE TO
DECISIONS BY THE SOVIET AUTHORITIES, NOT TO ANY ISRAELI POLICY
CHANGES.
STOESSEL

** 151026 1976NEWDE09903 0.007073384 | 1976-07-06 | NEW DELHI | STATE | INDIAN PRESS COMMENT ON ISRAELI RAID BEGIN SUMMARY: MOST EDITORIAL  COMMENT IN DELHI'S ENGLISH-
BEGIN SUMMARY: MOST EDITORIAL COMMENT IN DELHI'S ENGLISH-
LANGUAGE PRESS ON THE ISRAELI RESCUE OPERATION AT ENTEBBE
AIRPORT PRAISED THE FEAT BUT HELD TEL AVIV RESPONSIBLE
FOR VIOLATION OF UGANDAN SOVEREIGNTY. END SUMMARY.
1. INDIAN PRESS COMMENT ON THE ISRAELI RAID AT ENTEBBE
AIRPORT TERMED THE ISRAELI OPERATION "EXTRAORDINARY...
FANTASTIC... SPECTACULAR" (INDIAN EXPRESS); "A
MOST NOTABLE FEAT OF ARMS" (STATESMAN), AND "BRILLIANT"
(TIMES OF INDIA). SOME COMMENTATORS CRITICIZED THE OPERATION
AS "WANTON" (CONGRESS-ORIENTED NATIONAL HERALD) AND
"UNCIVILIZED" (MOSCOW-LINING PATRIOT).
2. EDITORIAL WRITERS UNIFORMALY CONDEMNED THE ISRAELI
ACTION AS A VIOLATION OF UGANDAN SOVEREIGNTY. THE INDIAN EXPRESS
JUDGED THAT IT "AMOUNTS TO TERRORISM OF A KIND THAT IS
NO DIFFERENT FROM THAT OF THE SKYJACKERS ACTING IN SMALL
GROUPS..." THE NATIONAL HERALD OBSERVED THAT THE POLICY OF "AN
EYE FOR AN EYE IS PART OF THE ZIONIST TRADITION
AND ISRAEL SEEMS TO BE DETERMINED TO SETTLE EVERY INTER-
NATIONAL ISSUE WHICH CONCERNS HER BY THE USE OF FORCE."
THE PATRIOT WARNED THAT TO LET ISRAEL "GO UNPUNISHED FOR
BRAZEN AGGRESSION, VIOLATION OF UGANDA'S SOVEREIGNTY AND
KILLING OF ITS SOLDIERS WOULD BE TO GIVE THE
ZIONIST STATE ENCOURAGEMENT IN ITS HORRIBLE CARRER OF TERRORISM AND
VIOLENCE."SAXBE

** 78070 1976GEORGE01380 0.007073117 | 1976-07-07 | GEORGETOWN | STATE | GUYANA'S POSITION ON ISRAELI RESCUE OPERATION
1.  DURING MEETING IN HIS OFFICE JULY
6 WITH MATTHEWS AND BLACKEN, FONMIN WILLS SAID HE UNDERSTOOD THAT
UGANDA WOULD BRING THE ISSUE OF ISRAELI INTERVENTION IN UGANDA
BEFORE THE UNSC.  WILLS SAID THAT WHILE HIS GOVT CONDEMNED TERROR-
IST ACTS SUCH AS THE KIDNAPPING AND EXTORTION CARRIED OUT BY
PALESTINIAN ORGANIZATIONS, GUYANA WOULD HAVE TO JOIN A PROTEST
AGAINST THE ISRAELI QUOTE INVASION UNQUOTE OF UGANDAN TERRITORY.
REGARDLESS OF CIRCUMSTANCES, SUCH INTERVENTIONS COULD NOT BE
CONDONED.  APART FROM THE INTERNATIONAL ASPECTS OF THE MATTER,
HE SAID, DOMESTIC POLITICAL CONSIDERATIONS MADE IT NECESSARY FOR
GUYANA TO PUBLICLY OPPOSE THE ISRAELI ACTION IN UGANDA.  CLEARLY
HE WAS THINKING OF THE PRECEDENT THAT MIGHT BE SET FOR VENEZUELAN
INCURSIONS INTO GUYANESE TERRITORY.
2.  WILLS ALSO SAID HE BELIEVED THAT POLITICAL PRESSURES IN THE
U.S. WOULD INDUCE THE USG TO OPPOSE A CONDEMNATION OF THE ISRAELI
INTERVENTION.  HE ADDED THAT HE WOULD UNDERSTAND THE
NECESSITY OF THE U.S. ADOPTING SUCH A POSITION, BUT ASKED THAT
THE U.S. ALSO UNDERSTAND GUYANA'S POSITION.  MATTHEWS

** 299728 1976STOCKH03681 0.00707206 | 1976-07-06 | STOCKHOLM | STATE | POSSIBLE SC MEETING ON ISRAELI RESCUE OPERATION
1.  WE CALLED LEIF LEIFLAND, DIRECTOR OF MFA'S OFFICE OF
POLITICAL AFFAIRS, TO SEEK SWEDISH SUPPORT FOR RESOLUTION
ON ISRAELI RESCUE OPERATION IN UNSC ALONG LINES OF
LANGUAGE CONTAINED REFTEL.
2.  LEIFLAND SAID GOS WOULD STUDY OUR REQUEST.
HE NOTED THAT GOS HAD ISSUED CAREFULLY
WORDED STATEMENT EXPRESSING "RELIEF" AT RESCUE OF
HOSTAGES (SEE SEPTEL).  SPEAKING PERSONALLY, LEIFLAND SAID
LIKELIHOOD OF GOS SUPPORT FOR SUCH A RESOLUTION WOULD BE
INCREASED CONSIDERABLY IF USG COULD PROVIDE "WATER TIGHT
EVIDENCE" OF UGANDAN COMPLICITY IN PRESSURING OTHER
GOVERNMENTS TO ACCEDE TO TERRORIST DEMANDS.  HE NOTED THAT
THE PRESS HAD ALLUDED TO GOU SUPPORT OF TERRORISTS, BUT
GOS LACKED HARD FACTS.  IN ORDER TO HAVE IMPACT ON GOS
POSITION AT UNSC, LEIFLAND ADDED, THE INFORMATION SHOULD
BE PROVIDED URGENTLY.
3.  WE WOULD APPRECIATE RECEIVING BY IMMEDIATE CABLE
ANY FACTS DEPARTMENTS HAS ON UGANDAN SUPPORT OF
TERRORISTS' DEMANDS OR OTHER GOU INVOLVEMENT AFTER
TERRORISTS LANDED.

** 182538 1976ROME10862 0.00707184 | 1976-07-06 | ROME | STATE | POSSIBLE SC MEETING ON ISRAELI RESCUE OPERATION
1. WE CONVEYED POINTS MADE REFTEL TO MFA OFFICER DIRECTOR
FOR UN AFFAIRS, FERRABOSCHI, THIS MORNING. FERRABOSCHI SAID
MFA IS WATCHING CAREFULLY TO SEE IF AMIN IN FACT INTENDS TO
TAKE HIS CASE TO SECURITY COUNCIL, BUT HAS NO INDICATIONS
TO DATE THAT SUCH ACTION IS UNDERWAY. FOR THAT REASON, AND
BECAUSE THERE ARE DIFFERING VIEWS WITHIN THE MFA, FERRABOSCHI
SAID THERE IS NOT YET AN OFFICIAL GOI POSITION ON A
POSSIBLE AMIN INITIATIVE. HE ALSO AVOIDED SPECULATING
ON WHAT THE GOI STANCE WOULD BE IN THE EVENT.
2. COMMENT: WITHOUT NAMING FACTIONS, FERRABOSCHI SAID
THERE ARE THOSE IN THE MINISTRY ARGUING THE ILLEGALITY OF
THE ISRAELI MOVE, WITH OTHERS MAKING THE CASE FOR HUMANI-
TARIAN NEED. WHILE FERRABOSCHI, WITH PERHAPS EXCESSIVE
PRUDENCE, DECLINED TO PREDICT ITALIAN SUPPORT FOR THE US
VIEW, WE HAVE LITTLE DOUBT THAT GOI WILL RESPOND FAVORABLY
AND RAPIDLY IF THE PROBLEM MATERIALIZES, ALWAYS PROVIDING
OF COURSE THAT THE OTHER EC EIGHT ARE OF THE SAME GENERAL
VIEW.VOLPE

 * 299735 1976STOCKH03708 0.007071038 | 1976-07-07 | STOCKHOLM | STATE USUN NEW YORK | UGANDAN ROLE IN AIR FRANCE HIJACKING
(C) STOCKHOLM 3682
1.  WE PROVIDED MFA DIRECTOR OF POLITICAL AFFAIRS
LEIFLAND WITH EVIDENCE OF UGANDAN ASSISTANCE TO
HIJACKERS CONTAINED IN REF A.  AFTER READING MATERIAL,
LEIFLAND DESCRIBED IT AS "QUITE GOOD", AND SAID IT
WOULD BE HELPFUL FOR MEETING MFA HAS SCHEDULED FOR
EARLY THIS MORNING TO DETERMINE POSITION GOS WILL TAKE
AT JULY 8 UNSC CONSIDERATION OF ISRAELI RESCUE
OPERATION.
2.  CONTINUING, LEIFLAND SAID THAT HE ANTICIPATED
THAT THERE WOULD BE A CONSIDERABLE AMOUNT OF
"INFLIGHTING" WITHIN GOS RE POSITION IT WILL TAKE ON
ISSUE.  FOR THIS REASON, HE ADDED, IT IS IMPORTANT
THAT FACT HE HAD REQUESTED INFORMATION ON UGANDA'S ROLE
FROM USG NOT RPT NOT LEAK OUT.  WE ASSURED HIM THAT IT
WOULD NOT FROM OUR SIDE.
3.  COMMENT:  AS LEIFLAND HAS INDICATED, UNSC
CONSIDERATION OF ISRAELI RESCUE OPERATION WILL UNDOUBTEDLY
CAUSE CONFLICT WITHIN GOS BETWEEN THOSE OFFICIALS MOST
CONCERNED ABOUT TERRORISM AND THOSE WHOSE CHIEF
INTEREST LIES IN PRESERVING GOOD RELATIONS WITH ARAB
AND AFRICAN NATIONS.  IN HIS CONVERSATION WITH US,
LEIFLAND HAS MADE IT CLEAR THAT HE BELIEVES MOST
IMPORTANT CONSIDERATION IS THAT HOSTAGES ESCAPED
UNHARMED, AND STATEMENT ON OPERATION ISSUED BY SWEDISH
GOVERNMENT (OF WHICH LEIFLAND WAS PRINCIPLE AUTHOR)
REFLECTED THIS VIEW (REF C).  HOWEVER, IT IS
UNCERTAIN WHETHER HIS VIEWS WILL PREVAIL WITHIN GOS
COUNCILS.  BASED ON PAST PERFORMANCE, IT IS
POSSIBLE THAT SWEDES WILL WORK FOR CONCENSUS
RESOLUTION, AND, FAILING THAT, OPT FOR ABSTENTION
WHEN THE CRUNCH COMES.
4.  WE WILL CONTINUE TO PURSUE MATTER WITH LEIFLAND.  IN
THIS CONNECTION, WE WOULD WELCOME THE ADDITIONAL
INFORMATION ON UGANDAN INVOLVEMENT CITED IN PARA. 16 OF
REF A.

** 7501 1976AMMAN03531 0.007070442 | 1976-07-05 | AMMAN | STATE | ISRAELI ENTEBBE OPERATION
1.  WHEN I SAW KING HUSSEIN ON ANOTHER MATTER JULY 4, I
ASKED HIM FOR HIS REACTION TO ISRAELI ENTEBBE OPERATION.
HE WAS FULL OF ADMIRATION FOR THE ISRAELI OPERATION
AND OF PRAISE FOR WAY IT WAS CARRIED OUT.
2.  HE ADDED THAT A NUMBER OF HIS SENIOR PEOPLE HAD
CALLED HIM ABOUT IT IN THE SAME VEIN AND LAMENTED FACT
THEY COULD NOT SEND ISRAELIS CONGRATULAROTY MESSAGES.
3.  EMBASSY WOULD HAVE NO OBJECTION TO TEL AVIV PASSING
ALONG GENERAL TENOR THIS CONVERSATION TO A FEW SELECT
ISRAELIS, IF DEPARTMENT APPROVES, AND IT COULD BE DONE
WITHOUT INFORMATION GETTING INTO PRESS.
4.  FYI:  THIS COMMENT AT THE TOP IS BALANCED BY CRITICAL
COMMENTS FROM SOME JORDANIANS WHO CLAIM ISRAELIS ONLY
PREFER SOLUTIONS OF FORCE TO NEGOTIATION AND WHO SUSPECT
ISRAELIS WILL NOW BE TOUGHER TO DEAL WITH ON MIDDLE
EAST PEACE SETTLEMENT ISSUES.  NO EDITORIAL COMMENT YET.
END FYI.

 * 23572 1976BEIRUT05792 0.007069119 | 1976-07-02 | BEIRUT | STATE INFO AMMAN
CAIRO
DAMASCUS
JIDDA
KUWAIT
LONDON
PARIS
TEL AVIV | MEETING WITH SAEB SALAM
1.  SUMMARY: SAEB SALAM'S EXPRESSION OF SORROW RE MURDER OF
MELOY AND WARING GAVE ME OPENING TO URGE THAT HE USE HIS INFLUENCE TO
SEE THAT MURDERS ARE BROUGHT TO JUSTICE.  SALAM PLACED MUCH OF BLAME
FOR CURRENT LEBANESE SITUATION ON SYRIANS, WHO HE CLAIMED HAD ALIENAT
ED
ALL LEBANESE MOSLEMS. HE ACCUSED SYRIA AND U.S. OF MANIPULATING
SARKIS ELECTION AS PRESIDENT AND CONTENDED THAT SARKIS (IN CONTRAST
TO RAYMOND EDDE) HAS NO POLITICAL FOLLOWING. IN ADDITION, HE CLAIMED
SARKIS IS SURROUNDED BY CORRUPT INDIVIDUALS.  NEVERTHELESS, SINCE HE
HAS BEEN PICKED, ALL LEBANESE SHOULD LINE UP BEHIND HIM.
SALAM WELCOMED CONCEPT OF ROUNDTABLE CONFERENCE, BUT SAID
CEASEFIRE MUST COME FIRST. EGYPT'S STAR IN ARAB WORLD, HE
BELIEVED, HAS NOW RISEN AT SYRIA'S EXPENSE.  END SUMMARY.
2.  IN PROCEEDING TO MY MEETING JULY 1 WITH SAEB SALAM, FORMER
PRIME MINISTER, THERE WAS MUCH MORE NORMAL ACTIVITY ALONG THE
ROUTE THAN THE DAY I CALLED ON PRIME MINISTER KARAME (JUNE 29).
IN THE LATTER INSTANCE THE ROADS WE PASSED THROUGH WERE ALMOST
DESERTED--THE BATTLES OF TELL ZAATAR AND JISR AL-BASHA WERE AT
THEIR HEIGHT. YESTERDAY, PEOPLE WERE WALKING THE SIDEWALKS, AND
MAKESHIFT SHOPS LINED THE SEASIDE CORNICHE.
3.  MY MEETING WITH SAEB SALAM JULY 1, WHICH LASTED TWO HOURS
(HALF HOUR LONGER THAN THE MEETING WITH KARAME), BEGAN WITH HIS
EXPRESSING HIS SORROW ON DEATH OF AMBASSADOR MELOY AND BOB
WARING. HE ASKED IF WE KNEW WHO HAD COMMITTED THE MURDERS. I
REPLIED IN THE NEGATIVE AND SAID IT WOULD BE USEFUL IF HE COULD HELP
US TO GET MORE INFORMATION. HE AGREED IMMEDIATELY TO RAISE THE
QUESTION WITH THE PEOPLE CARRYING OUT THE INVESTIGATION (I.E.
PALESTINIANS). I ADDED THAT WE WOULD EXPECT IN SUCH A CASE FOR THE
QRIMINALS TO BE TRIED AND PENALTY OF DEATH IMPOSED. HE SAID MOST
IMPORTANT THING IS TO FIND OUT WHY THEY DID IT AND WHO ORDERED THE
MEN TO DO IT. HE ADDED THAT HE THOUGHT PALESTINIANS CARRYING OUT
THE INVESTIGATION HAD NOT YET FOUND THE PEOPLE WHO ACTUALLY DID THE
KILLING.
3.  I EXPLAINED TO SALAM THE FRAME OF REFERENCE FOR MY PRESENCE
IN LEBANON AND STRESSED THAT I HAD NO ANSWER TO LEBANON'S
PROBLEMS. I WAS, HOWEVER, PREPARED TO BE HELPFUL IF THERE WAS
ANYTHING THE U.S. COULD USEFULLY DO. I INTENDED TO KEEP A RELATIVELY
LOW PROFILE. AS SOON AS POSSIBLE, I WANTED TO BE IN TOUCH WITH THE
CHRISTIANS ON THE OTHER SIDE. SALAM AGREED THAT I SHOULD DO SO
WHENEVER I COULD.
4.  I STRESSED THAT THE U.S. VIGOROUSLY OPPOSES PARTITION OF
LEBANON, DESPITE RUMORS TO CONTRARY CIRCULATING IN MOSLEM
QUARTERS. ALSO, U.S. DOES NOT CONDONE MILITARY INTERVENTION IN
LEBANON, DESPITE CONTRARY REPORTS. WHEN SALAM INDICATED THAT
THERE SEEMED TO BE SOME TRUTH TO POPULAR BELIEF OF EXISTENCE OF A
CONSPIRACY BETWEEN SYRIA, U.S., ISRAEL AND L
C EN CHRISTIANS,
I RESPONDED THAT THIS IS UNTRUE. FURTHERMORE, U.S. SUPPORTS NO FACTIO
N
IN LEBANON AND WANTS ONLY TO SEE PEACE AND STABILITY RESTORED TO
AN INDEPENDENT LEBANON IN FRAMEWORK OF UNITY AND COHESION.
5.  SALAM SAID HE WAS PREPARED TO ACCEPT FACT THAT U.S. DOES NOT
FAVOR PARTITION OF LEBANON BUT, FRANKLY, HE COULD NOT HELP BUT FEEL
THAT SYRIA WOULD NOT HAVE ACTED AS IT DID WITHOUT U.S. ENDORSEMENT
PLUS CLOSE COORDINATION WITH ISRAEL. THERE IS BOUND TO BE SUSPICION
OF U.S. MOTIVES AND ACTIONS IN VIEW OF LONG-ESTABLISHED AND STRONG
U.S. SUPPORT FOR ISRAEL. THIS IS WHY, HE CONTINUED, SOVIET
AMBASSADOR TODAY IN LEBANON IS FETED EVEN THOUGH LEBANESE DO NOT
LIKE COMMUNITOU HE ALLUDED TO "INCAPABILITY" OF USG TO INTRODUCE
TROOPS INTO LEBANON, AND SAID THIS IS GOOD THING. I AGREED USG WOULD
NOT MILITARILY INTERVENE IN LEBANON, BUT STATED THAT REASON FOR THIS
IS THAT SUCH A MOVE WOULD HURT U.S. INTERESTS ALL OVER ARAB WORLD.
6.  SALAM WAS HIGHLY CRITICAL OF THE SYRIANS. HE DEPLORED THEIR
BEHAVIOR IN LEBANON AND BLAMED THEM IN LARGE MEASURE FOR PRESENT
STATE OF AFFAIRS. HE SAID THE SYRIANS BEAR A GREAT DEAL OF
RESPONSIBILITY FOR THE EROSION OF SITUATION IN LEBANON BECAUSE THEY
HAD FIRST TRIED TO USE SAIQA AS THEIR INSTRUMENT IN LEBANON. THIS'
HAD ANTAGONIZED LEBANESE, PARTICULARLY SINCE SAIQA MISBEHAVED,
LOOTING ALMOST EVERYTHING IN SIGHT. SYRIANS HAD THOUGHT NAIVELY
THAT SOMEHOW SAIQA COULD PRESERVE SYRIA'S INTERESTS IN LEBANON,
BUT SAIQA WAS SOUNDLY DEFEATED. NOW THE SYRIANS HAD MADE EVERY
MOSLEM AN ENEMY AND THEY SHOULD LEAVE LEBANON. SALAM SAID U.S.
MUST BE HAPPY TO SEE THE ARABS IN DISARRAY BECAUSE THIS WEAKENS
THE ARABS. I RESPONDED THAT THIS IS ALSO UNTRUE AND, IF IT WOULD BE
HELPFUL, I WOULD BE SAYING AS MUCH TO THE PRESS. SALAM SAID THAT
ACTIONS SPEAK LOUDER THAN WORDS. AMONG OTHER THINGS, I OBSERVED,
ARAB DISARRAY IMPEDED ARAB-ISRAELI PEACE NEGOTIATIONS, TO WHICH
WE ATTACH THE GREATEST IMPORTANCE.
7.  SALAM NOTED THAT THE CONSPIRACY THEORY HAD BEEN PROPOUNDED
PUBLICLY BY RAYMOND EDDE FOR THE PAST YEAR AND A HALF. HE ACCUSED
US OF HAVING THEREFORE BEEN ANTI-EDDE IN THE PRESIDENTIAL ELECTION.
LAMBRAKIS, WHO WAS ALSO PRESENT, AND I DENIED U.S. HAD TAKEN ANY
POSITION IN THE PRESIDENTIAL ELECTION.  I SAID THAT WE HAD NO OBJECTI
ON
TO RAYMOND EDDE, EVENTHOUGH HE IS PRONE TO MAKE IRRESPONSIBLE
AND INACCURATE ALLEGATIONS. SALAM INSISTED THAT MOST LEBANESE
BELIEVED THAT U.S. AS WELL AS SYRIANS HAD BACKED SARKIS.  OTHERWISE,
EDDE WOULD HAVE BEEN ELECTED.  HE WAS UNABLE TO EXPLAIN HOW THIS
COULD BE THE CASE IF AT THE SAME TIME LEBANESE HAD LOSS OF
CONFIDENCE IN USG POLICY.
8.  IF EDDE HAD BECOME PRESIDENT, SALAM CONTINUED, HE WOULD HAVE
BEEN ABLE TO DRAW 90 PER CENT OF MARONITE SUPPORT AWAY FROM
TRADITIONAL EXTREMISTS SUCH AS GEMAYEL, CHAMOUN AND FRANGIE.
SARKIS, ON OTHER HAND, HAS NO POLITICAL FOLLOWING.  HE SAID EDDE
ACTUALLY POSSESSED A MAJORITY OF THE VOTES, AND PROBABLY WOULD HAVE
BEEN ELECTED PRESIDENT IN MARCH WHEN PARLIAMENT PRESENTED FRANGIE
WITH A PETITION FOR HIS RESIGNATWON SIGNED BY 66 DEPUTIES.  SALAM
PROFESSED TO KNOW FOR A FACT THAT FRANGIE WAS PREPARED TO RESIGN
THAT MORNING, BUT CHANGED HIS MIND AFTER HE GOT A TELEPHONE CALL
FROM PRESIDENT ASSAD IN DAMASCUS. THIS, HE STATED, WAS ANOTHER
INSTANCE OF SYRIAN RESPONSIBILITY FOR LEBANON'S PROBLEMS.  SALAM
WENT ON TO SAY THAT HE IS CONVINCED THAT SYRIA HAS DESIGNS ON THE
BEKAA.  HE ALLEGED THAT SYRIA IS NOW IN THE PROCESS OF INTEGRATING
THE SCHOOL SYSTEM THERE INTO THE SYRIAN SCHOOL SYSTEM.
9.  SALAM REITERATED HIS VIEW THAT SARKIS WAS ELECTED BY SYRIAN
BACKING.  BEISDES NOT HAVING POLITICAL SUPPORT AMONG THE MARONITES,
SARKIS HAS SURROUNDED HIMSELF WITH CHEHABISTS AND A GROUP OF
CORRUPT PEOPLE, MANY OF WHOM HAVE BEEN AROUND FRANGIE (SUCH AS
SHEIKH BUTROS KHOURY).  NEVERTHELESS, NOW THAT HE IS PRESIDENT,
CONTINUED SALAM, THERE IS NO CHOICE BUT TO LINE UP BEHIND SARKIS
AND TRY TO HELP HIM.
10.  SALAM SAID IT WAS A GREAT MISTAKE TO REFER TO CHRISTIAN
AND MOSLEM FACTIONS, RESPECTIVELY, AS "RIGHTISTS" AND "LEFTISTS."
MAJORITY OF MOSLEMS ARE NOT TO THE LEFT POLITICALLY.  LEBANESE DO
NOT LIKE OR WANT COMMUNISM.
11.  WHILE ACKNOWLEDGING EXISTENCE OF A PALESTINIAN PROBLEM IN
LEBANON, AS WELL AS CONFESSIONAL CONFLICT, SALAM REVERTED TO THEME
THAT NEFARIOUS OUTSIDE INFLUENCES, CHIEFLY THE SYRIANS, WERE PRIMARIL
Y
RESPONSIBLE FOR STIRRING THINGS UP. HE NOTED THAT THE PROPOSAL TO
HOLD A ROUNDTABLE CONFERENCE HAD BEEN ONE OF HIS EARLIEST IDEAS
WHEN SOME OONTHS AGO HE HAD ACTIVATED THE FORMATION OF THE DIALOGUE
COMMITTEE.  HOWEVER, DIALOGUE COMMITTEE, WHICH SHOULD HAVE BEEN
LIMITED TO FEW KEY INDIVIDUALS, HAD BEEN CONSTITUTED WITH TOO MANY
REPRESENTATIVES FROM JUMBLATT'S LEFTIST PARTIES, FOR EXAMPLE, AND
HAD NEVER GOTTEN GOING.  BY THE SAME TOKEN, HE WONDERED IF A
ROUNDTABLE CONFERENCE WERE POSSIBLE AT THIS TIME WHILE FIGHTING
CONTINUED.  A CEASEFIRE OUGHT TO BE THE FIRST STEP.
12.  SALAM NOTED THAT EGYPT HAS NOW ONCE AGAIN BECOME POPULAR IN
ARAB WORLD AT SYRIA'S EXPENSE. ARABS ARE NOW SAYING THAT AT LEAST
SADAT HAS BEEN DIRECT AND ABOVEBOARD IN AGREEMENTS HE NEGOTIATED
WITH ISRAEL RE SINAI. ASSAD, ON OTHER HAND, IS CONSIDERED
UNDERHANDED AND DEVIOUS. EGYPT HAS BENEFITED BY BECOMING
CH TWVON#OF PALESTINIANS.
13.  SAEB SALAM'S REMARKS ON TOPICS OF MORE CURRENT INTEREST
WERE REPORTED IN BEIRUT 5755.
14.  COMMENT: SAEB SALAM REMAINS AN INTERESTING AND CHARMING
PERSON TO TALK TO. THOUGH SEPTUAGENARIAN AND VOLUBLE, HE KEEPS UP
WITH THE TIMES REASONABLY WELL. MANY OF HIS INTERPRETATIONS OF
EVENTS FIT INTO A GENERAL PATTERN WHICH IS SHARED BY MARONITE LEADERS
SUCH AS RAYMOND EDDE AND RIVAL MOSLEM TRAIDITONALISTS SUCH AS
KARAME.  HE CONSIDERS JUMBLATT A CONSERVATIVE LIKE HIMSELF, THOUGH
ONE WHO IS PLAYING A DANGEROUS GAME WITH THE LEFT.  HE SEEMS TO HAVE
THE SAME FAITH KARAME EXPRESSED TO ME A FEW DAYS AGO THAT THE
LEBANESE CAN SETTLE THEIR DIFFERENCES REASONABLY WELL IF ONLY
OUTSIDERS--PARTICULARLY THE SYRIANS--WILL PERMIT THEM TO DO SO.
ALTHOUGH NOT ESPECIALLY IMPORTANT IN A TIME OF ARMED WARFARE, HE
REMAINS AN INFLUENTIAL POLITICIAN BEHIND THE SCENES AT LEAST UNTIL
SUCH TIME AS THE YOUNGER GENERATION PRODUCES POLITICIANS OF NOTE
RATHER THAN JUST FIGHTERS.
SEELYE
NOTE BY OC/T: AS RECEIVED.

 * 23624 1976BEIRUT05953 0.007068642 | 1976-07-07 | BEIRUT | STATE | LEBANESE SITUATION JULY 7: PALESTINIAN OFFENSIVE IN NORTH FALTERS;  ARAB LEAGUE MEDIATION EFFORT REVIVES
1. SUMMARY: PALESTINIAN DRIVE IN NORTH IS FALTERING AND
CHRISTIANS HOPE EXPAND EARLIER ESTABLISHED AREAS OF CONTROL
IN COUNTEROFFENSIVE. TELL ZAATAR MOP-UP CONTINUESUK FIGHTING
ELSEWHERE IN BEIRUT AND IN REST OF COUNTRY CONTINUES AT HIGH
LEVEL, BUT INDECISIVE. INTER-ARAB MEDIATION EFFORTS REVIVE,
WITH SECOND SOFAR MEETING SCHEDULED FOR JULY 7 TO INCLUDE MOST
MAJOR PARTIES TO CONFLICT. BEIRUT AIRPORT RUNWAYS APPEAR TO
BE ONLY SLIGHTLY DAMAGED AND COULD HANDLE LARGE AIRCRAFT.
MINIMAL CITY WATER SUPPLY IN BEIRUT NOW COMPLETELY STOPPED AS
FUEL SHORTAGE WORSENS. SMALL BRITISH-ORGANIZED CONVOY DEPARTS
FOR DAMASCUS. END SUMMARY.
2. NORTH LEBANON HOLDS SPOTLIGHT AS RIGHTIST FORCES APPEAR TO
HAVE RETAKEN CHEKKA AND JOINT CHRISTIAN/SYRIAN COUNTER-THRUST
GAINS PREDOMINANCE. RIGHTIST ALSO CLAIM TO HAVE TAKEN AMYOUN
AND SEVERAL SURROUNDING VILLAES IN THE KOURA. LEFTISTS SAY
THEY HAVE REPELLED ALL ATTACKS AND CONTINUE TO CONTROL EVEN
CHEKKA, BUT MORE RELIABLE INFORMATION CONTRADICTS THIS CLAIM.
OTHER NORTHERN AREAS ARE VERY ACTIVE WITH UNUSUALLY HEAVY
ARTILLERY BARRAGES AT ZGHORTA NAD HALBA. WE UNDERSTAND
COMBINED RIGHTIST/SYRIAN FORCES MAY NOT INTEND TO STOP WITH
PRESENT SUCCESSES, BUT MAY CONTINUE MOVE NORTHWARD TOWARD
TRIPOLI.
3. TELL ZAATAR CONTINUES RECEIVE WIDE PRESS COVERAGE, ALTHOUGH
ACCORDING TO OUR INFORMATION, BATTLE IS LARGELY OVER. ARTILLERY
BARRAGES NEVERTHELESS CONTINUE IN VICINITY AT NABAA, DEKOUANEH,
AND SIN EL-FIL AND LARGE FIRES, APPARENTLY WOODS, BURN AT SABTYE,
DEKOUANE, MANSOURIEH, AND MKALLES. PRESS COMMENTS ON
INACCESSIBLE BATTLE FIELDS AND CONTRADICTORY COMMUNIQUES FROM
VARIOUS GROUPS REVEAL LACK OF GOOD FIRST-HAND KNOWLEDGE.
PALESTINIAN ACCUSATIONS THAT SYRIANS HELPED CHRISTIANS AT TELL
ZAATAR CONTINUE, AND WE UNDERSTAND SYRIANS POSSIBLY DID AT LEAST
ASSIST RIGHTIST FORCES'S PLANNING. HEAVY MUTUAL BOMBARDMENTS AT CHIYA
H/
AIN EL-RUMMANEH AND SOME GROUND ACTION CONTINUE. ARTILLERY
DUELS CONTINUE AS WELL IN HADETH/LAYLAKE AREA. BEIRUT CENTRAL
CITY AREA IS ACTIVE, INCLUDING SORTIES WITH HAND GRENADES AND
SMALL WEAPONS. SPORADIC BOMBARDMENTS OF RESIDENTIAL AREAS IN EAST
AND WEST SECTORS OF CAPITAL CONTINUE (INCLUDING RAS BEIRUT)
4. ELSEWHERE IN COUNTRY, MILITARY SITUATION REMAINS RELATIVELY
STABLE. HEAVY SYRIAN ARTILLERY BARRAGES JULY 6 HIT SIDON,
NEARBY VILLAGE OF ANKOUN AND PALESTINIAN CAMPS OF MYE MYE
AND AIN EL-HELOUE, AS WELL AS ZAHRANI REFINERY (SEE BELOW).
THIS WAS PERHAPS IN RETALIATION FOR PALESTINIAN AMBUSHES ON
SIDON/JEZZINE ROAD. BEKAA REMAINS STABLE ALTHOUGH TENSIONS
ARE HIGH AND AINTOURA/MTEIN AXIS MAY BE HEATING UP. SOME
SYRIAN SHELLING OF VILLAGES REPORTED FROM HERMEL AREA.
PALESTINIAN COMMAND IN SOUTH CLAIMS ISRAELI AIRCRAFT FLEW
OVER BORDER AREA AND IDF ARTILLERY FIRED AT VILLAGES OF
AITAROUN AND BLIDA.
5. MARATHON JULY 6 MEETING OF ARAFAT, JUNBLATT, AND LIBYAN
PREMIER JALLOUD APPEARS TO HAVE BEEN A TENSE ROUND ROBIN ON
MANY ISSUES. DESPITE MILITARY DETERIORATION IN THE NORTH,
SECOND MAJOR DIALOGUE SESSION EXPECTED AT SOFAR JULY 7.
JUNBLATT REFUSING TO ATTEND THIS SOFAR MEETING PERHAPS DUE
FEELING PALESTINIANS ARE STEALING SHOW. ARAFAT, JALLOUD, AL
SECGEN MAHMOUD RIAD, REPRESENTATIVES FO SYRIA AND THE MARONITE
"KFOUR FRONT" ALL SAY THE WILL ATTEND. GENERAL NAJI JAMIL WILL
REPRESENT SYRIAN AND KARIM PAKRADOUNI AND MICHEL SAMAHA THE
"KFOUR FRONT." MEETING TOPIC OFFICIALLY ANNOUNCED AS MILITARY
DEVELOPMENTS AT TELL ZAATAR, BUT PRESS SPECULATES DELEGATES
WILL DEAL MAINLY WITH SYRIAN/PALESTINIAN DIFFERENCES AND
ESTABLISHMENT OF AL-SPONSORED CEASEFIRE. CONFLICTING DEMANDS
MAKE ANY IMMEDIATE AGREEMENTS UNLIKELY. LEBANESE LEFTISTS
SAY THEY WILL CONTINUE FIGHT UNTIL SYRIANS WITHDRAW ENTIRELY
FROM LEBANON. RIGHTISTS CONTINUE INSIST ON CIARO ACCORDS AAD
RETURN OF PALESTINIANS TO CAMPS.
6. EMBRYONIC MOSLEM DISSATISFACTION WITH PALESTINIAN
DOMINANCE IN WEST BEIRUT IS PLAYED ON BY PIERRE GEMAYEL IN
JULY 6 CALL TO POLITICAL LEADERS OF WEST BEIRUT TO CLOSE RANSK
WITHOUT DELAY "TO LIBERATE THE LEBANESE FROM THE PALESTINIAN
PROGRESSIVE YOKE." HE SAID THAT KATAEB PARTY WILL CONTINUE
FIGHT UNTIL ALL LEBANESE REGIONS ARE LIBERATED. SYRIA,
ACTIVE MILITARILY, AVOIDS GETTING INVOLVED IN "BATTLE OF THE
AIR WAVES."
7. WE UNDERSTAND CHAMOUN ATTEMPTING FORCE ISSUE OF HIS
CONTESTED APPOINTMENT AS FOREIGN MINISTER (BY FRANGIE, WITHOUT
AGREEMENT OF PRIME MINISTER KARAME) BY SENDING INSTRUCTIONS TO
ALL LEBANESE AMBASSADORS TO APPROACH HOST GOVERNMENT TO EXPLAIN
LEBANESE SITUATION AND INSTRUCTION TO LEBANESE UN MISSION TO
SUPPORT SUDAN IN SUDAN-LIBYA QUARREL.
8. ICRC DC-6 CARRIED SIX TONS OF MEDICINES INTO BEIRUT
AIRPORT JULY 6, AND ANOTHER FLIGHT EXPECTED JULY 7. MINISTER OF
ECONOMY AND TRANSPORTATION ADEL OSSEIRAN SAYS REOPENING OF
AIRPORT NOT EVEN CONSIDERED FOR PRESENT DUE "ILLOGICAL CONDITIONS
IMPOSED BY THE KATAEB WAR COUNCIL." ICRC FLIGHT WAS FIRST SINCE
JUNE 27 WHEN MEA PLANE HIT ON RUNWAY BY CHRISTIAN ARTILLERY.
RELIABLE MEA SOURCE SAID JULY 6 RUNWAY SURFACES HAVE EIGHT
SMALL RUPTURES, BUT THAT BOEING 707 TYPE AIRCRAFT COULD LAND
AND TAKE OFF. CLOSURE CAUSING GREAT DIFFIKLTY ESPECIALLY IN
VIEW NEED TO IMPORT FOOD SUPPLIES AND INABILITY WESTERN ZONE
LEBANESE TO EASILY ENTER AND LEAVE COUNTRY.
9. BEIRUT WATER BUREAU SAYS IT CAN NO LONGER DELIVER EVEN SMALL
AMOUNTS OF WATER TO VARIOUS BEIRUT SECTORS, AS LACK OF FUEL HAS
CUT OFF ELECTRICITY TO DBAYE PUMPING STATION, WHICH DURING PAST
TWO WEEKS HAS BEEN SOLE REMAINING CITY WATER SOURCE, PUMPING
SMALL AMOUNTS TO VARIOUS CITY SECTORS ON RATOATION BASIS.
BEIRUTIS MUST NOW RELY ON INSUFFICIENT AND OFTEN BRACKISH WELLS.
SITUATION MAY HAVE TAKEN ADDITIONAL CRITICAL TURN WITH NEWS
THAT ZAHRANI REFINERY NEAR SIDON WAS BOMBARDED BY SYRIANS
JULY 6 AND IS NOW REPORED BURNING. FUEL FOR ZOUK ELECTRIC
STATION NORTH OF BEIRUT HAS BEEN ORDERED FROM RUMANIA, BUT
DELIVERY NOT SCHEDULED FOR SOME TEN DAYS.
10. BRITISH EMBASSY SPONSORED COMPARATIVELY SMALL CONVOY OF 25
VEHICLES TO DAMASCUS JULY 7. CONVOY CARRED 10 AMCITS, INCLUDING
ONE EMBASSY MEMBER.
SEELYE

FOLLOWING IS TEXT OF TELEGRAM TO SECURITY COUNCIL PRESIDENT
FROM OAU CHAIRMAN RAMGOOLAM, PUBLISHED AS SECURITY COUNCIL
DOCUMENT:
QUOTE TELEGRAM FROM THE PRIME MINISTER OF MAURITIUS, CURRENT
CHAIRMAN OF THE ORGANIZATION OF AFRICAN UNITY, ADDRESSED TO
THE PRESIDENT OF THE SECURITY COUNCIL
ASSEMBLY OAU HEADS OF STATE AND GOVERNMENT MEETING IN ITS
13TH ASSEMBLY ORDINARY SESSION IN MAURITIUS ON 4 JULY 1976.
RECEIVED INFORMATION FROM PRESIDENT OF UGANDA FIELD MARSHAL
ALHEYI DR. IDI AMIN DADA THROUGH HIS FOREIGN MINISTER
CONCERNING THE INVASION OF UGANDA BY ISRAELI COMMANDOS AT
1 A.M. ON 4 JULY 1976. OVER 100 MEMBERS OF UGANDAN ARMY
WERE REPORTEDLY KILLED TOGETHER WITH A TOTAL LOSS OF SEVEN
MIG 21S AND FOUR MIG 17S AND A NUMBER OF CIVILIAN AIRCRAFT
AND COMPLETE DESTRUCTION OF OLD ENTEBBE AIRPORT. THIS
UNPRECEDENTED AGGRESSION AGAINST UGANDA BY ISRAEL CONSTITUTES
A DANGER NOT ONLY TO UGANDA AND AFRICA BUT TO INTERNATIONAL
PEACE AND SECURITY. OAU HEADS OF STATE AND GOVERNMENT
REQUEST YOU TO SUMMON IMMEDIATELY THE SECURITY COUNCIL TO
CONSIDER THIS WANTON ACT OF AGGRESSION AGAINST A MEMBER
STATE OF THE UNITED NATIONS. I REQUEST YOU TO PUBLISH
THE TEXT OF THE TELEGRAM AS AN OFFICIAL DOCUMENT OF THE
SECURITY COUNCIL.
SIGNED ON BEHALF OF OAU ASSEMBLY OF HEADS OF STATE AND
GOVERNMENT
SIR SEEWOOSAGUR RAMGOOLAM
PRIME MINISTER OF MAURITIUS
CURRENT CHAIRMAN OF THE ORGANIZATION OF AFRICAN UNITY UNQUOTE

 * 33753 1976BONN11368 0.007066171 | 1976-07-06 | BONN | STATE | FONMIN ALLON'S VISIT TO FRG, JUNE 23-25
1.  EMBOFF DISCUSSED ALLON VISIT WITH ECONMIN OFFICIAL.
ON THE SUBJECT OF INCREASING FRG OFFICIAL AID TO ISRAEL,
HE STATED THAT THE QUESTION OF AN INCREASE IN
TRADITIONAL FRG AID LEVELS COULD BE DISCUSSED WITH THE
ISRAELIS AT ANY TIME.  HE EMPHASIZED, HOWEVER, THAT HE
WAS NOT AWARE OF ANY FRG PROMISES TO BE FORTHCOMING
IN AID DISCUSSIONS AFTER OCTOBER 3.
2.  ECONMIN OFFICIAL CLAIMED THERE WERE IMPORTANT
REASONS WHY THE FRG COULD NOT SIGNIFICANTLY INCREASE
OFFICIAL AID TO ISRAEL IN THE NEAR FUTURE.
(A) THE FRG AID MINISTRY BUDGET IS VERY TIGHT
AT THE MOMENT.  THE FRG IS ATTEMPTING TO HOLD DOWN
GOVERNMENT EXPENDITURES AND A SIGNIFICANT INCREASE
IN THE AID BUDGET IS NOT LIKELY IN THE NEAR TERM.
(B)  THE FRG ATTEMPTS TO BALANCE AID TO ISRAEL
WITH AID TO ARAB COUNTRIES.  THUS A SIGNIFICANT
INCREASE FOR ISRAEL WOULD ENTAIL INCREASES FOR THE
ARAB NATIONS AS WELL.
(C)  THE FRG ALSO ATTEMPTS TO BALANCE ITS AID
WORLDWIDE.  ISRAEL ALREADY RECEIVES A VERY HIGH
AMOUNT OF PER CAPITA AID AS COMPARED TO INDIA FOR EXAMPLE.
A SIGNIFICANT INCREASE FOR ISRAEL WOULD PORTEND
INCREASES IN WORLDWIDE FRG AID WHICH DOES NOT SEEM
POSSIBLE AT THIS TIME.
3.  THE FRG AND ISRAEL SIGNED THE TRADITIONAL DM 140
MILLION ECONOMIC AID AGREEMENT FOR 1976 ON JULY 1.  THE
FOREIGN MINISTRY ANNOUNCED THAT THIS AID IS INTENDED
FOR HOUSING CONSTRUCTION, TELEPHONE PROJECTS, AND
THE DEVELOPMENT BANK IN ISRAEL.
4.  ECONMIN OFFICIAL MAINTAINED THAT INCREASED DIRECT
PRIVATE FRG INVESTMENT IN ISRAEL AND INCREASED
ISRAELI EXPORTS TO THE FRG WOULD PROVIDE MORE BILATERAL
ASSISTANCE TO ISRAEL'S BATTERED ECONOMY THAN ANY
POSSIBLE INCREASE IN OFFICIAL FRG AID.  THE INVESTMENT
PROMOTION AGREEMENT SIGNED DURING ALLON'S VISIT WOULD
HELP IMPROVE THE INVESTMENT CLIMATE, BUT ISRAEL'S
DEVALUATION POLICIES ARE THE KEY TO INVESTOR
RELUCTANCE.  ONCE THE CYCLE OF DEVALUATION IS HALTED,
ISRAEL COULD EXPECT GERMAN INVESTORS TO RESPOND.  THE
FRG ALSO WOULD DO ALL IT COULD TO AID ISRAEL'S EXPORTS
WHICH WERE PRIMARILY HINDERED BY A LACK OF ISRAELI
EXPORT ORIENTATION.  THE CONTACTS MADE BY ALLON'S PARTY
WITH VARIOUS TRADE PROMOTION GROUPS IN THE FRG AND THE
VARIOUS BILATERAL MECHANISMS NOW ESTABLISHED (SUCH AS
THE ECONOMIC COMMISSION) WOULD HELP STIMULATE ISRAELI
EXPORTS TO THE FRG.
HILLENBRAND



*******************

** 63751 1976DAMASC04328 0.007063835 | 1976-07-06 | DAMASCUS | STATE | SYRIA CONDEMNS ISRAELI OPERATION TO FREE AIR FRANCE CAPTIVES
1. JULY 6 MEDIA REPORTED CABLE FROM PRES. ASAD TO PRES.
AMIN OF UGANDA COMDEMNING "SAVAGE ACT OF AGRESSION
COMMITTED BY ISRAEL "AGAINST UGANDA. ASAD CLAIMED THAT
OPERATION PROVED ISRAELI DISREGARD FOR INTERNATIONAL LAW
AND FOR LIVES OF INNOCENT PASSENGERS.
2. SYRIAN PRESS HEADLINED INCIDENT: "WORLD DENOUNCES
TREACHEROUS ZIONIST RAID OF ENTEBBE AIRPORT. AFRICAN
SUMMIT CONFERENCE ASKS SECURITY COUNCIL FOR IMMEDIATE
MEETING. WALDHEIM DESCRIBES RAID AS FLAGRANT AGRESSION."
ONE PRESS COLUMNIST TERMED ACTION A "CHALLENGE TO AFRICA."
ANOTHER DENOUNCED PRES. FORD'S CABLE OF SUPPORT TO ISRAEL.
THIRD URGED THAT RAID BE AN INCENTIVE FOR ARABS TO
INCREASE THEIR SOLIDARITY.
3. COMMENT: IT NOT SURPRISING THAT SARG, WHICH
STRONGLY CONDEMNED ORIGINAL HIJACKING (REFTEL), WOULD
SHOW EQUAL FERVOR IN DENOUNCING ISRAELI RESCUE OPERATION.
IDI AMIN SPENT THREE-DAY VISIT IN DAMASCUS LAST MONTH AND
HAS SINCE PRAISED ASAD'S HANDLING OF LEBANESE CRISIS,
DEFENDING HIM AGAINST CHARGES OF PERSECUTING PALESTINIAN
RESISTANCE. UGANDAN ALSO PAID WIDELY PUBLICIZED VISIT TO
DAMASCUS JEWISH QUARTER, FACT WHICH LOCAL VOICE OF PALESTINE
COMMENTATOR RECALLED IN DAMASCUS BROADCAST, AFTER ENTEBBE
RAID. HE ASSERTED THAT UGANDAN LEADER NOT ANTI-JEWISH AND
HAD BEEN NEGOTIATING HONORABLY FOR RLEASE OF HOSTAGES UNTIL
ISRAELI RAID PREEMPTED HIS EFFORTS.

 * 89637 1976JERUSA00874 0.007061616 | 1976-07-06 | JERUSALEM | STATE | NABLUS YOUTH KILLED DURING DEMONSTRATIONS
1. SUMMARY: AN 18-YEAR-OLD YOUTH WAS KILLED BY ISRAELI
SECURITY FORCES DURING CLASHES IN NABLUS JULY 2 ARISING OUT
OF PROTESTS AGAINST IMPOSITION OF EQUIVALENT OF VALUE
ADDED TAX (VAT) AND AGAINST SYRIAN ACTION IN LEBANON. CURFEW
IMPOSED FOLLOWING VIOLENCE WAS LIFTED AFTERNOON JULY 3.
STRIKES THAT BEGAN JULY 1 CONTINUED FOR TWO OR THREE DAYS
IN MOST WEST BANK TOWNS. END SUMMARY.
2.PROTESTS AGAINST EQUIVALENT OF VAT TO BE IMPOSED IN
WEST BANK AUGUST 1 DEVELOPED INTO ANTI-SYRIAN, PRO-PLO DEMON-
STRATIONS IN NABLUS JULY 2 IN WHICH ROCKS AND BOTTLES
WERE THROWN BY YOUTHFUL DEMONSTRATORS AT ISRAELI SECURITY
FORCES. SHOTS FIRED BY SECURITY FORCES RESULTED IN
DEATH OF 18-YEAR-OLD HASHEM SHANTIR. PRESS REPORTS 15
TO 20 OTHERS INJURED DURING VIOLENCE WHICH JERUSALEM POST
REPORTS INCLUDED ATTACK ON TAX OFFICE. CURFEW WAS IMPOSED
IN MOST PARTS OF NABLUS BUT LIFTED ABOUT 4:00 P.M. FOL-
LOWING DAY, AFTER SHANTIR'S FUNERAL. MAYOR BASSAM SHAK'A HAS
VIGOROUSLY DENIED RADIO REPORTS THAT VIOLENCE INCLUDED
MUSLIM-CHRISTIAN CLASHES.
3. MANY OTHER WEST BANK TOWNS WITNESSED CONTINUATION ON
JULY 2 AND 3 OF COMMERCIAL STRIKE BEGUN ON JULY 1. MOST
SHOPS IN EAST JERUSALEM REMAINED CLOSED JULY 2 BUT RE-
OPENED IN LARGE PART JULY 3, AT LEAST IN PART AS RESULT OF
POLICE PRESSURE. POLICE WERE SEEN JULY 3 MAKING NOTE OF
THOSE ESTABLISHMENTS STILL CLOSED IN EAST JERUSALEM BUSINESS
DISTRICT, BUT THERE APPEARED TO BE NO PHYSICALLY-FORCED
OPENINGS.

 * 66315 1976DOHA00745 0.007060966 | 1976-07-07 | DOHA | STATE | SPECIAL CONTRIBUTIONS TO UNRWA
1. DURING COURSE OF JULY 6 MEETING WITH AMIR'S OFFICE DIRECTOR,
ISSA KAWARI, CHARGE TOOK OPPORTUNITY TO DISCUSS WITH HIM
PRESENT UNRWA FINANCIAL CRISIS AND REQUEST FOR SPECIAL UNRWA
CONTRIBUTION FROM GOQAM KAWARI SAID THAT GOQ HAD RECEIVED
CABLE FROM UNRWA REQUESTING ADDITIONAL FUNDS AND THAT MATTER
WOULD BE TAKEN UP DURING JULY 7 MEETING OF COUNCIL OF MINISTERS.
KAWARI ALSO SAID THAT QATAR WAS AWARE OF SAUDI SPECIAL CONTRIBUTION
OF TEN MILLION DOLLARS. CHARGE TOLD KAWARI THAT HE WAS PLEASED
TO HEAR THAT THIS UNRWA REQUEST WAS BEING CONSIDERED AND THEN
ASKED KAWARI IF HE HAD ANY IDEA OF AMOUNT THAT WOULD BE FORTH-
COMING. KAWARI SAID THAT HE DID NOT, BUT THAT HE WAS CERTAIN
THAT GOQ WOULD COME THROUGH WITH SPECIAL CONTRIBUTION. KAWARI
ENDED MEETING WITH PROMISE TO LET CHARGE KNOW AMOUNT OF CON-
TRIBUTION AS SOON AS MATTER ACTED ON BY COUNCIL OF MINISTERS AND
AMIR DECIDES ON AMOUNT OF CONTRIBUTION.
2. AFTER MEETING WITH KAWARI, CHARGE HAD OCCASION TO MEET
SEPARATELY WITH ANOTHER GOQ OFFICIAL WITH SOME RESPONSIBILITY
FOR UN AFFAIRS. HE ALSO CONFIRMED THAT UNRWA SPECIAL CONTRIBUTION
WILL BE ON AGENDA OF JULY 7 MEETING OF GOQ COUNCIL OF MINISTERS.
ALTHOUGH HE CLAIMED NOT TO KNOW AMOUNT OF CONTRIBUTION UNDER
CONSIDERATION, HE HINTED THAT AMOUNT MIGHT BE RELATIVELY GENEROUS.
HE SAID THAT SAUDI CONTRIBUTION OF TEN MILLION WAS INTENDED TO
PREVENT UNRWA FROM ENDING ITS ROLE IN WEST BANK AREA AND TO
PRECLUDE A TAKEOVER OF THESE UNRWA ACTIVITIES BY THE ISRAELIS;
THEREFORE, QATAR SHOULD FOLLOW THIS LINE.
3. ON MORNING JULY 7, CHARGE HAD OCCASION TO BRING UP AGAIN
UNRWA FINANCIAL CRISIS AND GOQ CONTRIBUTION WITH FONMIN OFFICIAL
IN CHARGE OF INTERNATIONAL AFFAIRS. UNFORTUNATELY, THIS
PERSON WAS NOT VERY CURRENT ON SUBJECT AND HAD VERY LITTLE TO
OFFER. HE DID ADD, HOWEVER, THAT HE THOUGH QATAR WOULD EVENTUALLY
APPROVE AROUND ONE AND HALF TO TWO MILLION DOLLAR CONTRIBUTION.
4. WE WILL REPORT RESULTS OF COUNCIL OF MINISTERS MEETING IN
SEPTEL AND AS SOON AS KNOWN.
YOUNG

ISRAEL AND POSSIBLY KENYA REGARDING ISRAELI RESCUE OPERATION
2. IT IS APPARENT, HOWEVER, THAT GOU AIDED TERRORISTS AFTER
THEIR LANDING AND IN EFFECT BECAME PARTY TO PRESSURE ON GOI
AND OTHER GOVERNMENTS TO ACCEDE TO TERRORISTS DEMANDS.
3. IN THIS SITUATION ANY SC ACTION CONDEMNING ISRAEL AND
KENYA BECOMES EFFORT TO EXONERATE TERRORISTS AND GOU. IF
SC MEETING IS CALLED WE ARE CONSIDERING TAKING INITIATIVE
WITH DRAFT RESOLUTION WHICH AFTER APPROPRIATE PREAMBULARS
CONCLUDES WITH OPERATIVE PARAGRAPH ALONG FOLLOWING LINE
"EVERY GOVERNMENT, REGARDLESS OF ITS POLITICAL VIEWS,HAS AN
OBLIGATION TO PUT AN END TO ACTS OF TERRORISM".
4. IT WOULD BE OUR INTENTION TO SEEK EARLY SUPPORT FOR
THIS COURSE OF ACTION WHICH IS DIRECTED AGAINST ALL STATES
INCLUDING UGANDA, WHICH DO NOT ACT VIGOROUSLY TO PUT AN
END TO TERRORISTS ACTS OR THREATS WHEN THEY ARE ABLE TO DO
SO. WE WILL BE DRAFTING APPROPRIATE RESOLUTION.
5. AT SAME TIME WE WOULD PLAN TO MAKE KNOWN IMMEDIATELY
OUR UNEQUIVOCAL OPPOSITION TO ANY UNBALANCED RESOLUTION,
ESPECIALLY ONE WHICH CONDEMNS ISRAEL AND/OR KENYA. IF
WE DO SO QUICKLY, BEFORE ANY TEXT IS TABLED, WE MIGHT BE
ABE TO RETAIN INITIATIVE.
6. LONDON AND PARIS SHOULD CONTACT FONMIN ASAP JULY 5 TO
SET FORTH OUR STRONG VIEWS AND SEEK THEIR SUPPORT FOR
PROCEDURE DESCRIBED PARA 5, EVEN TO EXTENT OF THREATENING
VETO.
7. ALL ACTION ADDRESSEES SHOULD STRONGLY URGE HOST GOVERNMENT
TO JOIN US IN MOVING RAPIDLY ON
RESOLUTION SUGGESTED PARA 4 IN EVENT SC CALLED INTO
SESSION. REPLIES SHOULD BE REPEATED USUN.
8. FOR GEORGETOWN, CONTONOU, PEKING, MOSCOW, TRIPOLI,
DAR ES SALAAM: WE SEE LITTLE POINT IN APPROACHING HOST
GOVERNMENTS AT THIS POINT BUT WOULD WELCOME YOUR COMMENTS
IMMEDIATE. ROBINSON UNQUOTE ROBINSON



*******************
